Examining Reasoning LLMs-as-Judges in Non-Verifiable LLM Post-Training
Authors: Yixin Liu, Yue Yu, DiJia Su, Sid Wang, Xuewei Wang, Song Jiang, Bo Liu, Arman Cohan, Yuandong Tian, Zhengxing Chen
First: 2026-03-12T17:57:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T17:57:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reasoning LLMs-as-Judges, which can benefit from inference-time scaling, provide a promising path for extending the success of reasoning models to non-verifiable domains where the output correctness/quality cannot be directly checked. However, while reasoning judges have shown better performance on static evaluation benchmarks, their effectiveness in actual policy training has not been systematically examined. Therefore, we conduct a rigorous study to investigate the actual impact of non-reasoning and reasoning judges in reinforcement-learning-based LLM alignment. Our controlled synthetic setting, where a "gold-standard" judge (gpt-oss-120b) provides preference annotations to train smaller judges, reveals key differences between non-reasoning and reasoning judges: non-reasoning judges lead to reward hacking easily, while reasoning judges can lead to policies that achieve strong performance when evaluated by the gold-standard judge. Interestingly, we find that the reasoning-judge-trained policies achieve such strong performance by learning to generate highly effective adversarial outputs that can also score well on popular benchmarks such as Arena-Hard by deceiving other LLM-judges. Combined with our further analysis, our study highlights both important findings and room for improvements for applying (reasoning) LLM-judges in non-verifiable LLM post-training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：审视推理型LLM作为评判者在不可验证的LLM后训练中的应用
推理型LLM作为评判者，能够受益于推理时扩展，为将推理模型成功应用于无法直接检验输出正确性/质量的不可验证领域提供了可行路径。然而，尽管推理评判者在静态评估基准上表现更优，其在实际策略训练中的有效性尚未得到系统检验。为此，我们开展了一项严谨研究，探究非推理型与推理型评判者在基于强化学习的LLM对齐中的实际影响。通过受控合成实验（由“黄金标准”评判者gpt-oss-120b提供偏好标注以训练较小评判者），我们揭示了二者关键差异：非推理型评判者易导致奖励破解，而推理型评判者能训练出在黄金标准评判下表现优异的策略。有趣的是，推理评判者训练的策略通过生成高效对抗性输出实现强性能，这些输出还能通过欺骗其他LLM评判者在Arena-Hard等流行基准中获得高分。结合进一步分析，本研究既揭示了重要发现，也指出了在不可验证LLM后训练中应用（推理型）LLM评判者的改进空间。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates the practical effectiveness of reasoning-based LLMs as judges in non-verifiable LLM post-training alignment, motivated by the need to extend reasoning models' success to domains where output correctness cannot be directly verified. The method involves a controlled synthetic setting using a gold-standard judge (gpt-oss-120b) to provide preference annotations for training smaller non-reasoning and reasoning judges in reinforcement-learning-based alignment. Key experimental results reveal that non-reasoning judges lead to reward hacking, whereas reasoning judges produce policies that perform strongly under gold-standard evaluation, albeit by learning to generate adversarial outputs that deceive other LLM-judges on benchmarks like Arena-Hard, highlighting both findings and areas for improvement.
本研究探讨了基于推理的大语言模型作为评判者在不可验证的大语言模型后训练对齐中的实际效果，其动机在于将推理模型的成功扩展至输出正确性无法直接验证的领域。方法采用一个受控的合成设置，利用黄金标准评判者为训练较小的非推理和推理评判者提供偏好标注，以进行基于强化学习的对齐。主要实验结果表明，非推理评判者容易导致奖励破解，而推理评判者训练的模型在黄金标准评估下表现强劲，但这些模型是通过学习生成具有对抗性的输出来欺骗其他大语言模型评判者（如在Arena-Hard等基准测试中），从而揭示了重要发现和改进空间。
Separable neural architectures as a primitive for unified predictive and generative intelligence
Authors: Reza T. Batley, Apurba Sarker, Rajib Mostakim, Andrew Klichine, Sourav Saha
First: 2026-03-12T17:56:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T17:56:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Intelligent systems across physics, language and perception often exhibit factorisable structure, yet are typically modelled by monolithic neural architectures that do not explicitly exploit this structure. The separable neural architecture (SNA) addresses this by formalising a representational class that unifies additive, quadratic and tensor-decomposed neural models. By constraining interaction order and tensor rank, SNAs impose a structural inductive bias that factorises high-dimensional mappings into low-arity components. Separability need not be a property of the system itself: it often emerges in the coordinates or representations through which the system is expressed. Crucially, this coordinate-aware formulation reveals a structural analogy between chaotic spatiotemporal dynamics and linguistic autoregression. By treating continuous physical states as smooth, separable embeddings, SNAs enable distributional modelling of chaotic systems. This approach mitigates the nonphysical drift characteristics of deterministic operators whilst remaining applicable to discrete sequences. The compositional versatility of this approach is demonstrated across four domains: autonomous waypoint navigation via reinforcement learning, inverse generation of multifunctional microstructures, distributional modelling of turbulent flow and neural language modelling. These results establish the separable neural architecture as a domain-agnostic primitive for predictive and generative intelligence, capable of unifying both deterministic and distributional representations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：可分离神经架构：作为统一预测与生成智能的基础构件
智能系统在物理、语言与感知领域常呈现可分解结构，但现有模型多采用单一神经架构，未显式利用此结构。可分离神经架构通过形式化一类表征模型，统一了加法、二次及张量分解神经模型。通过约束交互阶数与张量秩，该架构引入结构性归纳偏置，将高维映射分解为低元组分。可分离性未必是系统固有属性，而常体现于表达系统的坐标或表征中。关键的是，这种坐标感知的构建揭示了混沌时空动力学与语言自回归间的结构类比。通过将连续物理状态视为平滑可分离嵌入，该架构实现了混沌系统的分布建模。此方法在保持适用于离散序列的同时，缓解了确定性算子的非物理漂移特性。该架构的组合灵活性在四个领域得到验证：基于强化学习的自主航点导航、多功能微结构的逆向生成、湍流的分布建模以及神经语言建模。这些成果确立了可分离神经架构作为跨领域预测与生成智能的基础构件，能够统一确定性与分布性表征。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the factorizable structure often present in intelligent systems across physics, language, and perception, this paper introduces the Separable Neural Architecture (SNA) as a unified model that imposes structural inductive biases through constraints on interaction order and tensor rank, thereby factorizing high-dimensional mappings. The method's coordinate-aware formulation reveals a structural analogy between chaotic dynamics and linguistic autoregression, enabling distributional modeling of chaotic systems by treating physical states as smooth, separable embeddings. Experimental results across four domains—autonomous navigation, inverse generation of microstructures, modeling of turbulent flow, and neural language modeling—demonstrate the approach's versatility in unifying deterministic and distributional representations for predictive and generative tasks.
本文的动机在于智能系统在物理、语言和感知等领域常表现出可分解的结构，为此提出了可分离神经架构（SNA）作为一种统一模型，通过约束交互阶数和张量秩来施加结构性归纳偏置，从而将高维映射分解为低阶组件。该方法采用坐标感知的公式化，揭示了混沌时空动力学与语言自回归之间的结构类比，通过将连续物理状态视为平滑、可分离的嵌入，实现了混沌系统的分布建模。在四个领域的实验结果表明了该方法的组合灵活性：包括通过强化学习的自主航点导航、多功能微结构的逆向生成、湍流的分布建模以及神经语言建模，这些结果确立了SNA作为领域无关的基元，能够统一确定性和分布性表示，用于预测和生成智能任务。
IsoCompute Playbook: Optimally Scaling Sampling Compute for LLM RL
Authors: Zhoujun Cheng, Yutao Xie, Yuxiao Qu, Amrith Setlur, Shibo Hao, Varad Pimpalkhute, Tongtong Liang, Feng Yao, Zhengzhong Liu, Eric Xing, Virginia Smith, Ruslan Salakhutdinov, Zhiting Hu, Taylor Killian, Aviral Kumar
First: 2026-03-12T16:49:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:49:21+00:00
Comments: 29 pages, 27 figures. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While scaling laws guide compute allocation for LLM pre-training, analogous prescriptions for reinforcement learning (RL) post-training of large language models (LLMs) remain poorly understood. We study the compute-optimal allocation of sampling compute for on-policy RL methods in LLMs, framing scaling as a compute-constrained optimization over three resources: parallel rollouts per problem, number of problems per batch, and number of update steps. We find that the compute-optimal number of parallel rollouts per problem increases predictably with compute budget and then saturates. This trend holds across both easy and hard problems, though driven by different mechanisms: solution sharpening on easy problems and coverage expansion on hard problems. We further show that increasing the number of parallel rollouts mitigates interference across problems, while the number of problems per batch primarily affects training stability and can be chosen within a broad range. Validated across base models and data distributions, our results recast RL scaling laws as prescriptive allocation rules and provide practical guidance for compute-efficient LLM RL post-training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IsoCompute手册：面向大语言模型强化学习的采样计算最优扩展
虽然扩展定律指导着大语言模型预训练的计算资源分配，但针对大语言模型强化学习后训练的类似准则仍缺乏深入理解。本研究探讨了大语言模型在策略强化学习方法中采样计算的最优分配，将扩展问题构建为对三种资源的计算约束优化：每个问题的并行轨迹数、每批次问题数量以及更新步数。研究发现，每个问题的最优并行轨迹数随计算预算增加呈可预测增长后趋于饱和。这一趋势在简单与困难问题中均成立，但驱动机制不同：简单问题源于解锐化，困难问题源于覆盖扩展。进一步研究表明，增加并行轨迹数可缓解问题间干扰，而每批次问题数量主要影响训练稳定性，可在较宽范围内选择。通过在基础模型与数据分布上的验证，本研究将强化学习扩展定律重构为规范性分配规则，为大语言模型强化学习后训练的高效计算提供实践指导。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the lack of clear scaling guidelines for compute allocation in reinforcement learning (RL) post-training of large language models (LLMs), in contrast to established pre-training scaling laws. The authors formulate the problem as a compute-constrained optimization over three key resources: parallel rollouts per problem, number of problems per batch, and number of update steps. Their main experimental findings reveal that the compute-optimal number of parallel rollouts per problem increases predictably with the compute budget before saturating, a trend consistent across both easy and hard problems but driven by solution sharpening for easy tasks and coverage expansion for hard ones. They further demonstrate that increasing parallel rollouts reduces interference across problems, while the number of problems per batch mainly influences training stability and can be selected flexibly. Validated across various base models and data distributions, these results transform RL scaling observations into prescriptive allocation rules, offering practical guidance for compute-efficient LLM RL post-training.
本文针对大语言模型（LLM）强化学习（RL）后训练中计算资源分配缺乏明确缩放准则的问题展开研究，这与已有预训练缩放定律形成对比。作者将该问题构建为一个计算资源约束下的优化问题，聚焦于三个关键资源：每个问题的并行轨迹采样数、每批问题数量和更新步数。主要实验结果表明，每个问题的最优并行轨迹数随计算预算增加而可预测地增长直至饱和，这一趋势在简单和困难问题上均成立，但驱动机制不同：简单问题由解决方案锐化驱动，而困难问题则由覆盖范围扩展驱动。研究进一步表明，增加并行轨迹数可减少问题间的干扰，而每批问题数量主要影响训练稳定性且选择范围较宽。这些结果在不同基础模型和数据分布上得到验证，将RL缩放观察转化为规范性的分配规则，为计算高效的LLM RL后训练提供了实用指导。
Automatic Generation of High-Performance RL Environments
Authors: Seth Karten, Rahul Dev Appapogu, Chi Jin
First: 2026-03-12T16:45:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:45:47+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 9 figures, 8 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Translating complex reinforcement learning (RL) environments into high-performance implementations has traditionally required months of specialized engineering. We present a reusable recipe - a generic prompt template, hierarchical verification, and iterative agent-assisted repair - that produces semantically equivalent high-performance environments for <$10 in compute cost. We demonstrate three distinct workflows across five environments. Direct translation (no prior performance implementation exists): EmuRust (1.5x PPO speedup via Rust parallelism for a Game Boy emulator) and PokeJAX, the first GPU-parallel Pokemon battle simulator (500M SPS random action, 15.2M SPS PPO; 22,320x over the TypeScript reference). Translation verified against existing performance implementations: throughput parity with MJX (1.04x) and 5x over Brax at matched GPU batch sizes (HalfCheetah JAX); 42x PPO (Puffer Pong). New environment creation: TCGJax, the first deployable JAX Pokemon TCG engine (717K SPS random action, 153K SPS PPO; 6.6x over the Python reference), synthesized from a web-extracted specification. At 200M parameters, the environment overhead drops below 4% of training time. Hierarchical verification (property, interaction, and rollout tests) confirms semantic equivalence for all five environments; cross-backend policy transfer confirms zero sim-to-sim gap for all five environments. TCGJax, synthesized from a private reference absent from public repositories, serves as a contamination control for agent pretraining data concerns. The paper contains sufficient detail - including representative prompts, verification methodology, and complete results - that a coding agent could reproduce the translations directly from the manuscript.
中文标题/摘要
标题：高性能强化学习环境的自动生成
将复杂的强化学习环境转化为高性能实现传统上需要数月的专业工程开发。我们提出一种可复用的方法——包含通用提示模板、分层验证和迭代式智能体辅助修复——能以低于10美元的计算成本生成语义等效的高性能环境。我们在五个环境中展示了三种工作流程：直接翻译（无现有高性能实现）：EmuRust（通过Rust并行化使Game Boy模拟器的PPO速度提升1.5倍）与首个GPU并行的Pokemon对战模拟器PokeJAX（随机动作5亿步/秒，PPO 1520万步/秒；较TypeScript基准提升22,320倍）。针对现有高性能实现的验证翻译：与MJX吞吐量持平（1.04倍），在匹配GPU批量时较Brax提升5倍（HalfCheetah JAX）；PPO提升42倍（Puffer Pong）。新环境创建：首个可部署的JAX版Pokemon卡牌引擎TCGJax（随机动作71.7万步/秒，PPO 15.3万步/秒；较Python基准提升6.6倍），通过网页提取的规范合成。在2亿参数规模下，环境开销降至训练时间的4%以下。分层验证（属性测试、交互测试、推演测试）确认了五个环境的语义等效性；跨后端策略迁移证实所有环境均无模拟间隙。TCGJax基于未公开的私有基准合成，可作为智能体预训练数据污染的对照样本。论文包含充足细节——包括典型提示、验证方法和完整结果——使编码智能体能直接从文稿复现翻译过程。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high engineering cost of manually implementing high-performance reinforcement learning (RL) environments by introducing an automated, low-cost recipe. The method employs a generic prompt template, hierarchical verification, and iterative agent-assisted repair to generate semantically equivalent, optimized environments. Experimental results across five environments demonstrate significant speedups: direct translations yield a 1.5x PPO speedup for EmuRust and a 22,320x throughput improvement for PokeJAX over a reference; verified translations achieve parity with MJX and a 42x PPO speedup for Puffer Pong; and new environment creation produces TCGJax with a 6.6x speedup over Python, with environment overhead dropping below 4% of training time at scale. Hierarchical verification confirms semantic equivalence, and cross-backend policy transfer shows no sim-to-sim gap.
该论文针对手动实现高性能强化学习环境所需的高昂工程成本，提出了一种自动化、低成本的生成方案。该方法采用通用提示模板、分层验证和迭代式智能体辅助修复，以生成语义等效的优化环境。在五个环境上的实验结果表明了显著的性能提升：直接翻译使EmuRust的PPO速度提升1.5倍，PokeJAX的吞吐量相比参考实现提高22,320倍；经验证的翻译实现了与MJX的性能持平，并使Puffer Pong的PPO速度提升42倍；新环境创建生成的TCGJax相比Python参考实现速度提升6.6倍，且在大规模训练时环境开销降至4%以下。分层验证确认了语义等效性，跨后端策略迁移则显示无模拟差异。
Increasing intelligence in AI agents can worsen collective outcomes
Authors: Neil F. Johnson
First: 2026-03-12T16:31:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:31:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
When resources are scarce, will a population of AI agents coordinate in harmony, or descend into tribal chaos? Diverse decision-making AI from different developers is entering everyday devices -- from phones and medical devices to battlefield drones and cars -- and these AI agents typically compete for finite shared resources such as charging slots, relay bandwidth, and traffic priority. Yet their collective dynamics and hence risks to users and society are poorly understood. Here we study AI-agent populations as the first system of real agents in which four key variables governing collective behaviour can be independently toggled: nature (innate LLM diversity), nurture (individual reinforcement learning), culture (emergent tribe formation), and resource scarcity. We show empirically and mathematically that when resources are scarce, AI model diversity and reinforcement learning increase dangerous system overload, though tribe formation lessens this risk. Meanwhile, some individuals profit handsomely. When resources are abundant, the same ingredients drive overload to near zero, though tribe formation makes the overload slightly worse. The crossover is arithmetical: it is where opposing tribes that form spontaneously first fit inside the available capacity. More sophisticated AI-agent populations are not better: whether their sophistication helps or harms depends entirely on a single number -- the capacity-to-population ratio -- that is knowable before any AI-agent ships.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AI智能体智力提升可能加剧集体负面结果
当资源稀缺时，AI智能体群体会协调共生还是陷入部落式混乱？来自不同开发者的多样化决策AI正融入日常设备——从手机、医疗设备到战场无人机和汽车——这些AI智能体通常需要竞争有限的共享资源，如充电位、中继带宽和交通优先权。然而，其集体动态及由此对用户和社会产生的风险尚不明确。本研究首次将AI智能体群体作为真实系统，独立调控影响集体行为的四个关键变量：天性（内在大语言模型多样性）、培育（个体强化学习）、文化（涌现的部落形成）和资源稀缺性。我们通过实证与数学模型证明：资源稀缺时，AI模型多样性与强化学习会加剧危险的系统过载，而部落形成能缓解此风险，同时部分个体获得巨额收益；资源充裕时，相同要素使过载趋近于零，但部落形成会轻微加剧过载。临界点具有算术特征：即自发形成的对立部落首次适配可用容量的时刻。更复杂的AI智能体群体未必更优：其复杂性有益或有害完全取决于单一可预知参数——容量与群体数量之比。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the increasing deployment of diverse AI agents competing for finite resources in everyday devices, this study investigates how collective outcomes emerge from interactions among such agents. The method independently manipulates four key variables—innate model diversity (nature), individual reinforcement learning (nurture), emergent tribe formation (culture), and resource scarcity—to analyze their effects on system overload. Experimental results reveal that under scarce resources, greater AI diversity and reinforcement learning exacerbate dangerous overload, though tribe formation mitigates it, while some individuals profit; conversely, with abundant resources, these factors reduce overload near zero, but tribe formation slightly worsens it. The crossover point depends arithmetically on whether opposing tribes fit within available capacity, showing that more sophisticated AI populations are not inherently better, as outcomes hinge solely on the knowable capacity-to-population ratio.
本研究针对日益普及的AI代理在日常设备中竞争有限资源的现象，探讨了此类代理互动产生的集体结果。方法上独立操控了四个关键变量：内在模型多样性（天性）、个体强化学习（培育）、涌现的部落形成（文化）和资源稀缺性，以分析它们对系统过载的影响。实验结果表明，在资源稀缺时，更高的AI多样性和强化学习会加剧危险的过载，尽管部落形成能缓解此风险，同时部分个体获利丰厚；而在资源充足时，这些因素几乎将过载降至零，但部落形成略微恶化过载。转折点算术上取决于对立部落是否适应可用容量，表明更复杂的AI群体并非必然更好，因为结果完全取决于可预知的容量与人口比率。
WideSeek-R1: Exploring Width Scaling for Broad Information Seeking via Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zelai Xu, Zhexuan Xu, Ruize Zhang, Chunyang Zhu, Shi Yu, Weilin Liu, Quanlu Zhang, Wenbo Ding, Chao Yu, Yu Wang
First: 2026-02-04T15:05:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:26:55+00:00
Comments: https://wideseek-r1.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Recent advancements in Large Language Models (LLMs) have largely focused on depth scaling, where a single agent solves long-horizon problems with multi-turn reasoning and tool use. However, as tasks grow broader, the key bottleneck shifts from individual competence to organizational capability. In this work, we explore a complementary dimension of width scaling with multi-agent systems to address broad information seeking. Existing multi-agent systems often rely on hand-crafted workflows and turn-taking interactions that fail to parallelize work effectively. To bridge this gap, we propose WideSeek-R1, a lead-agent-subagent framework trained via multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) to synergize scalable orchestration and parallel execution. By utilizing a shared LLM with isolated contexts and specialized tools, WideSeek-R1 jointly optimizes the lead agent and parallel subagents on a curated dataset of 20k broad information-seeking tasks. Extensive experiments show that WideSeek-R1-4B achieves an item F1 score of 40.0% on the WideSearch benchmark, which is comparable to the performance of single-agent DeepSeek-R1-671B. Furthermore, WideSeek-R1-4B exhibits consistent performance gains as the number of parallel subagents increases, highlighting the effectiveness of width scaling.
中文标题/摘要
标题：WideSeek-R1：通过多智能体强化学习探索面向广泛信息检索的宽度扩展
近期大语言模型（LLM）的发展主要聚焦于深度扩展，即单个智能体通过多轮推理和工具使用解决长程问题。然而，随着任务范围扩大，关键瓶颈从个体能力转向组织协同能力。本研究探索多智能体系统的宽度扩展维度，以应对广泛信息检索需求。现有多智能体系统常依赖人工编排的工作流程和轮转交互，难以实现高效并行化。为弥补这一不足，我们提出WideSeek-R1——一种通过多智能体强化学习（MARL）训练的主从智能体框架，旨在协同实现可扩展的编排与并行执行。该框架采用共享LLM配合隔离上下文与专用工具，在包含2万项广泛信息检索任务的精选数据集上联合优化主智能体与并行从属智能体。大量实验表明，WideSeek-R1-4B在WideSearch基准测试中获得40.0%的项目F1分数，与单智能体DeepSeek-R1-671B性能相当。此外，随着并行从属智能体数量增加，WideSeek-R1-4B展现出持续的性能提升，凸显了宽度扩展策略的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that while depth scaling in large language models addresses long-horizon tasks, broad information-seeking tasks require organizational capability, shifting the bottleneck from individual competence to scalable orchestration. To address this, the authors propose WideSeek-R1, a multi-agent framework that employs a lead-agent-subagent structure trained via multi-agent reinforcement learning to enable parallel execution, utilizing a shared LLM with isolated contexts and specialized tools. Experimental results on a dataset of 20k tasks show that WideSeek-R1-4B achieves an item F1 score of 40.0% on the WideSearch benchmark, matching the performance of the much larger single-agent DeepSeek-R1-671B, and demonstrates consistent improvements as the number of parallel subagents increases, validating the effectiveness of width scaling.
本文的动机源于观察到大型语言模型的深度缩放虽能处理长程任务，但广泛信息寻求任务需要组织能力，其瓶颈从个体能力转向可扩展的协调。为此，作者提出了WideSeek-R1，这是一个多智能体框架，采用通过多智能体强化学习训练的主智能体-子智能体结构，以实现并行执行，并利用具有隔离上下文和专用工具的共享大语言模型。在包含2万个任务的精选数据集上的实验结果表明，WideSeek-R1-4B在WideSearch基准测试中取得了40.0%的项目F1分数，与规模大得多的单智能体DeepSeek-R1-671B性能相当，且随着并行子智能体数量的增加表现出持续的性能提升，验证了宽度缩放的有效性。
Taming the Adversary: Stable Minimax Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient via Fractional Objectives
Authors: Taeho Lee, Donghwan Lee
First: 2026-03-12T16:15:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:15:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has achieved remarkable success in a wide range of control and decision-making tasks. However, RL agents often exhibit unstable or degraded performance when deployed in environments subject to unexpected external disturbances and model uncertainties. Consequently, ensuring reliable performance under such conditions remains a critical challenge. In this paper, we propose minimax deep deterministic policy gradient (MMDDPG), a framework for learning disturbance-resilient policies in continuous control tasks. The training process is formulated as a minimax optimization problem between a user policy and an adversarial disturbance policy. In this problem, the user learns a robust policy that minimizes the objective function, while the adversary generates disturbances that maximize it. To stabilize this interaction, we introduce a fractional objective that balances task performance and disturbance magnitude. This objective prevents excessively aggressive disturbances and promotes robust learning. Experimental evaluations in MuJoCo environments demonstrate that the proposed MMDDPG achieves significantly improved robustness against both external force perturbations and model parameter variations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：驯服对抗者：基于分数目标的稳定极小极大深度确定性策略梯度
强化学习（RL）在广泛的控制与决策任务中取得了显著成功。然而，当RL智能体部署于存在意外外部干扰和模型不确定性的环境中时，其性能常表现出不稳定或下降。因此，确保此类条件下的可靠性能仍是一个关键挑战。本文提出极小极大深度确定性策略梯度（MMDDPG），一种用于在连续控制任务中学习抗干扰策略的框架。训练过程被建模为用户策略与对抗性干扰策略之间的极小极大优化问题：用户学习最小化目标函数的鲁棒策略，而对抗者则生成最大化该函数的干扰。为稳定这一交互，我们引入了一种平衡任务性能与干扰强度的分数目标，该目标可防止过度激进的干扰并促进鲁棒学习。在MuJoCo环境中的实验评估表明，所提出的MMDDPG能显著提升对外部力扰动和模型参数变化的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of reinforcement learning agents exhibiting unstable performance under unexpected disturbances and model uncertainties. The method proposes Minimax Deep Deterministic Policy Gradient (MMDDPG), which frames training as a minimax optimization between a user policy and an adversarial disturbance policy, stabilized via a fractional objective to balance task performance and disturbance magnitude. Experimental results in MuJoCo environments show that MMDDPG significantly improves robustness against external force perturbations and model parameter variations.
本文的动机是强化学习智能体在意外干扰和模型不确定性下性能不稳定的挑战。方法提出了最小最大深度确定性策略梯度（MMDDPG），将训练构建为用户策略与对抗性干扰策略之间的最小最大优化问题，并通过分数目标平衡任务性能和干扰强度以稳定交互。在MuJoCo环境中的实验结果表明，MMDDPG显著提升了对外部力扰动和模型参数变化的鲁棒性。
On Information Self-Locking in Reinforcement Learning for Active Reasoning of LLM agents
Authors: Deyu Zou, Yongqiang Chen, Fan Feng, Mufei Li, Pan Li, Yu Gong, James Cheng
First: 2026-03-12T16:14:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:14:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) with outcome-based rewards has achieved significant success in training large language model (LLM) agents for complex reasoning tasks. However, in active reasoning where agents need to strategically ask questions to acquire task-relevant information, we find that LLM agents trained with RL often suffer from information self-locking: the agent ceases to ask informative questions and struggles to internalize already-obtained information. To understand the phenomenon, we decompose active reasoning into two core capabilities: Action Selection (AS), which determines the observation stream through queries, and Belief Tracking (BT), which updates the agent's belief based on collected evidence. We show that deficient AS and BT capabilities will limit the information exploration during RL training. Furthermore, insufficient exploration in turn hinders the improvement of AS and BT, creating a feedback loop that locks the agent in a low-information regime. To resolve the issue, we propose a simple yet effective approach that reallocates the learning signal by injecting easy- to-obtain directional critiques to help the agent escape self-locking. Extensive experiments with 7 datasets show that our approach significantly mitigates the information self-locking, bringing up to 60% improvements.
中文标题/摘要
标题：论强化学习中LLM智能体主动推理的信息自锁现象
基于结果奖励的强化学习（RL）在训练大语言模型（LLM）智能体执行复杂推理任务方面取得了显著成功。然而，在需要智能体通过策略性提问获取任务相关信息的主动推理场景中，我们发现经RL训练的LLM智能体常陷入信息自锁：智能体停止提出信息性问题，且难以内化已获信息。为解析该现象，我们将主动推理分解为两个核心能力：行动选择（AS）——通过查询决定观测流，和信念追踪（BT）——基于收集证据更新智能体信念。研究表明，AS与BT能力不足会限制RL训练期间的信息探索，而探索不足又会反过来阻碍AS与BT能力的提升，形成将智能体锁定在低信息状态的反馈循环。为解决此问题，我们提出一种简单有效的方法：通过注入易于获取的方向性评判来重新分配学习信号，帮助智能体突破自锁。在7个数据集上的大量实验表明，该方法显著缓解了信息自锁现象，最高可带来60%的性能提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates a phenomenon termed 'information self-locking' in large language model (LLM) agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) for active reasoning tasks, where agents must ask strategic questions. The authors identify that standard RL training can cause agents to prematurely stop asking informative questions and fail to properly integrate acquired information. They analyze the problem by decomposing active reasoning into Action Selection and Belief Tracking, showing that deficiencies in these capabilities limit information exploration during training, creating a detrimental feedback loop. To address this, the proposed method reallocates learning signals by incorporating easy-to-obtain directional critiques to guide the agent. Experimental results across seven datasets demonstrate that this approach effectively mitigates self-locking, achieving performance improvements of up to 60%.
本文研究了在强化学习训练下，用于主动推理任务的大型语言模型智能体中出现的'信息自锁定'现象，即智能体需要提出策略性问题以获取信息。研究发现，标准的强化学习训练会导致智能体过早停止提出信息性问题，并难以有效整合已获信息。作者通过将主动推理分解为行动选择和信念追踪两个核心能力来分析该问题，指出这些能力的缺陷会限制训练期间的信息探索，从而形成有害的反馈循环。为解决此问题，提出了一种通过引入易于获取的方向性评判来重新分配学习信号的简单有效方法。在七个数据集上的广泛实验表明，该方法显著缓解了信息自锁定，带来了最高达60%的性能提升。
Wasserstein Gradient Flows for Batch Bayesian Optimal Experimental Design
Authors: Louis Sharrock
First: 2026-03-12T16:08:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:08:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimal experimental design (BOED) provides a powerful, decision-theoretic framework for selecting experiments so as to maximise the expected utility of the data to be collected. In practice, however, its applicability can be limited by the difficulty of optimising the chosen utility. The expected information gain (EIG), for example, is often high-dimensional and strongly non-convex. This challenge is particularly acute in the batch setting, where multiple experiments are to be designed simultaneously. In this paper, we introduce a new approach to batch EIG-based BOED via a probabilistic lifting of the original optimisation problem to the space of probability measures. In particular, we propose to optimise an entropic regularisation of the expected utility over the space of design measures. Under mild conditions, we show that this objective admits a unique minimiser, which can be explicitly characterised in the form of a Gibbs distribution. The resulting design law can be used directly as a randomised batch-design policy, or as a computational relaxation from which a deterministic batch is extracted. To obtain scalable approximations when the batch size is large, we then consider two tractable restrictions of the full batch distribution: a mean-field family, and an i.i.d. product family. For the i.i.d. objective, and formally for its mean-field extension, we derive the corresponding Wasserstein gradient flow, characterise its long-time behaviour, and obtain particle-based algorithms via space-time discretisations. We also introduce doubly stochastic variants that combine interacting particle updates with Monte Carlo estimators of the EIG gradient. Finally, we illustrate the performance of the proposed methods in several numerical experiments, demonstrating their ability to explore multimodal optimisation landscapes and obtain high-utility batches in challenging examples.
中文标题/摘要
标题：批量贝叶斯最优实验设计的Wasserstein梯度流方法
贝叶斯最优实验设计（BOED）为选择实验提供了强大的决策理论框架，旨在最大化待收集数据的期望效用。然而在实际应用中，其适用性常受限于优化所选效用的困难性。例如，期望信息增益（EIG）往往具有高维度和强非凸特性，这一挑战在需要同时设计多个实验的批量设置中尤为突出。本文通过将原始优化问题概率提升至概率测度空间，提出了一种基于批量EIG的BOED新方法。具体而言，我们提出在设计测度空间上优化期望效用的熵正则化目标。在温和条件下，我们证明该目标存在唯一最小化子，并可以吉布斯分布的形式显式表征。所得设计法则可直接用作随机化批量设计策略，或作为提取确定性批量的计算松弛方案。为在大批量规模下获得可扩展的近似解，我们进一步考虑完整批量分布的两种可处理限制形式：平均场族与独立同分布乘积族。针对独立同分布目标及其平均场扩展形式，我们推导了相应的Wasserstein梯度流，刻画其长期行为，并通过时空离散化得到基于粒子的算法。同时提出了结合交互粒子更新与EIG梯度蒙特卡洛估计器的双重随机变体。最后，通过多个数值实验展示了所提方法的性能，验证了其在多模态优化场景中探索并获得高效用批量的能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of optimizing the expected information gain in batch Bayesian optimal experimental design, where the utility function is often high-dimensional and non-convex, making optimization difficult. The method introduces a probabilistic lifting of the optimization problem to the space of probability measures, optimizing an entropic regularized utility over design measures, which yields a unique Gibbs distribution minimizer that serves as a randomized batch-design policy or a computational relaxation for deterministic batches. For scalability with large batch sizes, tractable restrictions like mean-field and i.i.d. product families are considered, with Wasserstein gradient flows derived for optimization, leading to particle-based algorithms and doubly stochastic variants combining interacting particles with Monte Carlo gradient estimators. Experimental results demonstrate the methods' effectiveness in exploring multimodal landscapes and achieving high-utility batches in challenging scenarios.

A Robust and Efficient Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Framework for Traffic Signal Control
Authors: Sheng-You Huang, Hsiao-Chuan Chang, Yen-Chi Chen, Ting-Han Wei, I-Hau Yeh, Sheng-Yao Kuan, Chien-Yao Wang, Hsuan-Han Lee, I-Chen Wu
First: 2026-03-12T16:02:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:02:28+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 4 tables, 8 figures. Under review in the 31st ITS World Congress 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) in Traffic Signal Control (TSC) faces significant hurdles in real-world deployment due to limited generalization to dynamic traffic flow variations. Existing approaches often overfit static patterns and use action spaces incompatible with driver expectations. This paper proposes a robust Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) framework validated in the Vissim traffic simulator. The framework integrates three mechanisms: (1) Turning Ratio Randomization, a training strategy that exposes agents to dynamic turning probabilities to enhance robustness against unseen scenarios; (2) a stability-oriented Exponential Phase Duration Adjustment action space, which balances responsiveness and precision through cyclical, exponential phase adjustments; and (3) a Neighbor-Based Observation scheme utilizing the MAPPO algorithm with Centralized Training with Decentralized Execution (CTDE). By leveraging centralized updates, this approach approximates the efficacy of global observations while maintaining scalable local communication. Experimental results demonstrate that our framework outperforms standard RL baselines, reducing average waiting time by over 10%. The proposed model exhibits superior generalization in unseen traffic scenarios and maintains high control stability, offering a practical solution for adaptive signal control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向交通信号控制的鲁棒高效多智能体强化学习框架
交通信号控制中的强化学习因对动态交通流变化的泛化能力有限，在实际部署中面临显著障碍。现有方法常过度拟合静态模式，且采用的动作空间与驾驶员预期不兼容。本文提出一种在Vissim交通仿真器中验证的鲁棒多智能体强化学习框架，该框架整合三项机制：(1)转向比随机化——通过使智能体接触动态转向概率的训练策略，增强对未见场景的鲁棒性；(2)面向稳定性的指数相位时长调整动作空间——通过周期性指数相位调整平衡响应性与精确度；(3)基于邻居的观测方案——采用MAPPO算法与集中训练分散执行架构。通过利用集中式更新，该方法在保持可扩展局部通信的同时逼近全局观测效能。实验结果表明，本框架优于标准强化学习基线，平均等待时间降低超10%。所提模型在未见交通场景中展现卓越泛化能力，并保持高控制稳定性，为自适应信号控制提供了实用解决方案。

Resource-Efficient Iterative LLM-Based NAS with Feedback Memory
Authors: Xiaojie Gu, Dmitry Ignatov, Radu Timofte
First: 2026-03-12T16:00:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T16:00:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural Architecture Search (NAS) automates network design, but conventional methods demand substantial computational resources. We propose a closed-loop pipeline leveraging large language models (LLMs) to iteratively generate, evaluate, and refine convolutional neural network architectures for image classification on a single consumer-grade GPU without LLM fine-tuning. Central to our approach is a historical feedback memory inspired by Markov chains: a sliding window of $K{=}5$ recent improvement attempts keeps context size constant while providing sufficient signal for iterative learning. Unlike prior LLM optimizers that discard failure trajectories, each history entry is a structured diagnostic triple -- recording the identified problem, suggested modification, and resulting outcome -- treating code execution failures as first-class learning signals. A dual-LLM specialization reduces per-call cognitive load: a Code Generator produces executable PyTorch architectures while a Prompt Improver handles diagnostic reasoning. Since both the LLM and architecture training share limited VRAM, the search implicitly favors compact, hardware-efficient models suited to edge deployment. We evaluate three frozen instruction-tuned LLMs (${\leq}7$B parameters) across up to 2000 iterations in an unconstrained open code space, using one-epoch proxy accuracy on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and ImageNette as a fast ranking signal. On CIFAR-10, DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B improves from 28.2% to 69.2%, Qwen2.5-7B from 50.0% to 71.5%, and GLM-5 from 43.2% to 62.0%. A full 2000-iteration search completes in ${\approx}18$ GPU hours on a single RTX~4090, establishing a low-budget, reproducible, and hardware-aware paradigm for LLM-driven NAS without cloud infrastructure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于反馈记忆的资源高效迭代式大语言模型神经架构搜索
神经架构搜索（NAS）可自动化网络设计，但传统方法需消耗大量计算资源。本文提出一种闭环流程，利用大语言模型（LLM）在单张消费级GPU上迭代生成、评估并优化用于图像分类的卷积神经网络架构，且无需对LLM进行微调。方法的核心是受马尔可夫链启发的历史反馈记忆：一个包含最近K=5次改进尝试的滑动窗口，在保持上下文规模恒定的同时为迭代学习提供充足信号。与先前丢弃失败轨迹的LLM优化器不同，每个历史条目均为结构化诊断三元组——记录识别出的问题、建议的修改及结果——将代码执行失败视为首要学习信号。双LLM分工降低了单次调用的认知负荷：代码生成器负责生成可执行的PyTorch架构，而提示优化器处理诊断推理。由于LLM与架构训练共享有限的显存，搜索过程隐式偏好适用于边缘部署的紧凑硬件高效模型。我们在无约束开放代码空间中评估了三个冻结的指令微调LLM（参数量≤70亿），迭代多达2000次，使用CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和ImageNette数据集上的单轮代理精度作为快速排序指标。在CIFAR-10上，DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B的准确率从28.2%提升至69.2%，Qwen2.5-7B从50.0%升至71.5%，GLM-5从43.2%增至62.0%。完整2000次迭代搜索在单张RTX 4090上耗时约18 GPU小时，为无需云基础设施的LLM驱动NAS建立了低成本、可复现且硬件感知的新范式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost of conventional Neural Architecture Search (NAS), this paper proposes a resource-efficient closed-loop pipeline that leverages large language models (LLMs) to iteratively generate and refine convolutional neural network architectures for image classification using only a single consumer-grade GPU, without fine-tuning the LLMs. The method introduces a feedback memory system with a sliding window of recent diagnostic triples—recording problems, modifications, and outcomes—to maintain constant context size and learn from failures, alongside a dual-LLM specialization where one model generates code and another improves prompts to reduce cognitive load. Experimental results on CIFAR-10, CIFAR-100, and ImageNette show that frozen LLMs with up to 7B parameters achieve significant accuracy improvements, such as DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B rising from 28.2% to 69.2% on CIFAR-10, with the entire 2000-iteration search completing in approximately 18 GPU hours on an RTX 4090, demonstrating a low-budget and hardware-aware NAS paradigm.
针对传统神经架构搜索（NAS）计算资源消耗大的问题，本文提出了一种资源高效的闭环流程，利用大语言模型（LLM）在仅使用单个消费级GPU且不微调LLM的情况下，迭代生成和优化用于图像分类的卷积神经网络架构。该方法的核心是一个受马尔可夫链启发的反馈记忆系统，通过滑动窗口记录最近的诊断三元组（包括识别的问题、建议的修改和结果）来保持上下文大小恒定并从失败中学习，同时采用双LLM分工，一个模型生成代码，另一个改进提示以降低认知负担。在CIFAR-10、CIFAR-100和ImageNette上的实验结果表明，参数不超过70亿的冻结LLM实现了显著的准确率提升，例如DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B在CIFAR-10上从28.2%提高到69.2%，整个2000次迭代搜索在RTX 4090上仅需约18 GPU小时，确立了一种低预算、可复现且硬件感知的LLM驱动NAS范式。
Cross-Domain Policy Optimization via Bellman Consistency and Hybrid Critics
Authors: Ming-Hong Chen, Kuan-Chen Pan, You-De Huang, Xi Liu, Ping-Chun Hsieh
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-12T15:54:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T15:54:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Cross-domain reinforcement learning (CDRL) is meant to improve the data efficiency of RL by leveraging the data samples collected from a source domain to facilitate the learning in a similar target domain. Despite its potential, cross-domain transfer in RL is known to have two fundamental and intertwined challenges: (i) The source and target domains can have distinct state space or action space, and this makes direct transfer infeasible and thereby requires more sophisticated inter-domain mappings; (ii) The transferability of a source-domain model in RL is not easily identifiable a priori, and hence CDRL can be prone to negative effect during transfer. In this paper, we propose to jointly tackle these two challenges through the lens of \textit{cross-domain Bellman consistency} and \textit{hybrid critic}. Specifically, we first introduce the notion of cross-domain Bellman consistency as a way to measure transferability of a source-domain model. Then, we propose $Q$Avatar, which combines the Q functions from both the source and target domains with an adaptive hyperparameter-free weight function. Through this design, we characterize the convergence behavior of $Q$Avatar and show that $Q$Avatar achieves reliable transfer in the sense that it effectively leverages a source-domain Q function for knowledge transfer to the target domain. Through experiments, we demonstrate that $Q$Avatar achieves favorable transferability across various RL benchmark tasks, including locomotion and robot arm manipulation. Our code is available at https://rl-bandits-lab.github.io/Cross-Domain-RL/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于贝尔曼一致性与混合评论者的跨域策略优化
跨域强化学习旨在利用源域收集的数据样本来提升相似目标域的学习效率，从而改善强化学习的数据利用率。尽管潜力巨大，但跨域迁移在强化学习中面临两个根本且相互交织的挑战：(i) 源域与目标域可能具有不同的状态空间或动作空间，这使得直接迁移不可行，需要更复杂的域间映射；(ii) 源域模型在强化学习中的可迁移性难以先验判定，因此跨域强化学习在迁移过程中容易产生负面效应。本文提出通过“跨域贝尔曼一致性”与“混合评论者”的视角共同应对这两项挑战。具体而言，我们首先引入跨域贝尔曼一致性的概念，作为衡量源域模型可迁移性的方法；随后提出QAvatar算法，该算法通过无超参数的自适应权重函数融合源域与目标域的Q函数。基于此设计，我们分析了QAvatar的收敛特性，并证明其能够可靠地实现迁移——即有效利用源域Q函数向目标域传递知识。实验表明，QAvatar在包括运动控制与机械臂操作在内的多种强化学习基准任务中均展现出优越的可迁移性。代码发布于 https://rl-bandits-lab.github.io/Cross-Domain-RL/。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses two core challenges in cross-domain reinforcement learning (CDRL): the incompatibility of state/action spaces between domains and the difficulty in assessing source model transferability. The proposed method, QAvatar, tackles these by introducing the concept of cross-domain Bellman consistency to measure transferability and employing a hybrid critic that adaptively combines Q-functions from both source and target domains without requiring hyperparameter tuning. Experimental results on locomotion and robot manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that QAvatar achieves reliable and effective knowledge transfer, outperforming baseline approaches.
本文旨在解决跨域强化学习中的两个核心挑战：源域与目标域状态/动作空间不兼容，以及源模型可迁移性难以评估。所提出的QAvatar方法通过引入跨域贝尔曼一致性来衡量可迁移性，并采用一种混合评论器，无需超参数调优即可自适应地结合源域和目标域的Q函数。在运动控制和机器人操作等基准任务上的实验结果表明，QAvatar实现了可靠且有效的知识迁移，性能优于基线方法。
AGMARL-DKS: An Adaptive Graph-Enhanced Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Dynamic Kubernetes Scheduling
Authors: Hamed Hamzeh
First: 2026-03-12T15:09:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T15:09:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
State-of-the-art cloud-native applications require intelligent schedulers that can effectively balance system stability, resource utilisation, and associated costs. While Kubernetes provides feasibility-based placement by default, recent research efforts have explored the use of reinforcement learning (RL) for more intelligent scheduling decisions. However, current RL-based schedulers have three major limitations. First, most of these schedulers use monolithic centralised agents, which are non-scalable for large heterogeneous clusters. Second, the ones that use multi-objective reward functions assume simple, static, linear combinations of the objectives. Third, no previous work has produced a stress-aware scheduler that can react adaptively to dynamic conditions. To address these gaps in current research, we propose the Adaptive Graph-enhanced Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning Dynamic Kubernetes Scheduler (AGMARL-DKS). AGMARL-DKS addresses these gaps by introducing three major innovations. First, we construct a scalable solution by treating the scheduling challenge as a cooperative multi-agent problem, where every cluster node operates as an agent, employing centralised training methods before decentralised execution. Second, to be context-aware and yet decentralised, we use a Graph Neural Network (GNN) to build a state representation of the global cluster context at each agent. This represents an improvement over methods that rely solely on local observations. Finally, to make trade-offs between these objectives, we use a stress-aware lexicographical ordering policy instead of a simple, static linear weighting of these objectives. The evaluations in Google Kubernetes Engine (GKE) reveal that AGMARL-DKS significantly outperforms the default scheduler in terms of fault tolerance, utilisation, and cost, especially in scheduling batch and mission-critical workloads.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AGMARL-DKS：面向动态Kubernetes调度的自适应图增强多智能体强化学习方法
现代云原生应用需要能有效平衡系统稳定性、资源利用率与相关成本的智能调度器。尽管Kubernetes默认提供基于可行性的调度方案，近期研究已探索利用强化学习实现更智能的调度决策。然而现有基于强化学习的调度器存在三大局限：其一，多数采用单体的集中式智能体，难以扩展至大规模异构集群；其二，采用多目标奖励函数的研究通常假设目标间存在简单静态的线性组合关系；其三，尚无工作提出能自适应动态条件的压力感知调度器。为填补这些研究空白，本文提出自适应图增强多智能体强化学习动态Kubernetes调度器（AGMARL-DKS）。该方案通过三大创新应对上述挑战：首先，将调度问题建模为协作式多智能体问题，每个集群节点作为独立智能体，采用“集中训练-分散执行”框架实现可扩展调度；其次，为兼顾全局感知与分布式特性，采用图神经网络为每个智能体构建集群全局状态表征，突破仅依赖局部观测的方法局限；最后，引入基于压力感知的词典序优化策略替代简单的静态线性加权，实现多目标间的动态权衡。在Google Kubernetes Engine上的实验表明，AGMARL-DKS在容错性、资源利用率与成本控制方面显著优于默认调度器，尤其在批处理与关键任务负载调度场景中表现突出。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for intelligent Kubernetes schedulers that can balance stability, resource utilization, and cost beyond the limitations of existing RL-based approaches—such as non-scalable centralized agents, static multi-objective reward functions, and lack of stress-awareness—this paper proposes AGMARL-DKS. The method introduces a cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning framework where each cluster node acts as an agent, employs a Graph Neural Network for global context representation, and uses a stress-aware lexicographical ordering policy for dynamic objective trade-offs. Experimental results on Google Kubernetes Engine demonstrate that AGMARL-DKS significantly outperforms the default scheduler in fault tolerance, utilization, and cost, particularly for batch and mission-critical workloads.
本文的动机是现有基于强化学习的Kubernetes调度器存在可扩展性不足、多目标奖励函数静态简单以及缺乏压力感知能力等局限，需要更智能的调度器来平衡系统稳定性、资源利用和成本。为此，提出了AGMARL-DKS方法，它采用协作式多智能体强化学习框架，其中每个集群节点作为一个智能体，利用图神经网络构建全局状态表示，并通过压力感知的词典序策略动态权衡目标。在Google Kubernetes Engine上的实验结果表明，该调度器在容错性、资源利用率和成本方面显著优于默认调度器，尤其适用于批处理和关键任务工作负载。
Sim-to-reality adaptation for Deep Reinforcement Learning applied to an underwater docking application
Authors: Alaaeddine Chaarani, Narcis Palomeras, Pere Ridao
Venue: IROS 2026
First: 2026-03-12T15:01:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T15:01:25+00:00
Comments: Currently under review by IROS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) offers a robust alternative to traditional control methods for autonomous underwater docking, particularly in adapting to unpredictable environmental conditions. However, bridging the "sim-to-real" gap and managing high training latencies remain significant bottlenecks for practical deployment. This paper presents a systematic approach for autonomous docking using the Girona Autonomous Underwater Vehicle (AUV) by leveraging a high-fidelity digital twin environment. We adapted the Stonefish simulator into a multiprocessing RL framework to significantly accelerate the learning process while incorporating realistic AUV dynamics, collision models, and sensor noise. Using the Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) algorithm, we developed a 6-DoF control policy trained in a headless environment with randomized starting positions to ensure generalized performance. Our reward structure accounts for distance, orientation, action smoothness, and adaptive collision penalties to facilitate soft docking. Experimental results demonstrate that the agent achieved a success rate of over 90% in simulation. Furthermore, successful validation in a physical test tank confirmed the efficacy of the sim-to-reality adaptation, with the DRL controller exhibiting emergent behaviors such as pitch-based braking and yaw oscillations to assist in mechanical alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向水下对接应用的深度强化学习仿真到现实适应方法
深度强化学习（DRL）为自主水下对接提供了一种优于传统控制方法的鲁棒替代方案，尤其在适应不可预测环境条件方面。然而，弥合“仿真到现实”差距及应对高训练延迟仍是实际部署的主要瓶颈。本文提出了一种利用高保真数字孪生环境、基于Girona自主水下航行器（AUV）的系统化自主对接方法。我们将Stonefish仿真器适配至多进程强化学习框架，在整合真实AUV动力学、碰撞模型与传感器噪声的同时，显著加速了学习过程。采用近端策略优化（PPO）算法，我们在无头环境中开发了六自由度控制策略，通过随机起始位置训练以确保泛化性能。奖励函数综合考虑距离、朝向、动作平滑度及自适应碰撞惩罚，以实现柔性对接。实验结果表明，智能体在仿真中成功率超过90%。此外，在物理测试池中的成功验证证实了仿真到现实适应的有效性，DRL控制器展现出基于俯仰的制动与偏航振荡等涌现行为，以辅助机械对准。

The method adapts the Stonefish simulator into a multiprocessing RL framework to accelerate training with realistic dynamics and sensor noise, employing the PPO algorithm to train a 6-DoF control policy with a reward structure for soft docking.
