Value Under Ignorance in Universal Artificial Intelligence
Authors: Cole Wyeth, Marcus Hutter
Venue: In International Conference on Artificial General Intelligence (pp. 338-349). Cham: Springer Nature Switzerland (2025)
First: 2025-12-18T21:34:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T14:48:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We generalize the AIXI reinforcement learning agent to admit a wider class of utility functions. Assigning a utility to each possible interaction history forces us to confront the ambiguity that some hypotheses in the agent's belief distribution only predict a finite prefix of the history, which is sometimes interpreted as implying a chance of death equal to a quantity called the semimeasure loss. This death interpretation suggests one way to assign utilities to such history prefixes. We argue that it is as natural to view the belief distributions as imprecise probability distributions, with the semimeasure loss as total ignorance. This motivates us to consider the consequences of computing expected utilities with Choquet integrals from imprecise probability theory, including an investigation of their computability level. We recover the standard recursive value function as a special case. However, our most general expected utilities under the death interpretation cannot be characterized as such Choquet integrals.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通用人工智能中无知状态下的价值评估
本研究将AIXI强化学习智能体推广至更广泛的效用函数类别。为每个可能的交互历史分配效用时，需处理智能体信念分布中某些假设仅能预测历史有限前缀的模糊性问题，这常被解释为隐含一种称为半测度损失的‘死亡概率’。该死亡解释为这类历史前缀的效用分配提供了一种思路。我们认为，将信念分布视为不精确概率分布，并将半测度损失视为完全无知状态同样具有自然性。这促使我们基于不精确概率理论中的Choquet积分计算期望效用，并探讨其可计算性层级。标准递归价值函数可作为特例被还原。然而，在死亡解释下最广义的期望效用无法被表征为此类Choquet积分。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of assigning utilities to interaction histories in the AIXI reinforcement learning framework when some hypotheses only predict finite prefixes, which is often interpreted as a 'semimeasure loss' akin to a chance of death. The motivation is to move beyond this death interpretation by treating belief distributions as imprecise probabilities, where the semimeasure loss represents total ignorance, prompting the use of Choquet integrals from imprecise probability theory to compute expected utilities. The method involves generalizing AIXI to accommodate a broader class of utility functions and investigating the computability level of these Choquet integrals. The main experimental results show that while the standard recursive value function emerges as a special case, the most general expected utilities under the death interpretation cannot be characterized as such Choquet integrals, highlighting limitations in this approach.
本文针对AIXI强化学习框架中，当某些假设仅能预测有限历史前缀时如何分配效用的问题展开研究，这一现象常被解释为类似于死亡机会的“半测度损失”。其动机是超越这种死亡解释，将信念分布视为不精确概率，其中半测度损失代表完全无知，从而促使使用不精确概率理论中的Choquet积分来计算期望效用。方法包括推广AIXI以容纳更广泛的效用函数类别，并探讨这些Choquet积分的可计算性水平。主要实验结果表明，虽然标准递归值函数可作为特例恢复，但基于死亡解释的最一般期望效用无法被表征为此类Choquet积分，揭示了该方法的局限性。
Impact of Markov Decision Process Design on Sim-to-Real Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tatjana Krau, Jorge Mandlmaier, Tobias Damm, Frieder Heieck
First: 2026-03-10T09:41:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T14:26:08+00:00
Comments: This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has demonstrated strong potential for industrial process control, yet policies trained in simulation often suffer from a significant sim-to-real gap when deployed on physical hardware. This work systematically analyzes how core Markov Decision Process (MDP) design choices -- state composition, target inclusion, reward formulation, termination criteria, and environment dynamics models -- affect this transfer. Using a color mixing task, we evaluate different MDP configurations and mixing dynamics across simulation and real-world experiments. We validate our findings on physical hardware, demonstrating that physics-based dynamics models achieve up to 50% real-world success under strict precision constraints where simplified models fail entirely. Our results provide practical MDP design guidelines for deploying RL in industrial process control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：马尔可夫决策过程设计对仿真到现实强化学习迁移的影响
强化学习在工业过程控制中展现出巨大潜力，但仿真训练的策略在部署到物理硬件时常面临显著的仿真与现实差距。本研究系统分析了马尔可夫决策过程的核心设计要素——状态构成、目标设定、奖励函数、终止条件与环境动力学模型——对迁移效果的影响。通过颜色混合任务，我们在仿真与真实实验中评估了不同MDP配置与混合动力学模型。在物理硬件上的验证表明：在简化模型完全失效的严格精度约束下，基于物理的动力学模型可实现高达50%的现实成功率。本研究为工业过程控制中强化学习的部署提供了实用的MDP设计指南。
Summary / 总结
This work is motivated by the significant sim-to-real performance gap that hinders the deployment of reinforcement learning (RL) policies trained in simulation for industrial process control. The method involves a systematic analysis of how core Markov Decision Process (MDP) design choices—including state composition, reward formulation, and environment dynamics models—affect policy transfer. The main experimental results, validated on a physical color mixing task, show that physics-based dynamics models achieve up to a 50% real-world success rate under strict precision constraints, whereas simplified models fail entirely, providing practical guidelines for RL deployment.
本研究的动机在于，在工业过程控制中，于仿真环境中训练的强化学习策略在部署到物理硬件时存在显著的仿真到现实性能差距。其方法系统分析了马尔可夫决策过程的核心设计选择——包括状态构成、奖励函数和环境动力学模型——如何影响策略的迁移。在以物理颜色混合任务验证的主要实验结果中表明，基于物理的动力学模型在严格精度约束下实现了高达50%的现实成功率，而简化模型则完全失败，从而为强化学习的实际部署提供了实用设计指南。
FlexRec: Adapting LLM-based Recommenders for Flexible Needs via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yijun Pan, Weikang Qiu, Qiyao Ma, Mingxuan Ju, Tong Zhao, Neil Shah, Rex Ying
First: 2026-03-12T13:14:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T13:14:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Modern recommender systems must adapt to dynamic, need-specific objectives for diverse recommendation scenarios, yet most traditional recommenders are optimized for a single static target and struggle to reconfigure behavior on demand. Recent advances in reinforcement-learning-based post-training have unlocked strong instruction-following and reasoning capabilities in LLMs, suggesting a principled route for aligning them to complex recommendation goals. Motivated by this, we study closed-set autoregressive ranking, where an LLM generates a permutation over a fixed candidate set conditioned on user context and an explicit need instruction. However, applying RL to this setting faces two key obstacles: (i) sequence-level rewards yield coarse credit assignment that fails to provide fine-grained training signals, and (ii) interaction feedback is sparse and noisy, which together lead to inefficient and unstable updates. We propose FlexRec, a post-training RL framework that addresses both issues with (1) a causally grounded item-level reward based on counterfactual swaps within the remaining candidate pool, and (2) critic-guided, uncertainty-aware scaling that explicitly models reward uncertainty and down-weights low-confidence rewards to stabilize learning under sparse supervision. Across diverse recommendation scenarios and objectives, FlexRec achieves substantial gains: it improves NDCG@5 by up to \textbf{59\%} and Recall@5 by up to \textbf{109.4\%} in need-specific ranking, and further achieves up to \textbf{24.1\%} Recall@5 improvement under generalization settings, outperforming strong traditional recommenders and LLM-based baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FlexRec：基于强化学习的LLM推荐系统灵活需求适配框架
现代推荐系统需适应动态、需求特定的多样化场景目标，但传统推荐器多针对单一静态目标优化，难以按需调整行为。基于强化学习的后训练技术近期释放了大语言模型（LLM）强大的指令跟随与推理能力，为对齐复杂推荐目标提供了理论路径。本文研究闭集自回归排序任务，即LLM根据用户上下文和显式需求指令对固定候选集生成排列序列。然而该场景应用强化学习面临两大挑战：（1）序列级奖励信号粗糙，缺乏细粒度训练指导；（2）交互反馈稀疏且含噪声，共同导致更新低效不稳定。为此提出FlexRec后训练强化学习框架，通过（1）基于候选池内反事实交换的因果化项目级奖励机制，以及（2）评论家引导的 uncertainty-aware 奖励缩放技术（显式建模奖励不确定性并降权低置信度信号），在稀疏监督下实现稳定学习。在多场景实验中，FlexRec在需求特定排序任务中NDCG@5提升最高达59%，Recall@5提升最高达109.4%；在泛化场景下Recall@5进一步提升最高达24.1%，显著优于传统推荐器与LLM基线模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for recommender systems that can dynamically adapt to diverse and specific user objectives, this paper introduces FlexRec, a reinforcement learning framework for post-training large language models (LLMs) to perform closed-set autoregressive ranking based on user context and explicit need instructions. The method addresses key challenges of coarse credit assignment and sparse, noisy feedback by employing a causally grounded item-level reward derived from counterfactual swaps and a critic-guided, uncertainty-aware scaling mechanism to stabilize learning. Experimental results across various recommendation scenarios show that FlexRec substantially outperforms baselines, achieving improvements of up to 59% in NDCG@5 and 109.4% in Recall@5 for need-specific ranking, and up to 24.1% in Recall@5 under generalization settings.
本文的动机是使推荐系统能够动态适应多样且具体的用户目标，为此提出了FlexRec，这是一个基于强化学习的框架，用于对大语言模型进行后训练，使其能够根据用户上下文和明确的需求指令执行闭集自回归排序。该方法通过采用基于反事实交换的因果性项目级奖励，以及评论家引导的、不确定性感知的缩放机制来解决信用分配粗糙和反馈稀疏嘈杂的关键挑战，从而稳定学习过程。在不同推荐场景下的实验结果表明，FlexRec显著优于基线方法，在需求特定排序中，NDCG@5和Recall@5分别提升了最高59%和109.4%，在泛化设置下Recall@5也提升了最高24.1%。
Bielik-Minitron-7B: Compressing Large Language Models via Structured Pruning and Knowledge Distillation for the Polish Language
Authors: Remigiusz Kinas, Paweł Kiszczak, Sergio P. Perez, Krzysztof Ociepa, Łukasz Flis, Krzysztof Wróbel, Adrian Gwoździej
First: 2026-03-12T12:57:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T12:57:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This report details the creation of Bielik-Minitron-7B, a compressed 7.35B parameter version of the Bielik-11B-v3.0 model, specifically optimized for European languages. By leveraging a two-stage compression methodology inspired by the NVIDIA Minitron approach, we combined structured hybrid pruning and knowledge distillation to reduce the model's parameter count by 33.4%, from 11.04B to 7.35B. We utilized the NVIDIA Model Optimizer for structural pruning and the NVIDIA NeMo Framework for logit-based distillation for quality recovery. Following distillation, the model underwent a rigorous alignment pipeline consisting of Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT), Direct Preference Optimization (DPO-P), and Reinforcement Learning (GRPO). Our final model successfully recovered approximately 90% of the baseline model's performance while providing up to 50% inference speedup. This approach demonstrates an efficient pathway to create language models for less-represented languages, preserving the original model quality while reducing inference deployment costs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Bielik-Minitron-7B：通过结构化剪枝与知识蒸馏为波兰语压缩大语言模型
本报告详述了Bielik-Minitron-7B的创建过程，该模型是Bielik-11B-v3.0的压缩版本（7.35B参数），专为欧洲语言优化。借鉴NVIDIA Minitron方法的两阶段压缩策略，我们结合结构化混合剪枝与知识蒸馏，将参数量从11.04B减少至7.35B（压缩率33.4%）。采用NVIDIA Model Optimizer进行结构剪枝，并利用NVIDIA NeMo框架通过基于logit的蒸馏实现质量恢复。蒸馏后，模型经历了包含监督微调（SFT）、直接偏好优化（DPO-P）和强化学习（GRPO）的严格对齐流程。最终模型在恢复基线模型约90%性能的同时，推理速度提升最高达50%。该方法为构建低资源语言模型提供了高效路径，在降低推理部署成本的同时保持了原始模型质量。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for efficient language models for less-represented languages like Polish, this work introduces Bielik-Minitron-7B, a compressed version of the Bielik-11B model. The method employs a two-stage compression pipeline combining structured hybrid pruning via NVIDIA Model Optimizer and knowledge distillation using the NVIDIA NeMo Framework, followed by an alignment pipeline of SFT, DPO-P, and GRPO. Experimental results show the model reduces parameters by 33.4% to 7.35B, recovers about 90% of the baseline performance, and achieves up to 50% inference speedup, demonstrating a cost-effective pathway for deploying quality models.
本研究旨在为波兰语等资源较少语言开发高效语言模型，提出了Bielik-Minitron-7B，这是Bielik-11B模型的压缩版本。方法采用两阶段压缩流程，结合了基于NVIDIA Model Optimizer的结构化混合剪枝和基于NVIDIA NeMo Framework的知识蒸馏，随后通过监督微调、直接偏好优化和强化学习进行对齐。实验结果表明，模型参数量减少33.4%至7.35B，恢复了基线模型约90%的性能，并实现高达50%的推理加速，为部署高质量模型提供了一条成本效益高的路径。
An Evolutionary Algorithm with Probabilistic Annealing for Large-scale Sparse Multi-objective Optimization
Authors: Shuai Shao, Yuhao Sun, Xing Chen, Ye Tian, Guan Wang, Jin Li
First: 2026-03-12T12:48:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T12:48:49+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 4 figures, 3 tables. Preprint. Under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large-scale sparse multi-objective optimization problems (LSMOPs) are prevalent in real-world applications, where optimal solutions typically contain only a few nonzero variables, such as in adversarial attacks, critical node detection, and sparse signal reconstruction. Since the function evaluation of LSMOPs often relies on large-scale datasets involving a large number of decision variables, the search space becomes extremely high-dimensional. The coexistence of sparsity and high dimensionality greatly intensifies the conflict between exploration and exploitation, making it difficult for existing multi-objective evolutionary algorithms (MOEAs) to identify the critical nonzero decision variables within limited function evaluations. To address this challenge, this paper proposes an evolutionary algorithm with probabilistic annealing for large-scale sparse multi-objective optimization. The algorithm is driven by two probability vectors with distinct entropy characteristics: a convergence-oriented probability vector with relatively low entropy ensures stable exploitation, whereas an annealed probability vector with gradually decreasing entropy enables an adaptive transition from global exploration to local refinement. By integrating these complementary search dynamics, the proposed algorithm achieves a dynamic equilibrium between exploration and exploitation. Experimental results on benchmark problems and real-world applications demonstrate that the proposed algorithm outperforms state-of-the-art evolutionary algorithms in terms of both convergence and diversity.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大规模稀疏多目标优化的概率退火进化算法
大规模稀疏多目标优化问题在现实应用中普遍存在，其最优解通常仅包含少量非零变量，例如在对抗攻击、关键节点检测和稀疏信号重建等场景中。由于此类问题的函数评估常依赖涉及大量决策变量的大规模数据集，搜索空间变得极高维。稀疏性与高维度的并存极大加剧了探索与利用之间的冲突，使得现有多目标进化算法在有限函数评估次数内难以识别关键的非零决策变量。为应对这一挑战，本文提出一种面向大规模稀疏多目标优化的概率退火进化算法。该算法由两个具有不同熵特性的概率向量驱动：熵值相对较低、面向收敛的概率向量确保稳定利用，而熵值逐渐衰减的退火概率向量则实现从全局探索到局部细化的自适应过渡。通过整合这两种互补的搜索动态，所提算法实现了探索与利用间的动态平衡。在基准问题和实际应用中的实验结果表明，该算法在收敛性和多样性方面均优于当前最先进的进化算法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of solving large-scale sparse multi-objective optimization problems (LSMOPs), where optimal solutions have few nonzero variables, but the high-dimensional search space from many decision variables intensifies the conflict between exploration and exploitation, hindering existing multi-objective evolutionary algorithms. The authors propose an evolutionary algorithm with probabilistic annealing, which employs two probability vectors: a low-entropy vector for stable exploitation and an annealed vector with decreasing entropy to adaptively transition from global exploration to local refinement, achieving a dynamic balance. Experimental results on benchmarks and real-world applications show that the algorithm outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both convergence and diversity.
本文针对大规模稀疏多目标优化问题（LSMOPs）的求解挑战展开研究，这类问题的最优解通常仅含少量非零变量，但由于决策变量众多导致搜索空间维度极高，加剧了探索与利用之间的冲突，使现有多目标进化算法难以有效处理。作者提出了一种采用概率退火的进化算法，通过使用两个具有不同熵特性的概率向量：一个低熵向量用于稳定利用，另一个熵值逐渐降低的退火向量实现从全局探索到局部细化的自适应过渡，从而达到动态平衡。在基准问题和实际应用上的实验结果表明，该算法在收敛性和多样性方面均优于现有先进方法。
Hybrid Human-Agent Social Dilemmas in Energy Markets
Authors: Isuri Perera, Frits de Nijs, Julian Garcia
First: 2026-03-12T11:59:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T11:59:35+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 7 figures. Submitted to Proceedings of the Royal Society A, Special Issue on "The evolution of sociality in hybrid human AI populations"
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In hybrid populations where humans delegate strategic decision-making to autonomous agents, understanding when and how cooperative behaviors can emerge remains a key challenge. We study this problem in the context of energy load management: consumer agents schedule their appliance use under demand-dependent pricing. This structure can create a social dilemma where everybody would benefit from coordination, but in equilibrium agents often choose to incur the congestion costs that cooperative turn-taking would avoid. To address the problem of coordination, we introduce artificial agents that use globally observable signals to increase coordination. Using evolutionary dynamics, and reinforcement learning experiments, we show that artificial agents can shift the learning dynamics to favour coordination outcomes. An often neglected problem is partial adoption: what happens when the technology of artificial agents is in the early adoption stages? We analyze mixed populations of adopters and non-adopters, demonstrating that unilateral entry is feasible: adopters are not structurally penalized, and partial adoption can still improve aggregate outcomes. However, in some parameter regimes, non-adopters may benefit disproportionately from the cooperation induced by adopters. This asymmetry, while not precluding beneficial entry, warrants consideration in deployment, and highlights strategic issues around the adoption of AI technology in multiagent settings.
中文标题/摘要
标题：能源市场中混合人机代理的社会困境
在人类将战略决策委托给自主代理的混合群体中，理解合作行为何时及如何产生仍是一个关键挑战。本研究以能源负荷管理为背景展开探讨：消费者代理在需求依赖型定价下安排电器使用。这种结构可能形成社会困境——协调本可使各方受益，但在均衡状态下代理往往选择承担拥堵成本，而合作轮转本可避免该成本。为解决协调问题，我们引入利用全局可观测信号增强协调的人工代理。通过演化动力学和强化学习实验，我们证明人工代理能改变学习动态以促进协调结果。一个常被忽视的问题是部分采纳：当人工代理技术处于早期采纳阶段时会发生什么？我们分析采纳者与非采纳者的混合群体，证明单边进入是可行的：采纳者不会遭受结构性惩罚，部分采纳仍能改善总体结果。然而在某些参数区间，非采纳者可能从采纳者引发的合作中不成比例地获益。这种不对称性虽不阻碍有益进入，但在部署中需予以考量，并凸显了多智能体场景中AI技术采纳的战略性问题。
Summary / 总结
The study investigates how cooperative behavior can emerge in hybrid human-agent populations within energy markets, motivated by the challenge of coordination in social dilemmas where decentralized agents scheduling appliance use under dynamic pricing often lead to congestion costs. The method introduces artificial agents that utilize globally observable signals to foster coordination, employing evolutionary dynamics and reinforcement learning experiments to analyze their impact. Key experimental results show that these artificial agents can shift learning dynamics toward cooperative outcomes, and even in scenarios of partial adoption, adopters are not penalized and aggregate outcomes improve, though non-adopters may sometimes benefit disproportionately from the induced cooperation, highlighting strategic considerations for AI deployment.
本研究探讨了在能源市场的混合人机群体中如何促进合作行为，其动机源于协调社会困境的挑战，即在动态定价下分散代理调度电器使用常导致拥堵成本。方法引入了利用全局可观测信号的人工代理以增强协调，通过进化动力学和强化学习实验分析其影响。主要实验结果表明，这些人工代理能够将学习动态转向合作结果，即使在部分采用场景中，采用者不会受到结构性惩罚且总体结果有所改善，但非采用者有时可能从诱导的合作中不成比例地获益，这凸显了AI部署中的战略考量。
MedEyes: Learning Dynamic Visual Focus for Medical Progressive Diagnosis
Authors: Chunzheng Zhu, Yangfang Lin, Shen Chen, Yijun Wang, Jianxin Lin
Venue: AAAI 2026
First: 2025-11-27T01:47:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T11:42:07+00:00
Comments: AAAI 2026, Medical Chain-of-Thought (CoT), Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), Multimodal Grounded Reasoning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Accurate medical diagnosis often involves progressive visual focusing and iterative reasoning, characteristics commonly observed in clinical workflows. While recent vision-language models demonstrate promising chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning capabilities via reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), their purely on-policy learning paradigm tends to reinforce superficially coherent but clinically inaccurate reasoning paths. We propose MedEyes, a novel reinforcement learning framework that dynamically models clinician-style diagnostic reasoning by progressively attending to and interpreting relevant medical image regions. By incorporating off-policy expert guidance, MedEyes converts expert visual search trajectories into structured external behavioral signals, guiding the model toward clinically aligned visual reasoning. We design the Gaze-guided Reasoning Navigator (GRN) to emulate the diagnostic process through a dual-mode exploration strategy, scanning for systematic abnormality localization and drilling for detailed regional analysis. To balance expert imitation and autonomous discovery, we introduce the Confidence Value Sampler (CVS), which employs nucleus sampling and adaptive termination to create diverse yet credible exploration paths. Finally, the dual-stream GRPO optimization framework decouples on-policy and off-policy learning signals, mitigating reward assimilation and entropy collapse. Experiments demonstrate that MedEyes achieves an average performance improvement of +8.5pp across multiple medical VQA benchmarks, validating MedEyes's potential in building trustworthy medical AI systems. Code is available at https://github.com/zhcz328/MedEyes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MedEyes：面向医学渐进式诊断的动态视觉焦点学习
准确的医学诊断通常涉及渐进式视觉聚焦与迭代推理，这是临床工作流的常见特征。尽管近期视觉语言模型通过可验证奖励的强化学习展现出有前景的思维链推理能力，但其纯在线策略学习范式容易强化表面连贯但临床不准确的推理路径。我们提出MedEyes——一种新颖的强化学习框架，通过渐进关注并解读相关医学图像区域，动态模拟临床医生风格的诊断推理。通过融入离线策略专家指导，MedEyes将专家视觉搜索轨迹转化为结构化外部行为信号，引导模型实现临床对齐的视觉推理。我们设计凝视引导推理导航器，通过双模探索策略模拟诊断过程：系统性异常定位扫描与精细化区域分析钻取。为平衡专家模仿与自主发现，我们引入置信度值采样器，采用核心采样与自适应终止机制生成多样且可信的探索路径。最终，双流GRPO优化框架解耦在线与离线策略学习信号，缓解奖励同化与熵崩溃问题。实验表明MedEyes在多个医学视觉问答基准上平均性能提升+8.5个百分点，验证了其在构建可信赖医学人工智能系统方面的潜力。代码发布于https://github.com/zhcz328/MedEyes。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to emulate the progressive visual focusing and iterative reasoning of clinical diagnosis, which existing vision-language models often fail to achieve due to on-policy learning reinforcing superficially coherent but inaccurate paths, this paper introduces MedEyes, a reinforcement learning framework that dynamically models clinician-style diagnostic reasoning. The method incorporates off-policy expert guidance to convert expert visual search trajectories into behavioral signals, using a Gaze-guided Reasoning Navigator for dual-mode exploration (scanning and drilling) and a Confidence Value Sampler for balanced imitation and discovery, optimized via a dual-stream GRPO framework to decouple learning signals. Experimental results show an average performance improvement of +8.5 percentage points across multiple medical VQA benchmarks, validating its effectiveness for trustworthy medical AI.
本文的动机是模拟临床诊断中渐进式视觉聚焦和迭代推理的过程，现有视觉语言模型常因在线学习强化表面连贯但不准确的路径而难以实现。为此，提出MedEyes强化学习框架，动态建模临床医生风格的诊断推理。方法融合离线专家指导，将专家视觉搜索轨迹转化为行为信号，采用凝视引导推理导航器进行双模式探索（扫描和钻取），并通过置信值采样器平衡模仿与自主发现，利用双流GRPO优化框架解耦学习信号。实验结果表明，在多个医疗视觉问答基准上平均性能提升8.5个百分点，验证了其在构建可信医疗AI系统方面的潜力。
RetroAgent: From Solving to Evolving via Retrospective Dual Intrinsic Feedback
Authors: Xiaoying Zhang, Zichen Liu, Yipeng Zhang, Xia Hu, Wenqi Shao
First: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T11:31:58+00:00
Comments: 45 pages, update the abstract and introduction
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Standard reinforcement learning (RL) for large language model (LLM)-based agents typically optimizes extrinsic task-success rewards, prioritizing one-off task solving over continual adaptation. As a result, agents may converge to suboptimal policies due to limited exploration, and accumulated experience remains implicitly stored in model parameters, hindering efficient experiential learning. Inspired by humans' capacity for retrospective self-improvement, we introduce RetroAgent, an online RL framework that enables agents to master complex interactive environments not only by solving, but also by evolving under the joint guidance of extrinsic task-success rewards and retrospective dual intrinsic feedback. Concretely, RetroAgent features a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that produces: (1) intrinsic numerical feedback, which tracks incremental subtask completion relative to prior attempts to reward promising exploration; and (2) intrinsic language feedback, which distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer retrieved via our proposed Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound (SimUtil-UCB) strategy, jointly balancing relevance, utility, and exploration. Extensive experiments across four challenging agentic tasks show that RetroAgent achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance, substantially outperforming RL fine-tuning, memory-augmented RL, exploration-guided RL, and meta-RL methods -- e.g., exceeding Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)-trained agents by +18.3% on ALFWorld, +15.4% on WebShop, +27.1% on Sokoban, and +8.9% on MineSweeper -- while maintaining strong test-time adaptation and out-of-distribution generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RetroAgent：通过回顾式双重内在反馈实现从解决到进化的跨越
基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体在标准强化学习（RL）中通常优化外在任务成功奖励，优先考虑一次性任务解决而非持续适应。这导致智能体可能因探索有限而收敛至次优策略，且累积经验仅隐式存储于模型参数中，阻碍高效经验学习。受人类回顾式自我改进能力启发，我们提出RetroAgent——一种在线RL框架，使智能体不仅能通过解决任务，还能在外在任务成功奖励与回顾式双重内在反馈的共同指导下实现进化，从而掌握复杂交互环境。具体而言，RetroAgent具备事后自我反思机制，可生成：（1）内在数值反馈：追踪相对于先前尝试的增量子任务完成度，以奖励有前景的探索；（2）内在语言反馈：将可复用经验提炼至记忆缓冲区，并通过我们提出的相似性与效用感知上置信界（SimUtil-UCB）策略进行检索，协同平衡相关性、效用与探索。在四项挑战性智能体任务上的大量实验表明，RetroAgent实现了最先进（SOTA）性能，显著优于RL微调、记忆增强RL、探索引导RL及元RL方法——例如在ALFWorld上超越GRPO训练智能体+18.3%，WebShop上+15.4%，Sokoban上+27.1%，MineSweeper上+8.9%——同时保持强大的测试时适应性与分布外泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning (RL) for large language model agents, which focuses on extrinsic task rewards and lacks mechanisms for continual adaptation and efficient experiential learning, this paper introduces RetroAgent, an online RL framework that integrates retrospective dual intrinsic feedback. The method employs a hindsight self-reflection mechanism generating both intrinsic numerical feedback to reward incremental subtask progress and intrinsic language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, retrieved via a novel Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound strategy to balance relevance, utility, and exploration. Experimental results across four challenging agentic tasks demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, with substantial improvements over baseline methods, such as exceeding Group Relative Policy Optimization by +18.3% on ALFWorld and +27.1% on Sokoban, while also showing strong test-time adaptation and out-of-distribution generalization.
本文的动机在于标准强化学习针对大语言模型智能体时，通常优化外在任务成功奖励，侧重于一次性任务解决而缺乏持续适应能力，导致策略收敛至次优且经验隐式存储于模型参数中，阻碍高效经验学习。为此，研究提出RetroAgent这一在线强化学习框架，通过回顾性双重内在反馈使智能体在复杂交互环境中不仅解决任务还能持续进化，其方法采用事后自我反思机制，产生内在数值反馈以奖励增量子任务完成度，以及内在语言反馈将可重用经验提炼至记忆缓冲区，并通过提出的相似性与效用感知上置信界策略进行检索，平衡相关性、效用和探索。在四项挑战性智能体任务上的实验结果表明，该方法实现了最先进的性能，大幅超越基线方法，如在ALFWorld上超过组相对策略优化18.3%，在Sokoban上超过27.1%，同时保持了强大的测试时适应和分布外泛化能力。
Exploiting Expertise of Non-Expert and Diverse Agents in Social Bandit Learning: A Free Energy Approach
Authors: Erfan Mirzaei, Seyed Pooya Shariatpanahi, Alireza Tavakoli, Reshad Hosseini, Majid Nili Ahmadabadi
First: 2026-03-12T10:04:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:04:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Personalized AI-based services involve a population of individual reinforcement learning agents. However, most reinforcement learning algorithms focus on harnessing individual learning and fail to leverage the social learning capabilities commonly exhibited by humans and animals. Social learning integrates individual experience with observing others' behavior, presenting opportunities for improved learning outcomes. In this study, we focus on a social bandit learning scenario where a social agent observes other agents' actions without knowledge of their rewards. The agents independently pursue their own policy without explicit motivation to teach each other. We propose a free energy-based social bandit learning algorithm over the policy space, where the social agent evaluates others' expertise levels without resorting to any oracle or social norms. Accordingly, the social agent integrates its direct experiences in the environment and others' estimated policies. The theoretical convergence of our algorithm to the optimal policy is proven. Empirical evaluations validate the superiority of our social learning method over alternative approaches in various scenarios. Our algorithm strategically identifies the relevant agents, even in the presence of random or suboptimal agents, and skillfully exploits their behavioral information. In addition to societies including expert agents, in the presence of relevant but non-expert agents, our algorithm significantly enhances individual learning performance, where most related methods fail. Importantly, it also maintains logarithmic regret.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用非专家与多样化智能体在社交多臂赌博机学习中的专长：一种自由能方法
个性化AI服务依赖于个体强化学习智能体群体。然而，多数强化学习算法侧重于个体学习，未能充分利用人类与动物常见的社交学习能力。社交学习将个体经验与观察他人行为相结合，为提升学习效果提供了可能。本研究聚焦于社交多臂赌博机学习场景，其中社交智能体可观察其他智能体的行为，但无法获知其奖励。各智能体独立执行自身策略，无明确相互指导动机。我们提出一种基于自由能的策略空间社交多臂赌博机学习算法，使社交智能体无需依赖任何先知或社会规范即可评估其他智能体的专业水平。据此，社交智能体整合其在环境中的直接经验与其他智能体的估计策略。理论分析证明该算法能收敛至最优策略。实证评估验证了本社交学习方法在多种场景中优于其他方案。即使在存在随机或次优智能体的情况下，本算法仍能策略性地识别相关智能体并有效利用其行为信息。除包含专家智能体的群体外，在面对相关但非专家的智能体时，本算法显著提升个体学习性能（多数相关方法在此情况下失效），并保持对数级遗憾。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to enhance personalized AI services by enabling social learning among reinforcement learning agents, moving beyond individual-focused algorithms to mimic the social learning observed in humans and animals. The method proposes a free energy-based social bandit learning algorithm where a social agent observes others' actions without reward knowledge, estimates their expertise levels without external guidance, and integrates this with its own direct experiences to update its policy. Experimental results demonstrate the algorithm's convergence to optimal policy, superiority over alternatives in diverse scenarios, effective identification of relevant agents despite random or suboptimal ones, significant performance gains even with non-expert agents, and maintenance of logarithmic regret.
该研究的动机是通过在强化学习智能体中实现社会学习来增强个性化AI服务，超越仅关注个体学习的算法，模仿人类和动物中常见的社会学习能力。方法上提出了一种基于自由能的社会赌博学习算法，其中社会智能体在不知晓奖励的情况下观察其他智能体的行为，无需外部指导即可评估其专业水平，并将此与自身直接经验结合以更新策略。实验结果表明，该算法能收敛至最优策略，在多种场景中优于其他方法，有效识别相关智能体（即使存在随机或次优智能体），在包含非专家智能体时显著提升个体学习性能，并保持对数遗憾。
Stein Variational Evolution Strategies
Authors: Cornelius V. Braun, Robert T. Lange, Marc Toussaint
Venue: Proceedings of the Forty-first Conference on Uncertainty in Artificial Intelligence, PMLR 286:398-420, 2025
First: 2024-10-14T11:24:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T10:02:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Stein Variational Gradient Descent (SVGD) is a highly efficient method to sample from an unnormalized probability distribution. However, the SVGD update relies on gradients of the log-density, which may not always be available. Existing gradient-free versions of SVGD make use of simple Monte Carlo approximations or gradients from surrogate distributions, both with limitations. To improve gradient-free Stein variational inference, we combine SVGD steps with evolution strategy (ES) updates. Our results demonstrate that the resulting algorithm generates high-quality samples from unnormalized target densities without requiring gradient information. Compared to prior gradient-free SVGD methods, we find that the integration of the ES update in SVGD significantly improves the performance on multiple challenging benchmark problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：斯坦因变分进化策略
斯坦因变分梯度下降（SVGD）是一种从非归一化概率分布中采样的高效方法。然而，SVGD更新依赖于对数密度的梯度，而该梯度可能并非总是可获取。现有的无梯度SVGD版本采用简单的蒙特卡洛近似或替代分布的梯度，两者均存在局限性。为改进无梯度斯坦因变分推断，我们将SVGD步骤与进化策略（ES）更新相结合。实验结果表明，所提出的算法无需梯度信息即可从非归一化目标密度中生成高质量样本。与先前的无梯度SVGD方法相比，SVGD中集成ES更新显著提升了在多个具有挑战性的基准问题上的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of Stein Variational Gradient Descent (SVGD), which requires gradient information that is often unavailable, by proposing a gradient-free alternative. The method integrates SVGD with evolution strategy (ES) updates to circumvent the need for direct log-density gradients, overcoming the drawbacks of prior approximations like Monte Carlo or surrogate gradients. Experimental results on challenging benchmarks show that this hybrid approach generates high-quality samples from unnormalized target densities and significantly outperforms existing gradient-free SVGD methods.
本文针对Stein变分梯度下降（SVGD）需要梯度信息而该信息常不可得的局限，提出了一种无需梯度的替代方法。该方法将SVGD与进化策略（ES）更新相结合，避免了直接使用对数密度梯度，克服了先前基于蒙特卡洛或代理梯度等近似方法的不足。在多个具有挑战性的基准问题上的实验结果表明，这种混合方法能从非归一化目标密度中生成高质量样本，且性能显著优于现有的无需梯度SVGD方法。
Reasoning Boosts Opinion Alignment in LLMs
Authors: Frédéric Berdoz, Yann Billeter, Yann Vonlanthen, Roger Wattenhofer
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-01T18:19:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T09:18:20+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Opinion modeling aims to capture individual or group political preferences, enabling applications such as digital democracies, where models could help shape fairer and more popular policies. Given their versatility, strong generalization capabilities, and demonstrated success across diverse text-to-text applications, large language models (LLMs) are natural candidates for this task. However, due to their statistical nature and limited causal understanding, they tend to produce biased opinions when prompted naively. In this work, we study whether reasoning can improve opinion alignment. Motivated by the recent advancement in mathematical reasoning enabled by reinforcement learning (RL), we train models to produce profile-consistent answers through structured reasoning. We evaluate our approach on three datasets covering U.S., European, and Swiss politics. Results indicate that reasoning enhances opinion modeling and is competitive with strong baselines, but does not fully remove bias, highlighting the need for additional mechanisms to build faithful political digital twins using LLMs. By releasing both our method and datasets, we establish a solid baseline to support future research on LLM opinion alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理能力提升大语言模型中的观点对齐
观点建模旨在捕捉个体或群体的政治偏好，支持数字民主等应用场景，使模型能够协助制定更公平、更受欢迎的政策。鉴于大语言模型（LLMs）的多功能性、强大的泛化能力以及在多样化文本生成任务中的成功表现，它们自然成为此项任务的理想候选。然而，由于其统计本质和有限的因果理解能力，当被简单提示时，它们往往会产生带有偏见的观点。本研究探讨推理能否改善观点对齐。受近期强化学习推动数学推理进展的启发，我们训练模型通过结构化推理生成与用户画像一致的答案。我们在涵盖美国、欧洲和瑞士政治的三个数据集上评估了该方法。结果表明，推理能有效提升观点建模性能，并与强基线模型表现相当，但未能完全消除偏见，这凸显了需要额外机制来构建基于LLMs的忠实政治数字孪生。通过公开我们的方法和数据集，我们为未来LLM观点对齐研究建立了坚实的基线。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether structured reasoning can improve the alignment of large language models (LLMs) with specific political opinions, addressing the issue that naively prompted LLMs often produce biased outputs due to their statistical nature. Motivated by advances in reinforcement learning for mathematical reasoning, the method trains models to generate profile-consistent answers through structured reasoning processes. Experimental evaluation on three political datasets covering U.S., European, and Swiss politics shows that reasoning enhances opinion modeling performance and competes with strong baselines, though it does not fully eliminate bias, indicating a need for further mechanisms to develop faithful political digital twins.
本研究探讨结构化推理是否能提升大语言模型与特定政治观点的一致性，以解决模型因统计特性而在简单提示下常产生偏见的问题。受强化学习在数学推理中进展的启发，该方法通过结构化推理训练模型生成与人物档案一致的答案。在美国、欧洲和瑞士政治的三个数据集上的实验结果表明，推理能提升观点建模性能并与强基线竞争，但未能完全消除偏见，这凸显了需要额外机制来构建可信的政治数字孪生模型。
STAIRS-Former: Spatio-Temporal Attention with Interleaved Recursive Structure Transformer for Offline Multi-task Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiwon Jeon, Myungsik Cho, Youngchul Sung
First: 2026-03-12T08:56:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T08:56:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) with multi-task datasets is challenging due to varying numbers of agents across tasks and the need to generalize to unseen scenarios. Prior works employ transformers with observation tokenization and hierarchical skill learning to address these issues. However, they underutilize the transformer attention mechanism for inter-agent coordination and rely on a single history token, which limits their ability to capture long-horizon temporal dependencies in partially observable MARL settings. In this paper, we propose STAIRS-Former, a transformer architecture augmented with spatial and temporal hierarchies that enables effective attention over critical tokens while capturing long interaction histories. We further introduce token dropout to enhance robustness and generalization across varying agent populations. Extensive experiments on diverse multi-agent benchmarks, including SMAC, SMAC-v2, MPE, and MaMuJoCo, with multi-task datasets demonstrate that STAIRS-Former consistently outperforms prior methods and achieves new state-of-the-art performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：STAIRS-Former：面向离线多任务多智能体强化学习的时空注意力与交错递归结构Transformer
离线多任务多智能体强化学习（MARL）面临跨任务智能体数量变化及需泛化至未见场景的挑战。先前研究采用基于观测标记化与分层技能学习的Transformer应对，但其未充分利用注意力机制实现智能体间协调，且依赖单一历史标记，限制了在部分可观测MARL中捕捉长期时序依赖的能力。本文提出STAIRS-Former，一种增强时空层次结构的Transformer架构，能对关键标记实现高效注意力并捕获长程交互历史。我们进一步引入标记丢弃策略以提升对动态智能体群体的鲁棒性与泛化能力。在包含SMAC、SMAC-v2、MPE及MaMuJoCo的多智能体基准测试中，基于多任务数据集的实验表明，STAIRS-Former持续超越现有方法并达到新的最优性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenges in offline multi-agent reinforcement learning with multi-task datasets, where varying agent numbers and the need for generalization to unseen scenarios complicate learning. The proposed STAIRS-Former method enhances transformer architecture by incorporating spatio-temporal attention hierarchies and interleaved recursive structures, enabling better inter-agent coordination and capture of long-term temporal dependencies in partially observable settings, alongside token dropout for improved robustness. Experimental results on benchmarks like SMAC, SMAC-v2, MPE, and MaMuJoCo show that STAIRS-Former consistently outperforms prior methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance.
本文针对离线多智能体强化学习在多任务数据集中的挑战，即智能体数量变化和需泛化至未见场景的问题。提出的STAIRS-Former方法通过增强Transformer架构，引入时空注意力层次和交错递归结构，以改善智能体间协调并捕捉部分可观测环境中的长期时间依赖，同时使用令牌丢弃提升鲁棒性。在SMAC、SMAC-v2、MPE和MaMuJoCo等基准上的实验结果表明，STAIRS-Former持续优于现有方法，实现了最先进的性能。
Entropy-Preserving Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Aleksei Petrenko, Ben Lipkin, Kevin Chen, Erik Wijmans, Marco Cusumano-Towner, Raja Giryes, Philipp Krähenbühl
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-12T08:47:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T08:47:40+00:00
Comments: Published at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy gradient algorithms have driven many recent advancements in language model reasoning. An appealing property is their ability to learn from exploration on their own trajectories, a process crucial for fostering diverse and creative solutions. As we show in this paper, many policy gradient algorithms naturally reduce the entropy -- and thus the diversity of explored trajectories -- as part of training, yielding a policy increasingly limited in its ability to explore. In this paper, we argue that entropy should be actively monitored and controlled throughout training. We formally analyze the contributions of leading policy gradient objectives on entropy dynamics, identify empirical factors (such as numerical precision) that significantly impact entropy behavior, and propose explicit mechanisms for entropy control. These include REPO, a family of algorithms that modify the advantage function to regulate entropy, and ADAPO, an adaptive asymmetric clipping approach. Models trained with our entropy-preserving methods maintain diversity throughout training, yielding final policies that are more performant and retain their trainability for sequential learning in new environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：熵保持强化学习
策略梯度算法推动了语言模型推理领域的许多最新进展。其吸引人的特性在于能够从自身轨迹的探索中学习，这一过程对促进多样化和创造性解决方案至关重要。本文指出，许多策略梯度算法在训练过程中会自然降低熵——从而减少探索轨迹的多样性——导致策略的探索能力逐渐受限。我们认为，应在整个训练过程中主动监测并控制熵。我们形式化分析了主流策略梯度目标对熵动态的贡献，识别出显著影响熵行为的实证因素（如数值精度），并提出明确的熵控制机制。这些机制包括REPO（通过修改优势函数调节熵的算法族）和ADAPO（自适应非对称截断方法）。采用我们熵保持方法训练的模型能在整个训练过程中保持多样性，最终得到性能更优的策略，并保留在新环境中进行序列学习的可训练性。

The paper is motivated by the observation that standard policy gradient algorithms, while successful in language model reasoning, often reduce entropy and thus the diversity of explored trajectories during training, limiting the policy's exploratory capacity. To address this, the authors propose actively monitoring and controlling entropy by analyzing entropy dynamics in policy gradient objectives and identifying empirical factors like numerical precision that affect entropy. They introduce explicit control mechanisms, including REPO algorithms that adjust the advantage function and ADAPO, an adaptive asymmetric clipping method. Experimental results show that models trained with these entropy-preserving methods maintain diversity throughout training, leading to more performant final policies and better trainability for sequential learning in new environments.
本文的动机是观察到标准策略梯度算法虽然在语言模型推理中取得成功，但常在训练过程中降低熵从而减少探索轨迹的多样性，限制了策略的探索能力。为解决此问题，作者提出主动监控和控制熵，通过分析策略梯度目标中的熵动态并识别如数值精度等影响熵的经验因素。他们引入了明确的控制机制，包括调整优势函数的REPO算法和自适应非对称裁剪方法ADAPO。实验结果表明，使用这些保熵方法训练的模型在训练全程保持多样性，最终策略性能更优，并在新环境中具有更好的顺序学习可训练性。
Simple Recipe Works: Vision-Language-Action Models are Natural Continual Learners with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiaheng Hu, Jay Shim, Chen Tang, Yoonchang Sung, Bo Liu, Peter Stone, Roberto Martin-Martin
First: 2026-03-12T08:22:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T08:22:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Continual Reinforcement Learning (CRL) for Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models is a promising direction toward self-improving embodied agents that can adapt in openended, evolving environments. However, conventional wisdom from continual learning suggests that naive Sequential Fine-Tuning (Seq. FT) leads to catastrophic forgetting, necessitating complex CRL strategies. In this work, we take a step back and conduct a systematic study of CRL for large pretrained VLAs across three models and five challenging lifelong RL benchmarks. We find that, contrary to established belief, simple Seq. FT with low-rank adaptation (LoRA) is remarkably strong: it achieves high plasticity, exhibits little to no forgetting, and retains strong zero-shot generalization, frequently outperforming more sophisticated CRL methods. Through detailed analysis, we show that this robustness arises from a synergy between the large pretrained model, parameter-efficient adaptation, and on-policy RL. Together, these components reshape the stability-plasticity trade-off, making continual adaptation both stable and scalable. Our results position Sequential Fine-Tuning as a powerful method for continual RL with VLAs and provide new insights into lifelong learning in the large model era. Code is available at github.com/UT-Austin-RobIn/continual-vla-rl.
中文标题/摘要
标题：简单方法有效：视觉-语言-动作模型通过强化学习实现自然持续学习
视觉-语言-动作模型的持续强化学习是实现能在开放动态环境中自我改进的具身智能体的重要方向。传统持续学习观点认为，简单的顺序微调会导致灾难性遗忘，需要复杂的持续强化学习策略。本研究通过系统评估三种预训练大模型在五个终身强化学习基准上的表现，发现采用低秩适配的顺序微调方法具有显著优势：它展现出高可塑性、几乎无遗忘现象，并保持强大的零样本泛化能力，其表现常优于复杂方法。深入分析表明，这种鲁棒性源于大规模预训练模型、参数高效适配与在线强化学习的协同作用，重构了稳定性与可塑性的平衡机制，使持续适应兼具稳定性与可扩展性。本研究确立了顺序微调作为视觉-语言-动作模型持续强化学习的有效方法，为大规模模型时代的终身学习提供了新见解。代码发布于github.com/UT-Austin-RobIn/continual-vla-rl。

This paper challenges the conventional wisdom in continual reinforcement learning (CRL) for vision-language-action (VLA) models, which holds that naive sequential fine-tuning leads to catastrophic forgetting. The authors systematically evaluate CRL across several models and benchmarks, finding that simple sequential fine-tuning combined with low-rank adaptation (LoRA) is surprisingly robust, achieving high plasticity with minimal forgetting and strong zero-shot generalization, often outperforming more complex CRL methods. They attribute this success to a synergy between the large pretrained model, parameter-efficient adaptation, and on-policy RL, which reshapes the stability-plasticity trade-off, positioning sequential fine-tuning as a powerful and scalable approach for continual learning with VLAs.
本文对视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型的持续强化学习（CRL）中的传统观点提出了挑战，该观点认为简单的顺序微调会导致灾难性遗忘。作者在多个模型和基准上系统评估了CRL，发现结合低秩适应（LoRA）的顺序微调方法异常鲁棒，能实现高可塑性、几乎无遗忘，并保持强大的零样本泛化能力，常常优于更复杂的CRL方法。他们将此成功归因于大型预训练模型、参数高效适应和在线策略强化学习之间的协同作用，这重塑了稳定性与可塑性之间的权衡，从而将顺序微调确立为VLA持续学习的一种强大且可扩展的方法。
Enhancing Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Cooperation in Decentralized MARL via GNN-driven Intrinsic Rewards
Authors: Jahir Sadik Monon, Deeparghya Dutta Barua, Md. Mosaddek Khan
Venue: Proceedings of the 24th International Conference on Autonomous Agents and Multiagent Systems (AAMAS 2025), pages 2681-2683, 2025
First: 2024-08-12T21:38:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T07:05:45+00:00
Comments: Full paper version for AAMAS 2025 (https://ifaamas.org/Proceedings/aamas2025/pdfs/p2681.pdf), 9 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) is emerging as a key framework for various sequential decision-making and control tasks. Unlike their single-agent counterparts, multi-agent systems necessitate successful cooperation among the agents. The deployment of these systems in real-world scenarios often requires decentralized training, a diverse set of agents, and learning from infrequent environmental reward signals. These challenges become more pronounced under partial observability and the lack of prior knowledge about agent heterogeneity. While notable studies use intrinsic motivation (IM) to address reward sparsity or cooperation in decentralized settings, those dealing with heterogeneity typically assume centralized training, parameter sharing, and agent indexing. To overcome these limitations, we propose the CoHet algorithm, which utilizes a novel Graph Neural Network (GNN) based intrinsic motivation to facilitate the learning of heterogeneous agent policies in decentralized settings, under the challenges of partial observability and reward sparsity. Evaluation of CoHet in the Multi-agent Particle Environment (MPE) and Vectorized Multi-Agent Simulator (VMAS) benchmarks demonstrates superior performance compared to the state-of-the-art in a range of cooperative multi-agent scenarios. Our research is supplemented by an analysis of the impact of the agent dynamics model on the intrinsic motivation module, insights into the performance of different CoHet variants, and its robustness to an increasing number of heterogeneous agents.

标题：基于图神经网络内在奖励增强去中心化多智能体强化学习中的异构协作
多智能体强化学习（MARL）正成为各类序贯决策与控制任务的关键框架。与单智能体系统不同，多智能体系统需实现智能体间的有效协作。在实际应用中，这类系统常需进行去中心化训练、容纳多样化的智能体，并从稀疏的环境奖励信号中学习。在部分可观测性及缺乏智能体异构先验知识的条件下，这些挑战尤为突出。现有研究虽利用内在动机（IM）应对奖励稀疏性或去中心化协作问题，但针对异构性的方法通常假设集中式训练、参数共享和智能体索引。为突破这些限制，我们提出CoHet算法，该算法基于新型图神经网络（GNN）内在动机，在部分可观测和奖励稀疏的挑战下，促进去中心化环境中异构智能体策略的学习。在Multi-agent Particle Environment（MPE）和Vectorized Multi-Agent Simulator（VMAS）基准测试中，CoHet在一系列协作多智能体场景中展现出优于现有技术的性能。本研究进一步分析了智能体动力学模型对内在动机模块的影响，探讨了不同CoHet变体的性能表现，并验证了其对增长异构智能体数量的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of fostering cooperation among heterogeneous agents in decentralized multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) under conditions of partial observability and sparse environmental rewards. The proposed method, CoHet, introduces a novel intrinsic motivation mechanism driven by a Graph Neural Network (GNN) to guide the learning of distinct agent policies without relying on centralized training, parameter sharing, or agent indexing. Experimental results on MPE and VMAS benchmarks show that CoHet outperforms state-of-the-art methods across various cooperative scenarios, with additional analysis confirming its robustness to increasing agent heterogeneity and providing insights into model variants.

Hybrid Energy-Aware Reward Shaping: A Unified Lightweight Physics-Guided Methodology for Policy Optimization
Authors: Qijun Liao, Jue Yang, Yiting Kang, Xinxin Zhao, Yong Zhang, Mingan Zhao
First: 2026-03-12T06:47:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T06:47:01+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 27 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning excels in continuous control but often requires extensive exploration, while physics-based models demand complete equations and suffer cubic complexity. This study proposes Hybrid Energy-Aware Reward Shaping (H-EARS), unifying potential-based reward shaping with energy-aware action regularization. H-EARS constrains action magnitude while balancing task-specific and energy-based potentials via functional decomposition, achieving linear complexity O(n) by capturing dominant energy components without full dynamics. We establish a theoretical foundation including: (1) functional independence for separate task/energy optimization; (2) energy-based convergence acceleration; (3) convergence guarantees under function approximation; and (4) approximate potential error bounds. Lyapunov stability connections are analyzed as heuristic guides. Experiments across baselines show improved convergence, stability, and energy efficiency. Vehicle simulations validate applicability in safety-critical domains under extreme conditions. Results confirm that integrating lightweight physics priors enhances model-free RL without complete system models, enabling transfer from lab research to industrial applications.

标题：混合能量感知奖励塑形：一种用于策略优化的统一轻量级物理引导方法
深度强化学习在连续控制任务中表现出色，但通常需要大量探索；而基于物理的模型需要完整方程且存在立方复杂度问题。本研究提出混合能量感知奖励塑形方法，将基于势能的奖励塑形与能量感知动作正则化相统一。该方法通过功能分解约束动作幅度，同时平衡任务特定势能与能量势能，仅捕获主导能量分量而无需完整动力学模型，实现线性复杂度O(n)。我们建立了理论基础，包括：(1) 任务与能量优化的功能独立性；(2) 基于能量的收敛加速；(3) 函数逼近下的收敛保证；(4) 近似势能误差界。李雅普诺夫稳定性关联被分析为启发式指导。多基线实验显示其在收敛性、稳定性和能量效率方面的改进。车辆仿真验证了该方法在极端条件下安全关键领域的适用性。结果表明，集成轻量级物理先验可在无需完整系统模型的情况下增强无模型强化学习，推动从实验室研究到工业应用的迁移。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high exploration cost of deep reinforcement learning and the impracticality of full physics models, this paper proposes Hybrid Energy-Aware Reward Shaping (H-EARS), a unified method that combines potential-based reward shaping with energy-aware action regularization. The method functionally decomposes the reward to balance task and energy objectives, achieving linear complexity by focusing on dominant energy components without requiring complete system dynamics. Experimental results across benchmarks demonstrate improved convergence, stability, and energy efficiency, with vehicle simulations validating its applicability in safety-critical scenarios, confirming that lightweight physics priors can enhance model-free RL for industrial transfer.
针对深度强化学习探索成本高以及完整物理模型不实用的问题，本研究提出了混合能量感知奖励塑形（H-EARS），这是一种将基于势能的奖励塑形与能量感知动作正则化相统一的轻量级方法。该方法通过功能分解平衡任务与能量目标，仅捕捉主导能量成分而无需完整系统动力学，实现了线性复杂度。在多个基准测试中的实验结果表明，该方法提升了收敛性、稳定性和能量效率，车辆仿真验证了其在安全关键场景下的适用性，证实了轻量级物理先验能够增强无模型强化学习，并促进其向工业应用迁移。
Randomized Kriging Believer for Parallel Bayesian Optimization with Regret Bounds
Authors: Shuhei Sugiura, Ichiro Takeuchi, Shion Takeno
First: 2026-03-02T05:32:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T06:20:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider an optimization problem of an expensive-to-evaluate black-box function, in which we can obtain noisy function values in parallel. For this problem, parallel Bayesian optimization (PBO) is a promising approach, which aims to optimize with fewer function evaluations by selecting a diverse input set for parallel evaluation. However, existing PBO methods suffer from poor practical performance or lack theoretical guarantees. In this study, we propose a PBO method, called randomized kriging believer (KB), based on a well-known KB heuristic and inheriting the advantages of the original KB: low computational complexity, a simple implementation, versatility across various BO methods, and applicability to asynchronous parallelization. Furthermore, we show that our randomized KB achieves Bayesian expected regret guarantees. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method through experiments on synthetic and benchmark functions and emulators of real-world data.

标题：具有遗憾界保证的并行贝叶斯优化随机克里金置信方法
本文研究一个评估成本高昂的黑箱函数优化问题，其中可并行获取带噪声的函数值。针对此问题，并行贝叶斯优化（PBO）是一种前景广阔的方法，其通过选择多样化的输入集进行并行评估，旨在以更少的函数评估次数实现优化。然而，现有PBO方法存在实际性能不佳或缺乏理论保证的局限。本研究提出一种基于经典克里金置信启发式策略的PBO方法——随机克里金置信法，该方法继承了原始克里金置信策略的优势：计算复杂度低、实现简单、可适配多种贝叶斯优化方法，并适用于异步并行场景。此外，我们证明随机克里金置信法能够实现贝叶斯期望遗憾的理论保证。通过合成函数、基准函数以及真实数据仿真器的实验，验证了所提方法的有效性。

Experimental results on synthetic functions, benchmarks, and real-world data emulators demonstrate its effectiveness, while theoretical analysis confirms it achieves Bayesian expected regret bounds.

Diffusion Blend: Inference-Time Multi-Preference Alignment for Diffusion Models
Authors: Min Cheng, Fatemeh Doudi, Dileep Kalathil, Mohammad Ghavamzadeh, Panganamala R. Kumar
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-24T06:27:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T06:09:47+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms have been used recently to align diffusion models with downstream objectives such as aesthetic quality and text-image consistency by fine-tuning them to maximize a single reward function under a fixed KL regularization. However, this approach is inherently restrictive in practice, where alignment must balance multiple, often conflicting objectives. Moreover, user preferences vary across prompts, individuals, and deployment contexts, with varying tolerances for deviation from a pre-trained base model. We address the problem of inference-time multi-preference alignment: given a set of basis reward functions and a reference KL regularization strength, can we design a fine-tuning procedure so that, at inference time, it can generate images aligned with any user-specified linear combination of rewards and regularization, without requiring additional fine-tuning? We propose Diffusion Blend, a novel approach to solve inference-time multi-preference alignment by blending backward diffusion processes associated with fine-tuned models, and we instantiate this approach with two algorithms: DB-MPA for multi-reward alignment and DB-KLA for KL regularization control. Extensive experiments show that Diffusion Blend algorithms consistently outperform relevant baselines and closely match or exceed the performance of individually fine-tuned models, enabling efficient, user-driven alignment at inference-time. The code is available at https://github.com/bluewoods127/DB-2025.
中文标题/摘要
标题：扩散融合：扩散模型的推理时多偏好对齐
近期强化学习算法通过微调扩散模型以最大化单一奖励函数（在固定KL正则化下），实现了与下游目标（如美学质量、图文一致性）的对齐。然而实践中常需平衡多个可能冲突的目标，且用户偏好随提示词、个体及部署环境变化，对预训练基模型的偏离容忍度也不同。本文研究推理时多偏好对齐问题：给定一组基础奖励函数和参考KL正则化强度，能否设计一种微调方法，使得在推理时无需额外微调即可生成符合用户指定的任意奖励与正则化线性组合的图像？我们提出Diffusion Blend方法，通过融合经微调模型的反向扩散过程实现推理时多偏好对齐，并实例化为两种算法：面向多奖励对齐的DB-MPA与控制KL正则化的DB-KLA。大量实验表明，Diffusion Blend算法持续优于基线方法，接近或超越独立微调模型的性能，实现了高效的推理时用户驱动对齐。代码发布于https://github.com/bluewoods127/DB-2025。

The method introduces Diffusion Blend, a novel approach for inference-time multi-preference alignment that blends backward diffusion processes from fine-tuned models, specifically through two algorithms: DB-MPA for multi-reward alignment and DB-KLA for KL regularization control. Experimental results demonstrate that Diffusion Blend consistently outperforms baselines and matches or exceeds the performance of individually fine-tuned models, enabling efficient, user-specified alignment without additional fine-tuning.

Evaluate-as-Action: Self-Evaluated Process Rewards for Retrieval-Augmented Agents
Authors: Jiangming Shu, Yuxiang Zhang, Ye Ma, Xueyuan Lin, Jitao Sang
First: 2026-03-10T05:22:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T06:04:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-augmented agents can query external evidence, yet their reliability in multi-step reasoning remains limited: noisy retrieval may derail multi-hop question answering, while outcome-only reinforcement learning provides credit signals that are too coarse to optimize intermediate steps. We propose \textsc{EvalAct} (Evaluate-as-Action), which converts implicit retrieval quality assessment into an explicit action and enforces a coupled Search-to-Evaluate protocol so that each retrieval is immediately followed by a structured evaluation score, yielding process signals aligned with the interaction trajectory. To leverage these signals, we introduce Process-Calibrated Advantage Rescaling (PCAR), a GRPO-based optimization method that rescales advantages at the segment level according to evaluation scores, emphasizing reliable segments while updating uncertain ones conservatively. Experiments on seven open-domain QA benchmarks show that \textsc{EvalAct} achieves the best average accuracy, with the largest gains on multi-hop tasks, and ablations verify that the explicit evaluation loop drives the primary improvements while PCAR provides consistent additional benefits.

标题：评估即行动：检索增强智能体的自评估过程奖励机制
检索增强智能体虽能查询外部证据，但其多步推理的可靠性仍受限：噪声检索可能干扰多跳问答，而仅基于结果的强化学习提供的奖励信号过于粗略，难以优化中间步骤。我们提出EvalAct（评估即行动）方法，将隐式的检索质量评估转化为显式动作，并强制执行耦合的“检索-评估”协议，使每次检索后立即生成结构化评估分数，从而产生与交互轨迹对齐的过程信号。为利用这些信号，我们提出过程校准优势重缩放（PCAR）方法——一种基于GRPO的优化技术，根据评估分数在片段层级重缩放优势值，强化可靠片段的同时保守更新不确定片段。在七个开放域QA基准测试中，EvalAct取得了最佳平均准确率，其中多跳任务提升最为显著。消融实验证实：显式评估循环是主要改进来源，而PCAR能持续提供额外增益。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the reliability issues of retrieval-augmented agents in multi-step reasoning, where noisy retrieval can disrupt multi-hop question answering and outcome-only reinforcement learning offers overly coarse credit signals. The proposed method, EvalAct, transforms implicit retrieval quality assessment into an explicit action by enforcing a Search-to-Evaluate protocol that pairs each retrieval with a structured evaluation score, providing process signals aligned with the interaction trajectory. To utilize these signals, the authors introduce Process-Calibrated Advantage Rescaling (PCAR), a GRPO-based optimization technique that rescales advantages at the segment level based on evaluation scores, emphasizing reliable segments while updating uncertain ones conservatively. Experimental results on seven open-domain QA benchmarks demonstrate that EvalAct achieves the highest average accuracy, with the most significant improvements on multi-hop tasks, and ablations confirm that the explicit evaluation loop drives primary gains while PCAR consistently adds further benefits.
本文针对检索增强代理在多步推理中的可靠性问题展开研究，指出噪声检索可能干扰多跳问答，而仅基于结果的强化学习提供的奖励信号过于粗糙。提出的方法EvalAct将隐式的检索质量评估转化为显式动作，通过强制实施“搜索-评估”协议，使每次检索后立即生成结构化评估分数，从而提供与交互轨迹对齐的过程信号。为利用这些信号，作者引入了过程校准优势重缩放（PCAR），这是一种基于GRPO的优化方法，根据评估分数在片段级别重缩放优势值，强调可靠片段同时保守更新不确定部分。在七个开放域问答基准上的实验表明，EvalAct实现了最佳平均准确率，尤其在多跳任务上提升最大，消融实验验证了显式评估循环是主要改进来源，而PCAR则持续提供额外增益。
Controllable Exploration in Hybrid-Policy RLVR for Multi-Modal Reasoning
Authors: Zhuoxu Huang, Mengxi Jia, Hao Sun, Xuelong Li, Jungong Han
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-02-22T07:23:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T05:35:48+00:00
Comments: Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a primary learning paradigm for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of multi-modal large language models (MLLMs). However, during RL training, the enormous state space of MLLM and sparse rewards often leads to entropy collapse, policy degradation, or over-exploitation of suboptimal behaviors. This necessitates an exploration strategy that maintains productive stochasticity while avoiding the drawbacks of uncontrolled random sampling, yielding inefficient exploration. In this paper, we propose CalibRL, a hybrid-policy RLVR framework that supports controllable exploration with expert guidance, enabled by two key mechanisms. First, a distribution-aware advantage weighting scales updates by group rareness to calibrate the distribution, therefore preserving exploration. Meanwhile, the asymmetric activation function (LeakyReLU) leverages the expert knowledge as a calibration baseline to moderate overconfident updates while preserving their corrective direction. CalibRL increases policy entropy in a guided manner and clarifies the target distribution by estimating the on-policy distribution through online sampling. Updates are driven by these informative behaviors, avoiding convergence to erroneous patterns. Importantly, these designs help alleviate the distributional mismatch between the model's policy and expert trajectories, thereby achieving a more stable balance between exploration and exploitation. Extensive experiments across eight benchmarks, including both in-domain and out-of-domain settings, demonstrate consistent improvements, validating the effectiveness of our controllable hybrid-policy RLVR training. Code is available at https://github.com/zhh6425/CalibRL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向多模态推理的混合策略RLVR可控探索方法
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为增强多模态大语言模型（MLLM）推理能力的主要学习范式。然而，在RL训练过程中，MLLM巨大的状态空间和稀疏奖励常导致熵崩溃、策略退化或对次优行为的过度利用。这需要一种探索策略，既能保持有效的随机性，又能避免无控随机采样的弊端（即低效探索）。本文提出CalibRL，一种支持专家引导可控探索的混合策略RLVR框架，其核心在于两个关键机制。首先，分布感知优势加权通过组稀有度缩放更新以校准分布，从而维持探索。同时，非对称激活函数（LeakyReLU）利用专家知识作为校准基线，在保留修正方向的同时抑制过度自信的更新。CalibRL以引导方式增加策略熵，并通过在线采样估计同策略分布来明确目标分布。更新由这些信息丰富的行为驱动，避免收敛到错误模式。重要的是，这些设计有助于缓解模型策略与专家轨迹之间的分布失配，从而在探索与利用之间实现更稳定的平衡。在八个基准（包括领域内和领域外设置）上的大量实验显示出一致的性能提升，验证了我们可控混合策略RLVR训练的有效性。代码发布于https://github.com/zhh6425/CalibRL。

The paper addresses the challenge of inefficient exploration in Reinforcement Learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) for multi-modal large language models, where sparse rewards and vast state spaces often lead to entropy collapse or policy degradation. To enable controllable exploration, the authors propose CalibRL, a hybrid-policy RLVR framework that incorporates distribution-aware advantage weighting to scale updates by group rareness and an asymmetric activation function (LeakyReLU) that uses expert knowledge as a baseline to moderate overconfident updates. Experimental results across eight benchmarks, including in-domain and out-of-domain settings, show consistent improvements, validating the framework's effectiveness in achieving a stable balance between exploration and exploitation.

Adversarial Reinforcement Learning for Detecting False Data Injection Attacks in Vehicular Routing
Authors: Taha Eghtesad, Yevgeniy Vorobeychik, Aron Laszka
First: 2026-03-12T01:53:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T01:53:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In modern transportation networks, adversaries can manipulate routing algorithms using false data injection attacks, such as simulating heavy traffic with multiple devices running crowdsourced navigation applications, to mislead vehicles toward suboptimal routes and increase congestion. To address these threats, we formulate a strategically zero-sum game between an attacker, who injects such perturbations, and a defender, who detects anomalies based on the observed travel times of network edges. We propose a computational method based on multi-agent reinforcement learning to compute a Nash equilibrium of this game, providing an optimal detection strategy, which ensures that total travel time remains within a worst-case bound, even in the presence of an attack. We present an extensive experimental evaluation that demonstrates the robustness and practical benefits of our approach, providing a powerful framework to improve the resilience of transportation networks against false data injection. In particular, we show that our approach yields approximate equilibrium policies and significantly outperforms baselines for both the attacker and the defender.

标题：对抗性强化学习在车辆路由虚假数据注入攻击检测中的应用
在现代交通网络中，攻击者可通过虚假数据注入攻击操纵路由算法，例如利用多设备运行众包导航应用模拟拥堵，误导车辆选择次优路径并加剧拥堵。为应对此类威胁，我们将攻击者（注入扰动）与防御者（基于观测路段行程时间检测异常）之间的对抗建模为策略性零和博弈。提出一种基于多智能体强化学习的计算方法，求解该博弈的纳什均衡，从而提供最优检测策略，确保即使在遭受攻击时总行程时间仍能控制在最坏情况界限内。通过大量实验评估，验证了所提方法的鲁棒性与实际效益，为提升交通网络抵御虚假数据注入攻击的韧性提供了有力框架。特别地，我们证明该方法能生成近似均衡策略，并在攻击方与防御方任务上均显著优于基线方法。

DriveCritic: Towards Context-Aware, Human-Aligned Evaluation for Autonomous Driving with Vision-Language Models
Authors: Jingyu Song, Zhenxin Li, Shiyi Lan, Xinglong Sun, Nadine Chang, Maying Shen, Joshua Chen, Katherine A. Skinner, Jose M. Alvarez
Venue: ICRA 2026
First: 2025-10-15T03:00:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T01:20:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICRA 2026; 8 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Benchmarking autonomous driving planners to align with human judgment remains a critical challenge, as state-of-the-art metrics like the Extended Predictive Driver Model Score (EPDMS) lack context awareness in nuanced scenarios. To address this, we introduce DriveCritic, a novel framework featuring two key contributions: the DriveCritic dataset, a curated collection of challenging scenarios where context is critical for correct judgment and annotated with pairwise human preferences, and the DriveCritic model, a Vision-Language Model (VLM) based evaluator. Fine-tuned using a two-stage supervised and reinforcement learning pipeline, the DriveCritic model learns to adjudicate between trajectory pairs by integrating visual and symbolic context. Experiments show DriveCritic significantly outperforms existing metrics and baselines in matching human preferences and demonstrates strong context awareness. Overall, our work provides a more reliable, human-aligned foundation to evaluating autonomous driving systems. The project page for DriveCritic is https://song-jingyu.github.io/DriveCritic

ARROW: Augmented Replay for RObust World models
Authors: Abdulaziz Alyahya, Abdallah Al Siyabi, Markus R. Ernst, Luke Yang, Levin Kuhlmann, Gideon Kowadlo
First: 2026-03-12T00:15:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-12T00:15:11+00:00
Comments: 27 pages and 8 figures (includes Appendix)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Continual reinforcement learning challenges agents to acquire new skills while retaining previously learned ones with the goal of improving performance in both past and future tasks. Most existing approaches rely on model-free methods with replay buffers to mitigate catastrophic forgetting; however, these solutions often face significant scalability challenges due to large memory demands. Drawing inspiration from neuroscience, where the brain replays experiences to a predictive World Model rather than directly to the policy, we present ARROW (Augmented Replay for RObust World models), a model-based continual RL algorithm that extends DreamerV3 with a memory-efficient, distribution-matching replay buffer. Unlike standard fixed-size FIFO buffers, ARROW maintains two complementary buffers: a short-term buffer for recent experiences and a long-term buffer that preserves task diversity through intelligent sampling. We evaluate ARROW on two challenging continual RL settings: Tasks without shared structure (Atari), and tasks with shared structure, where knowledge transfer is possible (Procgen CoinRun variants). Compared to model-free and model-based baselines with replay buffers of the same-size, ARROW demonstrates substantially less forgetting on tasks without shared structure, while maintaining comparable forward transfer. Our findings highlight the potential of model-based RL and bio-inspired approaches for continual reinforcement learning, warranting further research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARROW：面向鲁棒世界模型的增强回放方法
持续强化学习要求智能体在掌握新技能的同时保持已学技能，以提升其在过往及未来任务中的表现。现有方法多采用无模型方法配合回放缓冲区来缓解灾难性遗忘，但这些方案常因内存需求庞大而面临可扩展性挑战。受神经科学启发——大脑会将经验回放至预测性世界模型而非直接传递给策略，我们提出ARROW（面向鲁棒世界模型的增强回放），这是一种基于模型的持续强化学习算法。该算法通过内存高效的分布匹配回放缓冲区扩展了DreamerV3框架。与标准固定容量FIFO缓冲区不同，ARROW维护两个互补缓冲区：短期缓冲区存储近期经验，长期缓冲区通过智能采样保持任务多样性。我们在两种挑战性持续强化学习场景中评估ARROW：无共享结构的任务（Atari）和具备共享结构、允许知识迁移的任务（Procgen CoinRun变体）。与使用同等规模回放缓冲区的无模型及基于模型基线相比，ARROW在无共享结构任务上表现出显著更低的遗忘率，同时保持相当的前向迁移能力。本研究凸显了基于模型的强化学习与仿生方法在持续强化学习中的潜力，值得进一步探索。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of catastrophic forgetting in continual reinforcement learning and the scalability limitations of model-free replay buffers, this paper introduces ARROW, a model-based algorithm inspired by neuroscience that augments DreamerV3 with a memory-efficient, distribution-matching replay buffer. The method employs a dual-buffer system—a short-term buffer for recent experiences and a long-term buffer that intelligently samples to preserve task diversity—to enhance robustness. Experimental results on Atari (tasks without shared structure) and Procgen CoinRun variants (tasks with shared structure) show that ARROW substantially reduces forgetting compared to same-size buffer baselines while maintaining comparable forward transfer, highlighting the promise of bio-inspired, model-based approaches for continual learning.
本文针对持续强化学习中的灾难性遗忘问题以及模型自由回放缓冲区存在的可扩展性限制，受神经科学启发，提出了ARROW这一基于模型的算法，它在DreamerV3基础上引入了内存高效、分布匹配的回放缓冲区。该方法采用双缓冲区系统——一个用于近期经验的短期缓冲区和一个通过智能采样保持任务多样性的长期缓冲区——以增强鲁棒性。在Atari（无共享结构的任务）和Procgen CoinRun变体（有共享结构的任务）上的实验结果表明，与相同大小的缓冲区基线相比，ARROW显著减少了遗忘，同时保持了相当的前向迁移能力，这凸显了受生物启发、基于模型的方法在持续学习中的潜力。
Ensuring Safety in Automated Mechanical Ventilation through Offline Reinforcement Learning and Digital Twin Verification
Authors: Hang Yu, Huidong Liu, Qingchen Zhang, William Joy, Kateryna Nikulina, Andreas A. Schuppert, Sina Saffaran, Declan Bates
First: 2026-03-11T23:21:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T23:21:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mechanical ventilation (MV) is a life-saving intervention for patients with acute respiratory failure (ARF) in the ICU. However, inappropriate ventilator settings could cause ventilator-induced lung injury (VILI). Also, clinicians workload is shown to be directly linked to patient outcomes. Hence, MV should be personalized and automated to improve patient outcomes. Previous attempts to incorporate personalization and automation in MV include traditional supervised learning and offline reinforcement learning (RL) approaches, which often neglect temporal dependencies and rely excessively on mortality-based rewards. As a result, early stage physiological deterioration and the risk of VILI are not adequately captured. To address these limitations, we propose Transformer-based Conservative Q-Learning (T-CQL), a novel offline RL framework that integrates a Transformer encoder for effective temporal modeling of patient dynamics, conservative adaptive regularization based on uncertainty quantification to ensure safety, and consistency regularization for robust decision-making. We build a clinically informed reward function that incorporates indicators of VILI and a score for severity of patients illness. Also, previous work predominantly uses Fitted Q-Evaluation (FQE) for RL policy evaluation on static offline data, which is less responsive to dynamic environmental changes and susceptible to distribution shifts. To overcome these evaluation limitations, interactive digital twins of ARF patients were used for online "at the bedside" evaluation. Our results demonstrate that T-CQL consistently outperforms existing state-of-the-art offline RL methodologies, providing safer and more effective ventilatory adjustments. Our framework demonstrates the potential of Transformer-based models combined with conservative RL strategies as a decision support tool in critical care.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过离线强化学习与数字孪生验证确保自动化机械通气安全性
机械通气（MV）是ICU急性呼吸衰竭（ARF）患者的生命支持手段，但不当的呼吸机设置可能导致呼吸机相关性肺损伤（VILI），且临床工作负荷与患者预后直接相关。因此，MV需个性化和自动化以改善预后。现有基于传统监督学习和离线强化学习（RL）的方法常忽略时序依赖性、过度依赖死亡率奖励，未能充分捕捉早期生理恶化与VILI风险。为此，我们提出基于Transformer的保守Q学习（T-CQL）框架：通过Transformer编码器建模患者动态时序特征，基于不确定性量化的保守自适应正则化确保安全性，并采用一致性正则化增强决策鲁棒性。我们设计了融合VILI指标与病情严重度评分的临床奖励函数。针对静态离线数据评估中拟合Q评估（FQE）对动态环境响应不足、易受分布偏移影响的问题，采用ARF患者交互式数字孪生进行在线床旁评估。实验表明，T-CQL持续优于现有离线RL方法，能提供更安全有效的通气调节。该框架展现了Transformer模型与保守RL策略结合作为重症监护决策支持工具的潜力。

The authors propose Transformer-based Conservative Q-Learning (T-CQL), an offline reinforcement learning framework that uses a Transformer encoder to model temporal patient dynamics, incorporates conservative regularization for safety, and employs a clinically informed reward function. Experimental results show that T-CQL outperforms existing offline RL methods, with evaluation conducted via interactive digital twins for realistic assessment, demonstrating its potential as a safer decision support tool in critical care.
本文旨在通过自动化机械通气改善患者预后并减轻临床医生负担，同时降低呼吸机所致肺损伤等风险。作者提出了基于Transformer的保守Q学习框架，该框架利用Transformer编码器建模患者时序动态，结合保守正则化确保安全性，并采用临床启发的奖励函数。实验结果表明，该方法在通过交互式数字孪生进行评估时，优于现有离线强化学习方法，展现了其作为重症监护中更安全决策支持工具的潜力。
abx_amr_simulator: A simulation environment for antibiotic prescribing policy optimization under antimicrobial resistance
Authors: Joyce Lee, Seth Blumberg
First: 2026-03-11T23:15:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T23:15:32+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Antimicrobial resistance (AMR) poses a global health threat, reducing the effectiveness of antibiotics and complicating clinical decision-making. To address this challenge, we introduce abx_amr_simulator, a Python-based simulation package designed to model antibiotic prescribing and AMR dynamics within a controlled, reinforcement learning (RL)-compatible environment. The simulator allows users to specify patient populations, antibiotic-specific AMR response curves, and reward functions that balance immedi- ate clinical benefit against long-term resistance management. Key features include a modular design for configuring patient attributes, antibiotic resistance dynamics modeled via a leaky-balloon abstraction, and tools to explore partial observability through noise, bias, and delay in observations. The package is compatible with the Gymnasium RL API, enabling users to train and test RL agents under diverse clinical scenarios. From an ML perspective, the package provides a configurable benchmark environment for sequential decision-making under uncertainty, including partial observability induced by noisy, biased, and delayed observations. By providing a customizable and extensible framework, abx_amr_simulator offers a valuable tool for studying AMR dynamics and optimizing antibiotic stewardship strategies under realistic uncertainty.

标题：abx_amr_simulator：抗菌药物耐药性背景下抗生素处方策略优化的仿真环境
抗菌药物耐药性（AMR）构成全球健康威胁，降低抗生素疗效并增加临床决策难度。为应对这一挑战，我们推出abx_amr_simulator——基于Python的仿真工具包，可在强化学习兼容的受控环境中模拟抗生素处方与AMR动态。该仿真器支持用户定义患者群体、抗生素特异性AMR响应曲线，以及平衡即时临床获益与长期耐药管理的奖励函数。核心特性包括：用于配置患者属性的模块化设计、通过漏气球抽象模型实现的抗生素耐药动态建模，以及通过观测噪声、偏差和延迟探索部分可观测性的工具。本工具包兼容Gymnasium强化学习API，支持用户在不同临床场景下训练与测试强化学习智能体。从机器学习视角看，该工具包为不确定性（包括由含噪、有偏和延迟观测引发的部分可观测性）下的序列决策提供了可配置的基准环境。通过提供可定制、可扩展的框架，abx_amr_simulator为研究AMR动态及在现实不确定性下优化抗生素管理策略提供了重要工具。

Novelty Adaptation Through Hybrid Large Language Model (LLM)-Symbolic Planning and LLM-guided Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hong Lu, Pierrick Lorang, Timothy R. Duggan, Jivko Sinapov, Matthias Scheutz
First: 2026-03-11T22:38:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T22:38:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In dynamic open-world environments, autonomous agents often encounter novelties that hinder their ability to find plans to achieve their goals. Specifically, traditional symbolic planners fail to generate plans when the robot's planning domain lacks the operators that enable it to interact appropriately with novel objects in the environment. We propose a neuro-symbolic architecture that integrates symbolic planning, reinforcement learning, and a large language model (LLM) to learn how to handle novel objects. In particular, we leverage the common sense reasoning capability of the LLM to identify missing operators, generate plans with the symbolic AI planner, and write reward functions to guide the reinforcement learning agent in learning control policies for newly identified operators. Our method outperforms the state-of-the-art methods in operator discovery as well as operator learning in continuous robotic domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于混合大语言模型符号规划与大语言模型引导强化学习的新颖性适应方法
在动态开放世界环境中，自主智能体常遭遇阻碍其实现目标规划能力的新颖对象。具体而言，当机器人的规划域缺乏与环境新颖对象进行适当交互的算子时，传统符号规划器将无法生成有效规划。本文提出一种融合符号规划、强化学习与大语言模型的神经符号架构，以学习处理新颖对象的方法。我们利用大语言模型的常识推理能力识别缺失算子，通过符号AI规划器生成规划方案，并编写奖励函数以引导强化学习智能体掌握新识别算子的控制策略。实验表明，本方法在连续机器人领域的算子发现与算子学习任务上均优于现有最优方法。

本文针对自主智能体在动态开放世界中遇到新颖物体时，传统符号规划器因缺少操作符而无法生成计划的问题，提出了一种神经符号架构。该方法结合符号规划、强化学习和大型语言模型（LLM），利用LLM的常识推理能力识别缺失操作符，由符号AI规划器生成计划，并通过LLM编写奖励函数来指导强化学习智能体学习新操作符的控制策略。实验结果表明，该方法在连续机器人领域的操作符发现和学习方面均优于现有先进方法。
Enhancing Sample Efficiency in Multi-Agent RL with Uncertainty Quantification and Selective Exploration
Authors: Tom Danino, Nahum Shimkin
First: 2025-06-03T13:13:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T22:18:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) methods have achieved state-of-the-art results on a range of multi-agent tasks. Yet, MARL algorithms typically require significantly more environment interactions than their single-agent counterparts to converge, a problem exacerbated by the difficulty in exploring over a large joint action space and the high variance intrinsic to MARL environments. To tackle these issues, we propose a novel algorithm that combines a decomposed centralized critic with decentralized ensemble learning, incorporating several key contributions. The main component in our scheme is a selective exploration method that leverages ensemble kurtosis. We extend the global decomposed critic with a diversity-regularized ensemble of individual critics and utilize its excess kurtosis to guide exploration toward high-uncertainty states and actions. To improve sample efficiency, we train the centralized critic with a novel truncated variation of the TD($λ$) algorithm, enabling efficient off-policy learning with reduced variance. On the actor side, our suggested algorithm adapts the mixed samples approach to MARL, mixing on-policy and off-policy loss functions for training the actors. This approach balances between stability and efficiency and outperforms purely off-policy learning. The evaluation shows our method outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on standard MARL benchmarks, including a variety of SMAC II maps.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于不确定性量化与选择性探索提升多智能体强化学习的样本效率
多智能体强化学习方法已在多项多智能体任务中取得领先成果，但其收敛通常需要比单智能体方法更多的环境交互，这一难题因大规模联合动作空间的探索困难及环境固有高方差而加剧。为应对这些问题，我们提出一种融合分解式中心化评价器与去中心化集成学习的新算法，包含以下核心贡献：方案主体是基于集成峰度的选择性探索方法，通过多样性正则化的个体评价器集成扩展全局分解评价器，并利用其超值峰度引导智能体向高不确定性状态与动作探索；为提升样本效率，采用截断型TD(λ)算法变体训练中心化评价器，实现方差更小的高效离策略学习；在执行器层面，算法将混合样本方法适配至多智能体场景，融合同策略与离策略损失函数进行训练，在稳定性与效率间取得平衡。实验表明，本方法在包括多种SMAC II地图的标准多智能体强化学习基准测试中均优于现有先进基线。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high sample inefficiency of multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), which stems from the large joint action space and high environmental variance. The proposed method introduces a decomposed centralized critic enhanced with a decentralized ensemble, using the ensemble's kurtosis to guide selective exploration toward high-uncertainty states and actions. It employs a truncated TD(λ) for efficient off-policy critic training and mixes on-policy and off-policy losses for actor training to balance stability and efficiency. Experimental results demonstrate that the algorithm outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on standard MARL benchmarks, including various SMAC II maps.

Meta-Reinforcement Learning with Self-Reflection for Agentic Search
Authors: Teng Xiao, Yige Yuan, Hamish Ivison, Huaisheng Zhu, Faeze Brahman, Nathan Lambert, Pradeep Dasigi, Noah A. Smith, Hannaneh Hajishirzi
First: 2026-03-11T21:40:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T21:40:26+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper introduces MR-Search, an in-context meta reinforcement learning (RL) formulation for agentic search with self-reflection. Instead of optimizing a policy within a single independent episode with sparse rewards, MR-Search trains a policy that conditions on past episodes and adapts its search strategy across episodes. MR-Search learns to learn a search strategy with self-reflection, allowing search agents to improve in-context exploration at test-time. Specifically, MR-Search performs cross-episode exploration by generating explicit self-reflections after each episode and leveraging them as additional context to guide subsequent attempts, thereby promoting more effective exploration during test-time. We further introduce a multi-turn RL algorithm that estimates a dense relative advantage at the turn level, enabling fine-grained credit assignment on each episode. Empirical results across various benchmarks demonstrate the advantages of MR-Search over baselines based RL, showing strong generalization and relative improvements of 9.2% to 19.3% across eight benchmarks. Our code and data are available at https://github.com/tengxiao1/MR-Search.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具备自我反思能力的元强化学习在智能搜索中的应用
