Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the challenge of sparse rewards in single-episode reinforcement learning for search tasks, proposing MR-Search, a meta-reinforcement learning framework that conditions on past episodes and adapts strategies across episodes through self-reflection. The method involves generating explicit self-reflections after each episode to guide subsequent attempts, alongside a multi-turn RL algorithm for fine-grained credit assignment via dense relative advantage estimation. Experimental results across eight benchmarks show that MR-Search outperforms baseline RL methods, achieving relative improvements of 9.2% to 19.3% and demonstrating strong generalization capabilities.
本文针对单次独立强化学习在搜索任务中奖励稀疏的挑战，提出了MR-Search，这是一种基于自我反思的元强化学习框架，通过利用过往经验跨回合调整搜索策略。该方法在每轮搜索后生成明确的自我反思，作为后续尝试的额外上下文指导，并结合多回合强化学习算法，通过密集相对优势估计实现细粒度信用分配。在多个基准测试中的实证结果表明，MR-Search优于基于强化学习的基线方法，相对性能提升达9.2%至19.3%，并展现出强大的泛化能力。
Hindsight-Anchored Policy Optimization: Turning Failure into Feedback in Sparse Reward Settings
Authors: Yuning Wu, Ke Wang, Devin Chen, Kai Wei
First: 2026-03-11T21:33:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T21:33:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has emerged as a promising paradigm for post-training reasoning models. However, group-based methods such as Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) face a critical dilemma in sparse-reward settings: pure Reinforcement Learning (RL) suffers from advantage collapse and high-variance gradient estimation, while mixed-policy optimization introduces persistent distributional bias. To resolve this dilemma, we introduce Hindsight-Anchored Policy Optimization (HAPO). HAPO employs the Synthetic Success Injection (SSI) operator, a hindsight mechanism that selectively anchors optimization to teacher demonstrations during failure. This injection is governed by a Thompson sampling-inspired gating mechanism, creating an autonomous, self-paced curriculum. Theoretically, we demonstrate that HAPO achieves \textit{asymptotic consistency}: by naturally annealing the teacher signal as the policy improves, HAPO recovers the unbiased on-policy gradient. This ensures off-policy guidance acts as a temporary scaffold rather than a persistent ceiling, enabling the model to surpass the limitations of static teacher forcing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：后见锚定策略优化：在稀疏奖励环境中将失败转化为反馈
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已成为后训练推理模型的一种前景广阔的范式。然而，在稀疏奖励环境中，基于群体的方法（如群体相对策略优化GRPO）面临关键困境：纯强化学习（RL）存在优势崩溃和高方差梯度估计问题，而混合策略优化则引入持续分布偏差。为解决此困境，我们提出后见锚定策略优化（HAPO）。HAPO采用合成成功注入（SSI）算子——一种后见机制，能在失败时有选择地将优化锚定至教师示范。该注入过程受汤普森采样启发的门控机制调控，形成自主、自适应的学习进程。理论上，我们证明HAPO具有渐近一致性：通过随策略改进自然衰减教师信号，HAPO能恢复无偏的同策略梯度。这确保离策略指导仅作为临时支架而非永久上限，使模型能突破静态教师强制的局限。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of sparse rewards in reinforcement learning for reasoning models, where existing methods like GRPO suffer from either advantage collapse and high variance in pure RL or persistent bias in mixed-policy approaches. To resolve this, the authors propose Hindsight-Anchored Policy Optimization (HAPO), which uses a Synthetic Success Injection operator—a hindsight mechanism that selectively anchors optimization to teacher demonstrations during failures, guided by a Thompson sampling-inspired gating mechanism to create a self-paced curriculum. Theoretically, HAPO achieves asymptotic consistency by annealing teacher signals as the policy improves, recovering unbiased on-policy gradients and allowing the model to surpass static teacher limitations, with experimental results validating its effectiveness in sparse-reward settings.
本文针对强化学习中稀疏奖励场景下的挑战，现有方法如GRPO在纯强化学习中面临优势崩溃和高方差梯度估计问题，而在混合策略优化中则存在持续分布偏差。为解决这一困境，作者提出了后见锚定策略优化（HAPO），该方法采用合成成功注入算子——一种后见机制，在失败时选择性地将优化锚定到教师示范上，并通过汤普森采样启发的门控机制实现自主、自适应的课程学习。理论上，HAPO实现了渐近一致性：随着策略改进自然衰减教师信号，恢复无偏的在线策略梯度，确保离策略指导作为临时支架而非永久上限，使模型能超越静态教师强制的限制，实验结果验证了其在稀疏奖励环境中的有效性。
Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Greenhouse Gas Offset Credit Markets
Authors: Liam Welsh, Udit Grover, Sebastian Jaimungal
First: 2025-04-15T14:56:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T20:54:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Climate change is a major threat to the future of humanity, and its impacts are being intensified by excess man-made greenhouse gas emissions. One method governments can employ to control these emissions is to provide firms with emission limits and penalize any excess emissions above the limit. Excess emissions may also be offset by firms who choose to invest in carbon reducing and capturing projects. These projects generate offset credits which can be submitted to a regulating agency to offset a firm's excess emissions, or they can be traded with other firms. In this work, we characterize the finite-agent Nash equilibrium for offset credit markets. As computing Nash equilibria is an NP-hard problem, we utilize the modern reinforcement learning technique Nash-DQN to efficiently estimate the market's Nash equilibria. We demonstrate not only the validity of employing reinforcement learning methods applied to climate themed financial markets, but also the significant financial savings emitting firms may achieve when abiding by the Nash equilibria through numerical experiments.

DeepSport: A Multimodal Large Language Model for Comprehensive Sports Video Reasoning via Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Junbo Zou, Haotian Xia, Zhen Ye, Shengjie Zhang, Christopher Lai, Vicente Ordonez, Weining Shen, Hanjie Chen
First: 2025-11-17T02:57:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T20:52:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sports video understanding requires perceiving high-speed dynamics, complex rules, and long temporal contexts. Yet, current Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) remain narrowly focused on single sports, specific tasks, or training-free paradigms. We introduce DeepSport, the first end-to-end trained MLLM for multi-task, multi-sport video understanding. DeepSport shifts from passive frame processing to active, iterative reasoning, dynamically extracting frames to "think with videos." To train our model, we curate a unified 78k-sample dataset via a rigorous three-step text-and-vision distillation pipeline. We then employ a progressive two-stage training strategy: a Sports Curriculum Supervised Fine-Tuning phase to build foundational perception, followed by Agentic Reinforcement Learning with a novel tool-use reward. Extensive experiments on a comprehensive 6.7k benchmark demonstrate that DeepSport achieves state-of-the-art performance, outperforming powerful proprietary and open-source models, while utilizing significantly fewer frames. Furthermore, it exhibits strong zero-shot transferability to unseen sports and broad motion recognition tasks, establishing a highly efficient and generalized foundation for complex video reasoning.

Representation Finetuning for Continual Learning
Authors: Haihua Luo, Xuming Ran, Tommi Kärkkäinen, Huiyan Xue, Zhonghua Chen, Qi Xu, Fengyu Cong
First: 2026-03-11T18:15:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T18:15:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The world is inherently dynamic, and continual learning aims to enable models to adapt to ever-evolving data streams. While pre-trained models have shown powerful performance in continual learning, they still require finetuning to adapt effectively to downstream tasks. However, prevailing Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) methods operate through empirical, black-box optimization at the weight level. These approaches lack explicit control over representation drift, leading to sensitivity to domain shifts and catastrophic forgetting in continual learning scenarios. In this work, we introduce Continual Representation Learning (CoRe), a novel framework that for the first time shifts the finetuning paradigm from weight space to representation space. Unlike conventional methods, CoRe performs task-specific interventions within a low-rank linear subspace of hidden representations, adopting a learning process with explicit objectives, which ensures stability for past tasks while maintaining plasticity for new ones. By constraining updates to a low-rank subspace, CoRe achieves exceptional parameter efficiency. Extensive experiments across multiple continual learning benchmarks demonstrate that CoRe not only preserves parameter efficiency but also significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods. Our work introduces representation finetuning as a new, more effective and interpretable paradigm for continual learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向持续学习的表示微调
世界本质上是动态的，持续学习旨在使模型能够适应不断演变的数据流。尽管预训练模型在持续学习中展现出强大性能，但仍需通过微调来有效适应下游任务。然而，当前主流的参数高效微调方法依赖于权重层面的经验性黑盒优化，缺乏对表示漂移的显式控制，导致模型对领域偏移敏感，并在持续学习场景中出现灾难性遗忘。本文提出持续表示学习框架，首次将微调范式从权重空间转向表示空间。与传统方法不同，该框架在隐藏表示的低秩线性子空间内执行任务特异性干预，采用具有显式目标的学习过程，在保持对新任务可塑性的同时确保对旧任务的稳定性。通过将更新约束在低秩子空间，该方法实现了卓越的参数效率。在多个持续学习基准上的广泛实验表明，该框架不仅保持了参数高效性，且显著优于现有先进方法。本研究开创了表示微调这一更高效、可解释的持续学习新范式。

The motivation for this work stems from the need to adapt pre-trained models to dynamic data streams in continual learning, where existing parameter-efficient fine-tuning methods suffer from uncontrolled representation drift leading to forgetting and sensitivity to domain shifts. The proposed method, Continual Representation Learning (CoRe), shifts fine-tuning from weight space to representation space by performing task-specific interventions in a low-rank linear subspace of hidden representations, with explicit objectives to balance stability and plasticity. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks show that CoRe maintains parameter efficiency while significantly outperforming state-of-the-art methods, establishing representation fine-tuning as a more effective and interpretable paradigm.
本研究的动机在于使预训练模型适应持续学习中的动态数据流，现有参数高效微调方法存在表示漂移不受控的问题，导致遗忘和领域偏移敏感。所提出的方法——持续表示学习（CoRe）——将微调从权重空间转向表示空间，通过在隐藏表示的低秩线性子空间中进行任务特定干预，并采用明确目标以平衡稳定性和可塑性。在多个持续学习基准上的实验结果表明，CoRe在保持参数效率的同时显著优于现有最先进方法，从而确立了表示微调作为一种更有效且可解释的新范式。
Bayesian Optimization of Partially Known Systems using Hybrid Models
Authors: Eike Cramer, Luis Kutschat, Oliver Stollenwerk, Joel A. Paulson, Alexander Mitsos
First: 2026-03-11T18:13:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T18:13:26+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 5 Figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization (BO) has gained attention as an efficient algorithm for black-box optimization of expensive-to-evaluate systems, where the BO algorithm iteratively queries the system and suggests new trials based on a probabilistic model fitted to previous samples. Still, the standard BO loop may require a prohibitively large number of experiments to converge to the optimum, especially for high-dimensional and nonlinear systems. We present a hybrid model-based BO formulation that combines the iterative Bayesian learning of BO with partially known mechanistic physical models. Instead of learning a direct mapping from inputs to the objective, we write all known equations for a physics-based model and infer expressions for variables missing equations using a probabilistic model, in our case, a Gaussian process (GP). The final formulation then includes the GP as a constraint in the hybrid model, thereby allowing other physics-based nonlinear and implicit model constraints. This hybrid model formulation yields a constrained, nonlinear stochastic program, which we discretize using the sample-average approximation. In an in-silico optimization of a single-stage distillation, the hybrid BO model based on mass conservation laws yields significantly better designs than a standard BO loop. Furthermore, the hybrid model converges in as few as one iteration, depending on the initial samples, whereas, the standard BO does not converge within 25 for any of the seeds. Overall, the proposed hybrid BO scheme presents a promising optimization method for partially known systems, leveraging the strengths of both mechanistic modeling and data-driven optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于混合模型的部分已知系统贝叶斯优化方法
贝叶斯优化（BO）作为一种针对高成本评估系统的黑箱优化高效算法受到关注，其通过迭代查询系统并基于概率模型拟合历史样本提出新试验点。然而标准BO流程可能需要大量实验才能收敛至最优解，尤其对于高维非线性系统。本文提出一种基于混合模型的BO框架，将BO的迭代贝叶斯学习与部分已知的机理物理模型相结合。我们通过建立基于物理的模型方程，并利用高斯过程（GP）概率模型推断缺失方程的变量表达式，而非直接学习输入到目标的映射关系。最终框架将GP作为混合模型的约束条件，从而兼容其他基于物理的非线性和隐式模型约束。该混合模型构成一个带约束的非线性随机规划问题，我们采用样本平均逼近法进行离散化。在单级蒸馏的仿真优化中，基于质量守恒定律的混合BO模型相比标准BO流程获得了显著更优的设计方案。此外，混合模型仅需1次迭代即可收敛（取决于初始样本），而标准BO在25次迭代内均未收敛。总体而言，所提出的混合BO方案通过融合机理建模与数据驱动优化的优势，为部分已知系统提供了一种前景广阔的优化方法。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to enhance Bayesian optimization (BO) for expensive-to-evaluate systems by incorporating partial mechanistic knowledge, addressing the slow convergence of standard BO in high-dimensional, nonlinear settings. The method develops a hybrid model that integrates known physics-based equations with a Gaussian process (GP) to infer missing relationships, formulating a constrained stochastic program solved via sample-average approximation. Experimental results on an in-silico distillation case show the hybrid BO achieves significantly better designs and converges in as few as one iteration, outperforming standard BO which fails to converge within 25 iterations.
本研究旨在通过结合部分已知的机理知识来改进贝叶斯优化（BO）方法，以解决标准BO在高维非线性系统中收敛慢的问题。方法上提出了一种混合模型，将已知的物理方程与高斯过程（GP）结合以推断缺失关系，形成约束随机规划并通过样本平均近似求解。在单级蒸馏的仿真优化实验中，基于质量守恒定律的混合BO模型获得了显著更优的设计，且仅需一次迭代即可收敛，而标准BO在25次迭代内均未收敛。
Learning to Unscramble: Simplifying Symbolic Expressions via Self-Supervised Oracle Trajectories
Authors: David Shih
First: 2026-03-11T18:00:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T18:00:01+00:00
Comments: 14 pages, 6 figures, 2 tables; work done in collaboration with Claude Code
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present a new self-supervised machine learning approach for symbolic simplification of complex mathematical expressions. Training data is generated by scrambling simple expressions and recording the inverse operations, creating oracle trajectories that provide both goal states and explicit paths to reach them. A permutation-equivariant, transformer-based policy network is then trained on this data step-wise to predict the oracle action given the input expression. We demonstrate this approach on two problems in high-energy physics: dilogarithm reduction and spinor-helicity scattering amplitude simplification. In both cases, our trained policy network achieves near perfect solve rates across a wide range of difficulty levels, substantially outperforming prior approaches based on reinforcement learning and end-to-end regression. When combined with contrastive grouping and beam search, our model achieves a 100\% full simplification rate on a representative selection of 5-point gluon tree-level amplitudes in Yang-Mills theory, including expressions with over 200 initial terms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习解扰：通过自监督预言轨迹简化符号表达式
我们提出了一种新的自监督机器学习方法，用于复杂数学表达式的符号简化。训练数据通过打乱简单表达式并记录逆操作生成，从而创建同时提供目标状态及实现路径的预言轨迹。随后，基于置换等变的Transformer策略网络在此数据上逐步训练，以根据输入表达式预测预言动作。我们在高能物理的两个问题上验证了该方法：二对数归约与旋量螺旋度散射振幅简化。两种情况下，训练后的策略网络在广泛难度范围内均实现接近完美的求解率，显著优于此前基于强化学习和端到端回归的方法。结合对比分组与束搜索，我们的模型在杨-米尔斯理论中具有代表性的五点胶子树级振幅样本上实现了100%的完全简化率，包括初始项数超过200的表达式。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to automate the simplification of complex symbolic mathematical expressions, this paper introduces a self-supervised method that generates training data by scrambling simple expressions and recording the inverse operations as oracle trajectories. The method employs a permutation-equivariant transformer-based policy network trained step-wise on this data to predict the next simplification action. Experimental results on high-energy physics problems, including dilogarithm reduction and spinor-helicity amplitude simplification, show the policy achieves near-perfect solve rates, significantly outperforming prior reinforcement learning and regression approaches, and attains a 100% full simplification rate on complex 5-point gluon amplitudes when enhanced with contrastive grouping and beam search.
本文旨在自动化简化复杂的符号数学表达式，提出了一种自监督方法，通过打乱简单表达式并记录逆操作作为参考轨迹来生成训练数据。该方法采用基于置换等变Transformer的策略网络，在该数据上进行逐步训练以预测下一步简化操作。在高能物理问题上的实验结果表明，包括对双对数归约和旋量螺旋度振幅简化的任务中，该策略实现了接近完美的求解率，显著优于先前的强化学习和回归方法，并在结合对比分组和束搜索后，对复杂的5点胶子振幅实现了100%的完全简化率。
Bayesian Optimization with Gaussian Processes to Accelerate Stationary Point Searches
Authors: Rohit Goswami
First: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00
Comments: 57 pages, 22 figures. Invited article for ACS Physical Chemistry Au
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accelerating the explorations of stationary points on potential energy surfaces building local surrogates spans decades of effort. Done correctly, surrogates reduce required evaluations by an order of magnitude while preserving the accuracy of the underlying theory. We present a unified Bayesian Optimization view of minimization, single point saddle searches, and double ended saddle searches through a unified six-step surrogate loop, differing only in the inner optimization target and acquisition criterion. The framework uses Gaussian process regression with derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning. The Optimal Transport GP extensions of farthest point sampling with Earth mover's distance, MAP regularization via variance barrier and oscillation detection, and adaptive trust radius form concrete extensions of the same basic methodology, improving accuracy and efficiency. We also demonstrate random Fourier features decouple hyperparameter training from predictions enabling favorable scaling for high-dimensional systems. Accompanying pedagogical Rust code demonstrates that all applications use the exact same Bayesian optimization loop, bridging the gap between theoretical formulation and practical execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的贝叶斯优化加速势能面驻点搜索
通过构建局部代理模型加速势能面驻点探索已历经数十年研究。正确实施的代理模型能在保持底层理论精度的同时，将所需计算量降低一个数量级。本文提出统一的贝叶斯优化框架，通过六步代理循环统一处理极小值点搜索、单点鞍点搜索和双端鞍点搜索，仅在内层优化目标和采集准则上存在差异。该框架采用含导数观测的高斯过程回归、反距离核函数及主动学习技术。通过最远点采样与推土机距离的最优传输GP扩展、基于方差屏障与振荡检测的MAP正则化、自适应信任半径等具体扩展方法，在保持基础方法论一致性的同时提升了精度与效率。随机傅里叶特征的应用实现超参数训练与预测解耦，为高维系统提供优越的扩展性。配套的Rust教学代码表明所有应用均采用完全相同的贝叶斯优化循环，弥合了理论构建与实际执行间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing challenge of efficiently exploring stationary points on potential energy surfaces, this paper presents a unified Bayesian Optimization framework using Gaussian processes to accelerate such searches. The method employs a six-step surrogate loop with Gaussian process regression incorporating derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning, extended with techniques like Optimal Transport GP, farthest point sampling, and adaptive trust radius to improve performance. Key experimental results demonstrate that the approach reduces required evaluations by an order of magnitude while maintaining accuracy, with random Fourier features enabling favorable scaling for high-dimensional systems, as illustrated in accompanying pedagogical code.
本文旨在解决势能面上驻点搜索效率低下的长期挑战，提出了一个基于高斯过程的统一贝叶斯优化框架来加速此类搜索。该方法采用一个六步代理循环，结合了高斯过程回归、导数观测、反距离核和主动学习，并通过最优传输高斯过程、最远点采样和自适应信任半径等技术进行扩展以提升性能。主要实验结果表明，该方法在保持精度的同时将所需评估次数减少了一个数量级，其中随机傅里叶特征技术实现了对高维系统的良好扩展性，相关教学代码也验证了其可行性。
Learning What Reinforcement Learning Can't: Interleaved Online Fine-Tuning for Hardest Questions
Authors: Lu Ma, Hao Liang, Meiyi Qiang, Lexiang Tang, Xiaochen Ma, Zhen Hao Wong, Junbo Niu, Chengyu Shen, Runming He, Yanhao Li, Bin Cui, Wentao Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-09T08:11:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T17:08:49+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in large language model (LLM) reasoning have shown that sophisticated behaviors such as planning and self-reflection can emerge through reinforcement learning (RL). However, despite these successes, RL in its current form remains insufficient to induce capabilities that exceed the limitations of the base model, as it is primarily optimized based on existing knowledge of the model rather than facilitating the acquisition of new information. To address this limitation, we employ supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to learn what RL cannot, which enables the incorporation of new knowledge and reasoning patterns by leveraging high-quality demonstration data. We analyze the training dynamics of RL and SFT for LLM reasoning and find that RL excels at maintaining and improving performance on questions within the model's original capabilities, while SFT is more effective at enabling progress on questions beyond the current scope of the model. Motivated by the complementary strengths of RL and SFT, we introduce a novel training approach, \textbf{ReLIFT} (\textbf{Re}inforcement \textbf{L}earning \textbf{I}nterleaved with Online \textbf{F}ine-\textbf{T}uning). In ReLIFT, the model is primarily trained using RL, but when it encounters challenging questions, high-quality solutions are collected for fine-tuning, and the training process alternates between RL and fine-tuning to enhance the model's reasoning abilities. ReLIFT achieves an average improvement of over +5.2 points across five competition-level benchmarks and one out-of-distribution benchmark compared to other zero-RL models. Furthermore, we demonstrate that ReLIFT outperforms both RL and SFT while using only 13\% of the detailed demonstration data, highlighting its scalability. These results provide compelling evidence that ReLIFT overcomes the fundamental limitations of RL and underscores the significant potential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习强化学习无法掌握的内容：针对最难问题的交错在线微调
近期大语言模型（LLM）推理的进展表明，规划与自我反思等复杂行为可通过强化学习（RL）自然涌现。然而，尽管取得这些成功，当前形式的强化学习仍不足以突破基础模型的能力局限，因其主要基于模型已有知识进行优化，而非促进新信息的获取。为应对这一局限，我们采用监督微调（SFT）来学习强化学习无法掌握的内容，通过利用高质量示范数据实现新知识与推理模式的融合。我们分析了强化学习与监督微调在LLM推理中的训练动态，发现强化学习擅长维持并提升模型原有能力范围内问题的表现，而监督微调更有效推动模型突破当前能力边界。基于强化学习与监督微调的互补优势，我们提出一种新颖的训练方法——\textbf{ReLIFT}（\textbf{强化学习}与在线\textbf{微调}交错训练）。在ReLIFT中，模型主要使用强化学习训练，但当遇到挑战性问题时，会收集高质量解决方案进行微调，训练过程在强化学习与微调间交替进行以增强模型推理能力。相比其他零强化学习模型，ReLIFT在五个竞赛级基准和一个分布外基准上平均提升超过+5.2分。此外，我们证明ReLIFT仅需13%的详细示范数据即可超越纯强化学习与监督微调，凸显其可扩展性。这些结果为ReLIFT突破强化学习根本局限提供了有力证据，并彰显其巨大潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of reinforcement learning (RL) in enabling large language models to acquire new knowledge beyond their base capabilities, as RL primarily optimizes existing knowledge rather than facilitating learning of novel information. To overcome this, the authors propose ReLIFT, a method that interleaves RL training with online supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on high-quality demonstrations when challenging questions are encountered, leveraging the complementary strengths of RL for maintaining performance on within-capability questions and SFT for enabling progress on harder, out-of-scope problems. Experimental results show that ReLIFT achieves an average improvement of over +5.2 points across five competition-level and one out-of-distribution benchmark compared to zero-RL models, while using only 13% of demonstration data, demonstrating its effectiveness and scalability in enhancing reasoning abilities.
本文针对强化学习在使大语言模型获取超出其基础能力的新知识方面的局限性，因为强化学习主要优化现有知识而非促进新信息的学习。为此，作者提出了ReLIFT方法，该方法在训练过程中交替使用强化学习和在线监督微调，当遇到难题时收集高质量演示进行微调，从而结合强化学习在维持模型原有能力问题上的优势与监督微调在处理更困难、超出范围问题上的有效性。实验结果表明，ReLIFT在五个竞赛级基准和一个分布外基准上平均提升了超过+5.2分，且仅使用13%的演示数据，优于纯强化学习和监督微调，证明了其在提升推理能力方面的有效性和可扩展性。
Contact Coverage-Guided Exploration for General-Purpose Dexterous Manipulation
Authors: Zixuan Liu, Ruoyi Qiao, Chenrui Tie, Xuanwei Liu, Yunfan Lou, Chongkai Gao, Zhixuan Xu, Lin Shao
First: 2026-03-11T16:55:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:55:49+00:00
Comments: 16 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Deep Reinforcement learning (DRL) has achieved remarkable success in domains with well-defined reward structures, such as Atari games and locomotion. In contrast, dexterous manipulation lacks general-purpose reward formulations and typically depends on task-specific, handcrafted priors to guide hand-object interactions. We propose Contact Coverage-Guided Exploration (CCGE), a general exploration method designed for general-purpose dexterous manipulation tasks. CCGE represents contact state as the intersection between object surface points and predefined hand keypoints, encouraging dexterous hands to discover diverse and novel contact patterns, namely which fingers contact which object regions. It maintains a contact counter conditioned on discretized object states obtained via learned hash codes, capturing how frequently each finger interacts with different object regions. This counter is leveraged in two complementary ways: (1) to assign a count-based contact coverage reward that promotes exploration of novel contact patterns, and (2) an energy-based reaching reward that guides the agent toward under-explored contact regions. We evaluate CCGE on a diverse set of dexterous manipulation tasks, including cluttered object singulation, constrained object retrieval, in-hand reorientation, and bimanual manipulation. Experimental results show that CCGE substantially improves training efficiency and success rates over existing exploration methods, and that the contact patterns learned with CCGE transfer robustly to real-world robotic systems. Project page is https://contact-coverage-guided-exploration.github.io.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向通用灵巧操作的接触覆盖引导探索
深度强化学习（DRL）在奖励结构明确的领域（如Atari游戏和运动控制）已取得显著成功。相比之下，灵巧操作缺乏通用的奖励设计框架，通常依赖针对特定任务手工设计的先验知识来引导手-物体交互。本文提出接触覆盖引导探索（CCGE），一种专为通用灵巧操作任务设计的探索方法。CCGE将接触状态表示为物体表面点与预定义手部关键点的交集，激励灵巧手发现多样新颖的接触模式（即哪些手指接触哪些物体区域）。该方法通过基于学习哈希码离散化的物体状态维护接触计数器，记录各手指与不同物体区域的交互频率。该计数器通过两种互补方式被利用：（1）分配基于计数的接触覆盖奖励以促进探索新接触模式；（2）设计基于能量的接近奖励以引导智能体探索未充分覆盖的接触区域。我们在多种灵巧操作任务上评估CCGE，包括密集物体分离、受限物体抓取、手中重定向及双手操作。实验结果表明，CCGE相比现有探索方法显著提升了训练效率与成功率，且其学习的接触模式能稳健迁移至真实机器人系统。项目页面：https://contact-coverage-guided-exploration.github.io。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that dexterous manipulation lacks general-purpose reward formulations and often relies on task-specific priors. The proposed method, Contact Coverage-Guided Exploration (CCGE), represents contact states between hand keypoints and object surfaces, using a contact counter conditioned on discretized object states to encourage novel contact patterns via a count-based coverage reward and an energy-based reaching reward. Main experimental results on tasks like object singulation and in-hand reorientation show that CCGE substantially improves training efficiency and success rates over existing methods, with learned contact patterns transferring robustly to real-world robots.
本研究的动机在于灵巧操作缺乏通用奖励公式，通常依赖特定任务的手工先验。所提出的方法——接触覆盖引导探索（CCGE）——通过手部关键点与物体表面的接触状态表示，利用基于离散化物体状态的接触计数器，通过计数型覆盖奖励和基于能量的接近奖励来鼓励新颖的接触模式。在物体分离、手中重定向等任务上的主要实验结果表明，CCGE相比现有探索方法显著提高了训练效率和成功率，且学到的接触模式能鲁棒地迁移到真实机器人系统。
Safe RLHF Beyond Expectation: Stochastic Dominance for Universal Spectral Risk Control
Authors: Yaswanth Chittepu, Ativ Joshi, Rajarshi Bhattacharjee, Scott Niekum
First: 2026-03-11T16:24:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:24:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) typically enforces safety through expected cost constraints, but the expectation captures only a single statistic of the cost distribution and fails to account for distributional uncertainty, particularly under heavy tails or rare catastrophic events. This limitation is problematic when robustness and risk sensitivity are critical. Stochastic dominance offers a principled alternative by comparing entire cost distributions rather than just their averages, enabling direct control over tail risks and potential out-of-distribution failures that expectation-based constraints may overlook. In this work, we propose Risk-sensitive Alignment via Dominance (RAD), a novel alignment framework that replaces scalar expected cost constraints with First-Order Stochastic Dominance (FSD) constraints. We operationalize this constraint by comparing the target policy's cost distribution to that of a reference policy within an Optimal Transport (OT) framework, using entropic regularization and Sinkhorn iterations to obtain a differentiable and computationally efficient objective for stable end-to-end optimization. Furthermore, we introduce quantile-weighted FSD constraints and show that weighted FSD universally controls a broad class of Spectral Risk Measures (SRMs), so that improvements under weighted dominance imply guaranteed improvements in the corresponding spectral risk. This provides a principled mechanism for tuning a model's risk profile via the quantile weighting function. Empirical results demonstrate that RAD improves harmlessness over baselines while remaining competitive in helpfulness, and exhibits greater robustness on out-of-distribution harmlessness evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越期望的安全RLHF：基于随机占优的通用谱风险控制
基于人类反馈的安全强化学习（RLHF）通常通过期望成本约束来确保安全性，但期望仅捕捉成本分布的单一统计量，无法处理分布不确定性，尤其在重尾或罕见灾难性事件下。当鲁棒性和风险敏感性至关重要时，这一局限尤为突出。随机占优通过比较完整成本分布而非仅其均值，提供了一种原则性替代方案，能直接控制尾部风险及基于期望约束可能忽略的潜在分布外失效。本文提出风险敏感对齐占优（RAD），一种新颖的对齐框架，用一阶随机占优（FSD）约束替代标量期望成本约束。我们通过最优传输（OT）框架将目标策略的成本分布与参考策略进行比较，利用熵正则化和Sinkhorn迭代实现可微且计算高效的目标，以进行稳定的端到端优化。此外，我们引入分位数加权FSD约束，证明加权FSD可普遍控制一大类谱风险度量（SRM），从而在加权占优下的改进意味着相应谱风险的保证提升。这为通过分位数加权函数调整模型风险特征提供了原则性机制。实验结果表明，RAD在保持助益性竞争力的同时，较基线提升了无害性，并在分布外无害性评估中表现出更强的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of standard safe RLHF, which uses expected cost constraints that only capture a single statistic of the cost distribution and fail to account for distributional uncertainty, especially under heavy tails or rare catastrophic events, making it inadequate for critical robustness and risk sensitivity. To address this, the authors propose Risk-sensitive Alignment via Dominance (RAD), a novel alignment framework that replaces scalar expected cost constraints with First-Order Stochastic Dominance (FSD) constraints, operationalized by comparing the target policy's cost distribution to a reference policy within an Optimal Transport framework using entropic regularization and Sinkhorn iterations for differentiable and efficient optimization. The method also introduces quantile-weighted FSD constraints, showing that weighted FSD universally controls a broad class of Spectral Risk Measures, allowing principled tuning of risk profiles via the weighting function. Experimentally, RAD improves harmlessness over baselines while remaining competitive in helpfulness and exhibits greater robustness in out-of-distribution harmlessness evaluations.
本文的动机在于标准安全RLHF使用期望成本约束的局限性，该约束仅捕捉成本分布的单一统计量，无法考虑分布不确定性，特别是在重尾或罕见灾难事件下，这对于关键鲁棒性和风险敏感性不足。为解决此问题，作者提出了风险敏感对齐通过优势（RAD），一种新颖的对齐框架，用一阶随机优势（FSD）约束替代标量期望成本约束，通过在最优化传输框架内比较目标策略与参考策略的成本分布来实现，并利用熵正则化和Sinkhorn迭代实现可微分且高效的计算优化。该方法还引入了分位数加权FSD约束，表明加权FSD能普遍控制一类广泛的谱风险度量，从而通过加权函数实现风险配置的原则性调节。实验结果表明，RAD在保持帮助性竞争力的同时，相比基线提高了无害性，并在分布外无害性评估中表现出更强的鲁棒性。
Offline Dynamic Inventory and Pricing Strategy: Addressing Censored and Dependent Demand
Authors: Korel Gundem, Zhengling Qi
First: 2025-04-14T02:57:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:18:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In this paper, we study the offline sequential feature-based pricing and inventory control problem where the current demand depends on the past demand levels and any demand exceeding the available inventory is lost. Our goal is to leverage the offline dataset, consisting of past prices, ordering quantities, inventory levels, covariates, and censored sales levels, to estimate the optimal pricing and inventory control policy that maximizes long-term profit. While the underlying dynamic without censoring can be modeled by Markov decision process (MDP), the primary obstacle arises from the observed process where demand censoring is present, resulting in missing profit information, the failure of the Markov property, and a non-stationary optimal policy. To overcome these challenges, we first approximate the optimal policy by solving a high-order MDP characterized by the number of consecutive censoring instances, which ultimately boils down to solving a specialized Bellman equation tailored for this problem. Inspired by offline reinforcement learning and survival analysis, we propose two novel data-driven algorithms for solving these Bellman equations and, thus, estimate the optimal policy. Furthermore, we establish finite-sample regret bounds to validate the effectiveness of these algorithms. Finally, we conduct numerical experiments to demonstrate the efficacy of our algorithms in estimating the optimal policy. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first data-driven approach to learning optimal pricing and inventory control policies in a sequential decision-making environment characterized by censored and dependent demand. The implementations of the proposed algorithms are available at https://github.com/gundemkorel/Inventory_Pricing_Control
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线动态库存与定价策略：应对截尾与相依需求
本文研究了基于特征的离线序贯定价与库存控制问题，其中当前需求依赖于历史需求水平，且超出可用库存的需求将流失。我们的目标是通过离线数据集（包含历史价格、订购量、库存水平、协变量及截尾销售水平）来估计最大化长期利润的最优定价与库存控制策略。尽管无截尾情况下的底层动态可通过马尔可夫决策过程建模，但主要障碍源于观测过程中存在的需求截尾，这导致利润信息缺失、马尔可夫性质失效以及最优策略的非平稳性。为应对这些挑战，我们首先通过求解以连续截尾次数为特征的高阶MDP来近似最优策略，这最终归结为求解针对该问题特制的贝尔曼方程。受离线强化学习与生存分析的启发，我们提出了两种新颖的数据驱动算法来求解这些贝尔曼方程，从而估计最优策略。此外，我们建立了有限样本遗憾界以验证算法的有效性。最后，通过数值实验展示了算法在估计最优策略方面的效能。据我们所知，这是在以截尾与相依需求为特征的序贯决策环境中，首个数据驱动的学习最优定价与库存控制策略的方法。所提算法的实现代码可在 https://github.com/gundemkorel/Inventory_Pricing_Control 获取。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the offline sequential pricing and inventory control problem where demand depends on past levels and is censored when exceeding inventory, aiming to estimate an optimal policy from historical data to maximize long-term profit. The method overcomes challenges from censoring, which breaks the Markov property, by approximating the policy via a high-order Markov decision process and solving a specialized Bellman equation using novel algorithms inspired by offline reinforcement learning and survival analysis. Experimental results, supported by finite-sample regret bounds, demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed algorithms in estimating the optimal policy, marking the first data-driven approach for this censored and dependent demand setting.
本文研究了离线顺序定价和库存控制问题，其中需求依赖于历史水平且在超过库存时被截尾，目标是从历史数据中估计最优策略以最大化长期利润。方法通过高阶马尔可夫决策过程近似策略，并利用受离线强化学习和生存分析启发的新算法求解专门设计的贝尔曼方程，以克服截尾导致的马尔可夫性质失效等挑战。实验结果表明，所提算法在估计最优策略方面有效，并通过有限样本遗憾界验证，这是首个针对截尾和依赖需求环境的数据驱动方法。
Panda: A pretrained forecast model for chaotic dynamics
Authors: Jeffrey Lai, Anthony Bao, William Gilpin
First: 2025-05-19T21:59:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:51:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chaotic systems are intrinsically sensitive to small errors, challenging efforts to construct predictive data-driven models of real-world dynamical systems such as fluid flows or neuronal activity. Prior efforts comprise either specialized models trained on individual time series, or foundation models trained on vast time series databases with little underlying dynamical structure. Motivated by dynamical systems theory, we present Panda, Patched Attention for Nonlinear DynAmics. We train Panda on a novel synthetic, extensible dataset of $2 \times 10^4$ chaotic dynamical systems that we discover using an evolutionary algorithm. Trained purely on simulated data, Panda exhibits emergent properties: zero-shot forecasting of unseen chaotic systems preserving both short-term accuracy and distributional measures, nonlinear resonance patterns in attention heads, and effective prediction of real-world experimental time series. Despite having been trained only on low-dimensional ordinary differential equations, Panda spontaneously develops the ability to predict partial differential equations without retraining. We also demonstrate a neural scaling law for differential equations, underscoring the potential of pre-trained models for probing abstract mathematical domains like nonlinear dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Panda：面向混沌动力学的预训练预测模型
混沌系统对小误差具有内在敏感性，这对构建现实世界动力系统（如流体流动或神经元活动）的数据驱动预测模型提出了挑战。先前研究主要包括针对单个时间序列训练的专业模型，或基于缺乏底层动力学结构的大规模时间序列数据库训练的基础模型。受动力系统理论启发，我们提出Panda（非线性动力学的分块注意力模型）。我们在通过进化算法发现的2×10^4个混沌动力系统构成的新型可扩展合成数据集上训练Panda。该模型仅基于模拟数据训练即展现出涌现特性：对未见混沌系统进行零样本预测时能同时保持短期精度与分布度量；注意力头中呈现非线性共振模式；能有效预测真实世界实验时间序列。尽管仅基于低维常微分方程训练，Panda自发获得了无需重新训练即可预测偏微分方程的能力。我们还证明了微分方程的神经缩放定律，凸显了预训练模型在探索非线性动力学等抽象数学领域的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of predicting chaotic systems, which are sensitive to small errors and difficult to model from data, this paper introduces Panda, a pretrained forecast model based on patched attention for nonlinear dynamics. The method involves training Panda on a novel, synthetically generated dataset of 20,000 chaotic dynamical systems discovered via an evolutionary algorithm. Experimental results show that Panda exhibits emergent zero-shot forecasting capabilities on unseen chaotic systems, preserving both short-term accuracy and long-term statistical properties, predicts real-world experimental time series, and generalizes to partial differential equations despite being trained only on ordinary differential equations, while also revealing neural scaling laws for such systems.
本文针对混沌系统对微小误差敏感、难以从数据建模的预测挑战，提出了Panda，一种基于补丁注意力机制的预训练非线性动力学预测模型。该方法通过进化算法发现并生成了包含2万个混沌动力系统的合成数据集，并在此数据集上训练Panda。实验结果表明，Panda展现出涌现的零样本预测能力，能够准确预测未见混沌系统的短期动态和长期统计特性，成功预测真实世界实验时间序列，并且尽管仅基于常微分方程训练，却能泛化至偏微分方程预测，同时揭示了微分方程的神经缩放规律。
Ergodicity in reinforcement learning
Authors: Dominik Baumann, Erfaun Noorani, Arsenii Mustafin, Xinyi Sheng, Bert Verbruggen, Arne Vanhoyweghen, Vincent Ginis, Thomas B. Schön
First: 2026-03-11T15:42:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:42:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted article to appear in Philosophical Transactions of the Royal Society A: Mathematical, Physical and Engineering Sciences
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning, we typically aim to optimize the expected value of the sum of rewards an agent collects over a trajectory. However, if the process generating these rewards is non-ergodic, the expected value, i.e., the average over infinitely many trajectories with a given policy, is uninformative for the average over a single, but infinitely long trajectory. Thus, if we care about how the individual agent performs during deployment, the expected value is not a good optimization objective. In this paper, we discuss the impact of non-ergodic reward processes on reinforcement learning agents through an instructive example, relate the notion of ergodic reward processes to more widely used notions of ergodic Markov chains, and present existing solutions that optimize long-term performance of individual trajectories under non-ergodic reward dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中的遍历性
在强化学习中，我们通常旨在优化智能体在轨迹上收集的奖励总和的期望值。然而，如果生成这些奖励的过程是非遍历的，那么期望值——即给定策略下无限多条轨迹的平均值——对于单条无限长轨迹的平均值而言是无意义的。因此，如果我们关心个体智能体在部署期间的表现，期望值就不是一个良好的优化目标。本文通过一个示例性案例，探讨了非遍历奖励过程对强化学习智能体的影响，将遍历奖励过程的概念与更广泛使用的遍历马尔可夫链概念联系起来，并介绍了在非遍历奖励动态下优化个体轨迹长期性能的现有解决方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a fundamental issue in reinforcement learning where optimizing the expected sum of rewards can be misleading if the underlying reward process is non-ergodic, as it fails to reflect the performance of an individual agent over a single long trajectory. The authors motivate this by highlighting that standard expected value objectives are uninformative for deployment scenarios where agents follow one trajectory, and they relate ergodic reward processes to ergodic Markov chains to clarify the theoretical context. Through an instructive example, they illustrate the impact of non-ergodicity and present existing solutions aimed at optimizing long-term performance for individual trajectories under such dynamics, emphasizing practical relevance for agent deployment.
本文探讨了强化学习中的一个基本问题：如果底层奖励过程是非遍历的，优化奖励的期望总和可能会产生误导，因为它无法反映单个智能体在一条长轨迹上的实际性能。作者通过指出标准期望值目标在智能体部署场景中信息不足来阐述动机，并将遍历奖励过程与更广泛使用的遍历马尔可夫链概念联系起来以厘清理论背景。通过一个指导性示例，他们说明了非遍历性的影响，并介绍了现有解决方案，旨在优化非遍历奖励动态下个体轨迹的长期性能，强调了智能体部署的实际意义。
Dynamics-Predictive Sampling for Active RL Finetuning of Large Reasoning Models
Authors: Yixiu Mao, Yun Qu, Qi Wang, Heming Zou, Xiangyang Ji
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-11T15:31:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:31:14+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning has become a key technique for enhancing the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs). However, its effectiveness critically depends on the selection of training data. Recent advances underscore the importance of online prompt selection methods, which typically concentrate training on partially solved or moderately challenging examples under the current policy, thereby yielding more effective model updates. While significantly accelerating RL finetuning in terms of training steps, they also incur substantial computational overhead by requiring extensive LLM rollouts over large candidate batches to identify informative samples, an expense that can outweigh the finetuning process itself. To address this challenge, this work proposes Dynamics-Predictive Sampling (DPS), which online predicts and selects informative prompts by inferring their learning dynamics prior to costly rollouts. Specifically, we introduce a new perspective by modeling each prompt's solving progress during RL finetuning as a dynamical system, where the extent of solving is represented as the state and the transition is characterized by a hidden Markov model. Using historical rollout reward signals, we perform online Bayesian inference to estimate evolving state distributions, and the inference outcome provides a predictive prior for efficient prompt selection without rollout-intensive filtering. Empirical results across diverse reasoning tasks, including mathematics, planning, and visual geometry, demonstrate that DPS substantially reduces redundant rollouts, accelerates the training process, and achieves superior reasoning performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大型推理模型主动强化学习微调的动态预测采样
强化学习微调已成为提升大型语言模型推理能力的关键技术，但其效果高度依赖于训练数据的选择。近期研究强调在线提示选择方法的重要性，这类方法通常将训练集中在当前策略下部分解决或中等难度的样本上，从而产生更有效的模型更新。虽然这些方法在训练步数上显著加速了强化学习微调，但需要在大规模候选批次上进行大量语言模型推演以识别信息样本，由此产生的计算开销可能超过微调过程本身。为应对这一挑战，本研究提出动态预测采样方法，通过在昂贵推演前推断学习动态，在线预测并选择信息性提示。具体而言，我们引入新视角，将强化学习微调中每个提示的解决进度建模为动态系统：解决程度表征为状态，状态转移由隐马尔可夫模型刻画。利用历史推演奖励信号，我们进行在线贝叶斯推断以估计演化状态分布，推断结果为无需推演密集型筛选的高效提示选择提供预测先验。在数学、规划和视觉几何等多类推理任务上的实验结果表明，该方法显著减少了冗余推演，加速了训练过程，并实现了更优的推理性能。

This paper addresses the computational inefficiency of online prompt selection methods in reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning for large language models, which rely on extensive and costly rollouts to identify informative training data. The proposed method, Dynamics-Predictive Sampling (DPS), models each prompt's solving progress as a dynamical system using a hidden Markov model and performs online Bayesian inference on historical reward signals to predict learning dynamics, thereby enabling efficient prompt selection without rollout-intensive filtering. Experimental results across mathematics, planning, and visual geometry tasks show that DPS significantly reduces redundant rollouts, accelerates training, and achieves superior reasoning performance compared to existing approaches.
本文针对大型语言模型强化学习微调中在线提示选择方法依赖大量计算成本高昂的轨迹模拟来筛选训练数据的问题，提出了动态预测采样方法。该方法将每个提示的求解进度建模为一个动态系统，利用隐马尔可夫模型并通过历史奖励信号进行在线贝叶斯推断，从而预测学习动态，实现无需密集轨迹模拟的高效提示选择。在数学、规划和视觉几何等多种推理任务上的实验结果表明，该方法大幅减少了冗余的轨迹模拟，加速了训练过程，并取得了更优的推理性能。
Toward Closed-loop Molecular Discovery via Language Model, Property Alignment and Strategic Search
Authors: Junkai Ji, Zhangfan Yang, Dong Xu, Ruibin Bai, Jianqiang Li, Tingjun Hou, Zexuan Zhu
First: 2025-12-10T11:59:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:30:03+00:00
Comments: 30 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Drug discovery is a time-consuming and expensive process, with traditional high-throughput and docking-based virtual screening hampered by low success rates and limited scalability. Recent advances in generative modelling, including autoregressive, diffusion, and flow-based approaches, have enabled de novo ligand design beyond the limits of enumerative screening. Yet these models often suffer from inadequate generalization, limited interpretability, and an overemphasis on binding affinity at the expense of key pharmacological properties, thereby restricting their translational utility. Here we present Trio, a molecular generation framework integrating fragment-based molecular language modeling, reinforcement learning, and Monte Carlo tree search, for effective and interpretable closed-loop targeted molecular design. Through the three key components, Trio enables context-aware fragment assembly, enforces physicochemical and synthetic feasibility, and guides a balanced search between the exploration of novel chemotypes and the exploitation of promising intermediates within protein binding pockets. Experimental results show that Trio reliably achieves chemically valid and pharmacologically enhanced ligands, outperforming state-of-the-art approaches with improved binding affinity (+7.85%), drug-likeness (+11.10%) and synthetic accessibility (+12.05%), while expanding molecular diversity more than fourfold. By combining generalization, plausibility, and interpretability, Trio establishes a closed-loop generative paradigm that redefines how chemical space can be navigated, offering a transformative foundation for the next era of AI-driven drug discovery.

标题：通过语言模型、性质对齐与策略搜索实现闭环分子发现
药物发现是一个耗时且昂贵的过程，传统的高通量和基于对接的虚拟筛选受限于低成功率和有限的可扩展性。近年来，包括自回归、扩散和基于流的生成模型在内的进展，已实现超越枚举筛选限制的从头配体设计。然而，这些模型常存在泛化能力不足、可解释性有限，以及过度强调结合亲和力而忽视关键药理学性质的问题，从而限制了其转化应用。本文提出Trio，一个整合基于片段的分子语言建模、强化学习和蒙特卡洛树搜索的分子生成框架，用于高效且可解释的闭环靶向分子设计。通过三个核心组件，Trio实现了上下文感知的片段组装，强化了物理化学与合成可行性，并在探索新型化学类型与利用蛋白质结合口袋中有前景的中间体之间引导平衡搜索。实验结果表明，Trio能可靠地生成化学有效且药理学增强的配体，在结合亲和力（+7.85%）、类药性（+11.10%）和合成可及性（+12.05%）上优于现有先进方法，同时将分子多样性扩展四倍以上。通过结合泛化性、合理性与可解释性，Trio建立了一种闭环生成范式，重新定义了化学空间的探索方式，为人工智能驱动的药物发现新时代提供了变革性基础。

针对传统药物发现过程耗时昂贵且可扩展性有限的问题，本文提出了Trio框架，它整合了基于片段的分子语言建模、强化学习和蒙特卡洛树搜索，以实现闭环靶向分子设计。该方法通过上下文感知的片段组装，同时强化物理化学与合成可行性，在探索新型化学类型与利用有前景的中间体之间取得平衡。实验结果表明，Trio能可靠地生成化学有效且药理学增强的配体，在结合亲和力（+7.85%）、类药性（+11.10%）和合成可及性（+12.05%）上优于现有先进方法，并显著扩展了分子多样性。
Partially Equivariant Reinforcement Learning in Symmetry-Breaking Environments
Authors: Junwoo Chang, Minwoo Park, Joohwan Seo, Roberto Horowitz, Jongmin Lee, Jongeun Choi
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-30T14:41:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:19:35+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Group symmetries provide a powerful inductive bias for reinforcement learning (RL), enabling efficient generalization across symmetric states and actions via group-invariant Markov Decision Processes (MDPs). However, real-world environments almost never realize fully group-invariant MDPs; dynamics, actuation limits, and reward design usually break symmetries, often only locally. Under group-invariant Bellman backups for such cases, local symmetry-breaking introduces errors that propagate across the entire state-action space, resulting in global value estimation errors. To address this, we introduce Partially group-Invariant MDP (PI-MDP), which selectively applies group-invariant or standard Bellman backups depending on where symmetry holds. This framework mitigates error propagation from locally broken symmetries while maintaining the benefits of equivariance, thereby enhancing sample efficiency and generalizability. Building on this framework, we present practical RL algorithms -- Partially Equivariant (PE)-DQN for discrete control and PE-SAC for continuous control -- that combine the benefits of equivariance with robustness to symmetry-breaking. Experiments across Grid-World, locomotion, and manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that PE-DQN and PE-SAC significantly outperform baselines, highlighting the importance of selective symmetry exploitation for robust and sample-efficient RL. Project page: https://pranaboy72.github.io/perl_page/
中文标题/摘要
标题：对称性破缺环境中的部分等变强化学习
群对称性为强化学习提供了强大的归纳偏置，通过群不变马尔可夫决策过程实现对称状态与动作的高效泛化。然而，现实环境几乎从不满足完全群不变MDP；动力学、执行器限制与奖励设计常破坏对称性，且通常仅局部破缺。对此类情况采用群不变贝尔曼备份时，局部对称性破缺会引入误差并传播至整个状态-动作空间，导致全局价值估计偏差。为此，我们提出部分群不变MDP框架，根据对称性保持区域选择性应用群不变或标准贝尔曼备份。该框架在保持等变性优势的同时，缓解局部对称破缺引起的误差传播，从而提升样本效率与泛化能力。基于此框架，我们提出实用RL算法——面向离散控制的PE-DQN与面向连续控制的PE-SAC，融合等变性优势与对称破缺鲁棒性。在网格世界、运动控制与操作任务上的实验表明，PE-DQN与PE-SAC显著超越基线方法，凸显了选择性利用对称性对实现鲁棒高效强化学习的重要性。项目页面：https://pranaboy72.github.io/perl_page/
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the observation that while group symmetries offer a strong inductive bias for reinforcement learning (RL), enabling efficient generalization, real-world environments often break these symmetries locally, which can lead to global value estimation errors when using fully group-invariant methods. To address this, the authors introduce the Partially group-Invariant Markov Decision Process (PI-MDP) framework, which selectively applies group-invariant or standard Bellman backups depending on where symmetry holds, thereby mitigating error propagation from local symmetry-breaking while retaining the benefits of equivariance. The main experimental results, conducted on Grid-World, locomotion, and manipulation benchmarks, demonstrate that the proposed algorithms, PE-DQN and PE-SAC, significantly outperform baseline methods, highlighting the advantages of selective symmetry exploitation for robust and sample-efficient RL.
本研究的动机在于，尽管群对称性为强化学习提供了强大的归纳偏置以实现高效泛化，但现实环境常局部破坏这些对称性，若使用完全群不变方法会导致全局价值估计误差。为解决此问题，作者提出了部分群不变马尔可夫决策过程（PI-MDP）框架，该框架根据对称性是否成立选择性地应用群不变或标准贝尔曼备份，从而在保留等变性优势的同时减轻局部对称性破坏带来的误差传播。在网格世界、运动控制和操作任务基准上的主要实验结果表明，所提出的PE-DQN和PE-SAC算法显著优于基线方法，凸显了选择性利用对称性对于实现鲁棒且样本高效的强化学习的重要性。
$V_{0.5}$: Generalist Value Model as a Prior for Sparse RL Rollouts
Authors: Yi-Kai Zhang, Yueqing Sun, Hongyan Hao, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, De-Chuan Zhan, Han-Jia Ye
First: 2026-03-11T14:57:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:57:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), constructing a robust advantage baseline is critical for policy gradients, effectively guiding the policy model to reinforce desired behaviors. Recent research has introduced Generalist Value Models (such as $V_0$), which achieve pre-trained value estimation by explicitly encoding model capabilities in-context, eliminating the need to synchronously update the value model alongside the policy model. In this paper, we propose $V_{0.5}$, which adaptively fuses the baseline predicted by such value model (acting as a prior) with the empirical mean derived from sparse rollouts. This constructs a robust baseline that balances computational efficiency with extremely low variance. Specifically, we introduce a real-time statistical testing and dynamic budget allocation. This balances the high variance caused by sparse sampling against the systematic bias (or hallucinations) inherent in the value model's prior. By constructing a hypothesis test to evaluate the prior's reliability in real-time, the system dynamically allocates additional rollout budget on demand. This mechanism minimizes the baseline estimator's Mean Squared Error (MSE), guaranteeing stable policy gradients, even under extreme sparsity with a group size of 4. Extensive evaluations across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that $V_{0.5}$ significantly outperforms GRPO and DAPO, achieving faster convergence and over some 10% performance improvement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$V_{0.5}$：作为稀疏强化学习推演先验的通用价值模型
在可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）中，构建稳健的优势基线对策略梯度至关重要，能有效引导策略模型强化期望行为。近期研究提出的通用价值模型（如$V_0$）通过显式编码模型上下文能力实现预训练价值估计，无需与策略模型同步更新。本文提出$V_{0.5}$模型，自适应融合此类价值模型预测的基线（作为先验）与稀疏推演得到的经验均值，构建出平衡计算效率与极低方差的稳健基线。具体而言，我们引入实时统计检验与动态预算分配机制，平衡稀疏采样导致的高方差与价值模型先验固有的系统偏差（或幻觉）。通过构建假设检验实时评估先验可靠性，系统按需动态分配额外推演预算。该机制最小化基线估计器的均方误差（MSE），即使在组大小为4的极端稀疏条件下也能保证策略梯度稳定性。在六个数学推理基准上的广泛评估表明，$V_{0.5}$显著优于GRPO和DAPO，实现更快收敛与约10%的性能提升。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to improve Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) by constructing a more robust and efficient advantage baseline for policy gradients, addressing the challenge of high variance from sparse reward sampling. The method introduces $V_{0.5}$, which adaptively fuses a prior from a pre-trained Generalist Value Model with the empirical mean from sparse rollouts, using real-time statistical testing and dynamic budget allocation to balance variance and bias. The main experimental results show that $V_{0.5}$ significantly outperforms baselines like GRPO and DAPO across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks, achieving faster convergence and over 10% performance improvement even with extremely sparse group sizes of 4.
本研究的动机是通过构建更稳健高效的策略梯度优势基线来改进可验证奖励的强化学习，以解决稀疏奖励采样带来的高方差问题。方法上提出了$V_{0.5}$，它自适应地融合了预训练通用价值模型提供的先验与稀疏模拟的经验均值，并采用实时统计检验和动态预算分配来平衡方差与偏差。主要实验结果表明，在六个数学推理基准测试中，$V_{0.5}$显著优于GRPO和DAPO等基线方法，即使在组大小仅为4的极端稀疏条件下，也实现了更快的收敛和超过10%的性能提升。
Towards Cold-Start Drafting and Continual Refining: A Value-Driven Memory Approach with Application to NPU Kernel Synthesis
Authors: Yujie Zheng, Zhuo Li, Shengtao Zhang, Hanjing Wang, Junjie Sheng, Jiaqian Wang, Junchi Yan, Weinan Zhang, Ying Wen, Bo Tang, Muning Wen
First: 2026-03-11T14:57:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:57:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deploying Large Language Models to data-scarce programming domains poses significant challenges, particularly for kernel synthesis on emerging Domain-Specific Architectures where a "Data Wall" limits available training data. While models excel on data-rich platforms like CUDA, they suffer catastrophic performance drops on data-scarce ecosystems such as NPU programming. To overcome this cold-start barrier without expensive fine-tuning, we introduce EvoKernel, a self-evolving agentic framework that automates the lifecycle of kernel synthesis from initial drafting to continual refining. EvoKernel addresses this by formulating the synthesis process as a memory-based reinforcement learning task. Through a novel value-driven retrieval mechanism, it learns stage-specific Q-values that prioritize experiences based on their contribution to the current objective, whether bootstrapping a feasible draft or iteratively refining latency. Furthermore, by enabling cross-task memory sharing, the agent generalizes insights from simple to complex operators. By building an NPU variant of KernelBench and evaluating on it, EvoKernel improves frontier models' correctness from 11.0% to 83.0% and achieves a median speedup of 3.60x over initial drafts through iterative refinement. This demonstrates that value-guided experience accumulation allows general-purpose models to master the kernel synthesis task on niche hardware ecosystems. Our official page is available at https://evokernel.zhuo.li.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向冷启动草拟与持续优化的价值驱动记忆方法及其在NPU内核合成中的应用
将大语言模型部署至数据稀缺的编程领域面临重大挑战，尤其在面向新兴领域专用架构的内核合成中，"数据壁垒"严重限制了可用训练数据。虽然模型在CUDA等数据丰富的平台上表现优异，但在NPU编程等数据稀缺生态系统中性能会急剧下降。为在不依赖昂贵微调的情况下突破冷启动障碍，我们提出了EvoKernel——一种自进化的智能体框架，实现了从初始草拟到持续优化的内核合成全生命周期自动化。该框架将合成过程构建为基于记忆的强化学习任务，通过创新的价值驱动检索机制，学习阶段特定的Q值函数，根据经验对当前目标（无论是引导可行草案生成还是迭代优化延迟）的贡献度进行优先级排序。此外，通过跨任务记忆共享机制，智能体能将简单算子的经验泛化至复杂算子。通过构建KernelBench的NPU变体并开展评估，EvoKernel将前沿模型的正确率从11.0%提升至83.0%，并通过迭代优化使中位加速比达到初始草案的3.60倍。这表明价值引导的经验积累能使通用模型掌握小众硬件生态系统的内核合成任务。项目主页：https://evokernel.zhuo.li。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of deploying Large Language Models for kernel synthesis on emerging Domain-Specific Architectures like NPUs, where scarce training data causes catastrophic performance drops. To overcome this cold-start barrier without costly fine-tuning, the authors propose EvoKernel, a self-evolving agentic framework that formulates synthesis as a memory-based reinforcement learning task, using a value-driven retrieval mechanism to prioritize experiences for drafting or refining kernels and enabling cross-task memory sharing. Experimental results on an NPU variant of KernelBench show that EvoKernel improves model correctness from 11.0% to 83.0% and achieves a median speedup of 3.60x over initial drafts through iterative refinement, demonstrating that value-guided experience accumulation enables general-purpose models to master kernel synthesis on niche hardware.
该论文针对在如NPU等新兴领域特定架构上部署大语言模型进行内核合成时，因训练数据稀缺导致性能急剧下降的挑战。为在不进行昂贵微调的情况下克服这一冷启动障碍，作者提出了EvoKernel，一个自演化的智能体框架，将合成过程建模为基于记忆的强化学习任务，通过一种价值驱动的检索机制，根据经验对当前目标（如引导可行草案或迭代优化延迟）的贡献进行优先级排序，并支持跨任务记忆共享。在NPU版本的KernelBench上的实验结果表明，EvoKernel将模型正确率从11.0%提升至83.0%，并通过迭代优化实现了相对于初始草案中位数3.60倍的加速，证明了价值引导的经验积累能使通用模型掌握小众硬件上的内核合成任务。
LexiSafe: Offline Safe Reinforcement Learning with Lexicographic Safety-Reward Hierarchy
Authors: Hsin-Jung Yang, Zhanhong Jiang, Prajwal Koirala, Qisai Liu, Cody Fleming, Soumik Sarkar
First: 2026-02-19T12:22:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:41:41+00:00
Comments: 17th ACM/IEEE International Conference on Cyber-Physical Systems
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline safe reinforcement learning (RL) is increasingly important for cyber-physical systems (CPS), where safety violations during training are unacceptable and only pre-collected data are available. Existing offline safe RL methods typically balance reward-safety tradeoffs through constraint relaxation or joint optimization, but they often lack structural mechanisms to prevent safety drift. We propose LexiSafe, a lexicographic offline RL framework designed to preserve safety-aligned behavior. We first develop LexiSafe-SC, a single-cost formulation for standard offline safe RL, and derive safety-violation and performance-suboptimality bounds that together yield sample-complexity guarantees. We then extend the framework to hierarchical safety requirements with LexiSafe-MC, which supports multiple safety costs and admits its own sample-complexity analysis. Empirically, LexiSafe demonstrates reduced safety violations and improved task performance compared to constrained offline baselines. By unifying lexicographic prioritization with structural bias, LexiSafe offers a practical and theoretically grounded approach for safety-critical CPS decision-making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LexiSafe：基于词典序安全-奖励层级的离线安全强化学习
离线安全强化学习对信息物理系统日益重要，因其训练过程不允许出现安全违规，且仅能使用预收集数据。现有方法通常通过约束松弛或联合优化平衡奖励与安全，但缺乏防止安全漂移的结构化机制。本文提出词典序离线强化学习框架LexiSafe，旨在保持安全对齐行为。首先构建单成本模型LexiSafe-SC，推导出安全违规与性能次优性边界，共同形成样本复杂度保证。随后扩展为多安全成本框架LexiSafe-MC，支持层级安全需求并具备独立样本复杂度分析。实验表明，相比约束基线方法，LexiSafe能减少安全违规并提升任务性能。该框架通过词典序优先级与结构化偏差的统一，为安全关键信息物理系统决策提供兼具实用性与理论依据的解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LexiSafe, an offline safe reinforcement learning framework motivated by the need to ensure safety in cyber-physical systems where training must avoid real-world violations and rely solely on pre-collected data. The method employs a lexicographic hierarchy to prioritize safety over reward, with LexiSafe-SC handling single safety costs and LexiSafe-MC extending to multiple safety requirements, both supported by theoretical sample-complexity guarantees. Experimental results show that LexiSafe reduces safety violations and improves task performance compared to existing constrained offline baselines, offering a practical solution for safety-critical decision-making.
本文提出了LexiSafe，一种离线安全强化学习框架，其动机在于确保网络物理系统的安全性，其中训练必须避免现实世界中的违规行为并仅依赖预先收集的数据。该方法采用词典序层次结构，将安全性置于奖励之上，LexiSafe-SC处理单一安全成本，LexiSafe-MC扩展至多重安全需求，两者均得到理论样本复杂度保证的支持。实验结果表明，与现有的约束离线基线方法相比，LexiSafe减少了安全违规并提升了任务性能，为安全关键决策提供了实用解决方案。
ReTabSyn: Realistic Tabular Data Synthesis via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaofeng Lin, Seungbae Kim, Zhuoya Li, Zachary DeSoto, Charles Fleming, Guang Cheng
First: 2026-03-11T14:31:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:31:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep generative models can help with data scarcity and privacy by producing synthetic training data, but they struggle in low-data, imbalanced tabular settings to fully learn the complex data distribution. We argue that striving for the full joint distribution could be overkill; for greater data efficiency, models should prioritize learning the conditional distribution $P(y\mid \bm{X})$, as suggested by recent theoretical analysis. Therefore, we overcome this limitation with \textbf{ReTabSyn}, a \textbf{Re}inforced \textbf{Tab}ular \textbf{Syn}thesis pipeline that provides direct feedback on feature correlation preservation during synthesizer training. This objective encourages the generator to prioritize the most useful predictive signals when training data is limited, thereby strengthening downstream model utility. We empirically fine-tune a language model-based generator using this approach, and across benchmarks with small sample sizes, class imbalance, and distribution shift, ReTabSyn consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. Moreover, our approach can be readily extended to control various aspects of synthetic tabular data, such as applying expert-specified constraints on generated observations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReTabSyn：基于强化学习的真实表格数据合成
深度生成模型可通过生成合成训练数据缓解数据稀缺与隐私问题，但在低数据量、不平衡的表格场景中难以完整学习复杂数据分布。我们认为追求完整联合分布可能过度；为提高数据效率，模型应优先学习条件分布 $P(y\mid \bm{X})$（近期理论分析支持此观点）。为此，我们提出 \textbf{ReTabSyn}——一种基于\textbf{强化学习}的\textbf{表格数据合成}流程，在合成器训练期间直接反馈特征相关性保持情况。该目标促使生成器在训练数据有限时优先学习最具预测价值的信号，从而增强下游模型效用。我们采用此方法对基于语言模型的生成器进行实证微调，在小样本量、类别不平衡及分布偏移的基准测试中，ReTabSyn 均持续优于前沿基线方法。此外，本方法可轻松扩展至控制合成表格数据的多维度属性，例如对生成观测值施加专家指定的约束条件。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of deep generative models in low-data, imbalanced tabular settings where learning the full joint distribution is inefficient, this paper proposes ReTabSyn, a reinforced tabular synthesis pipeline that prioritizes learning the conditional distribution P(y|X) to enhance data efficiency. The method employs reinforcement learning to provide direct feedback on feature correlation preservation during generator training, encouraging the model to focus on the most useful predictive signals. Experimental results on benchmarks with small sample sizes, class imbalance, and distribution shift show that ReTabSyn consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in downstream utility and can be extended to apply expert constraints on synthetic data.
针对深度生成模型在低数据、不平衡的表格数据场景中难以有效学习完整联合分布的问题，本文提出了ReTabSyn，一种基于强化学习的表格数据合成流程，其动机是通过优先学习条件分布P(y|X)来提高数据效率。该方法在生成器训练过程中利用强化学习直接反馈特征相关性保持情况，促使模型专注于最有用的预测信号。在小型样本、类别不平衡和分布偏移的基准测试中，实验结果表明ReTabSyn在提升下游模型性能方面持续优于现有先进方法，并且该方法易于扩展以对合成数据施加专家指定的约束。
Mindstorms in Natural Language-Based Societies of Mind
Authors: Mingchen Zhuge, Haozhe Liu, Francesco Faccio, Dylan R. Ashley, Róbert Csordás, Anand Gopalakrishnan, Abdullah Hamdi, Hasan Abed Al Kader Hammoud, Vincent Herrmann, Kazuki Irie, Louis Kirsch, Bing Li, Guohao Li, Shuming Liu, Jinjie Mai, Piotr Piękos, Aditya Ramesh, Imanol Schlag, Weimin Shi, Aleksandar Stanić, Wenyi Wang, Yuhui Wang, Mengmeng Xu, Deng-Ping Fan, Bernard Ghanem, Jürgen Schmidhuber
Venue: (2025). Computational Visual Media, 11(1), 29-81
First: 2023-05-26T16:21:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T13:43:31+00:00
Comments: published in Computational Visual Media Journal (CVMJ); 9 pages in main text + 7 pages of references + 38 pages of appendices, 14 figures in main text + 13 in appendices, 7 tables in appendices
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Both Minsky's "society of mind" and Schmidhuber's "learning to think" inspire diverse societies of large multimodal neural networks (NNs) that solve problems by interviewing each other in a "mindstorm." Recent implementations of NN-based societies of minds consist of large language models (LLMs) and other NN-based experts communicating through a natural language interface. In doing so, they overcome the limitations of single LLMs, improving multimodal zero-shot reasoning. In these natural language-based societies of mind (NLSOMs), new agents -- all communicating through the same universal symbolic language -- are easily added in a modular fashion. To demonstrate the power of NLSOMs, we assemble and experiment with several of them (having up to 129 members), leveraging mindstorms in them to solve some practical AI tasks: visual question answering, image captioning, text-to-image synthesis, 3D generation, egocentric retrieval, embodied AI, and general language-based task solving. We view this as a starting point towards much larger NLSOMs with billions of agents-some of which may be humans. And with this emergence of great societies of heterogeneous minds, many new research questions have suddenly become paramount to the future of artificial intelligence. What should be the social structure of an NLSOM? What would be the (dis)advantages of having a monarchical rather than a democratic structure? How can principles of NN economies be used to maximize the total reward of a reinforcement learning NLSOM? In this work, we identify, discuss, and try to answer some of these questions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自然语言的思维社会中的思维风暴
明斯基的“思维社会”与施密德胡伯的“学会思考”理论共同启发了由大型多模态神经网络构成的多样化社会系统，这些网络通过“思维风暴”相互访谈来解决问题。近期基于神经网络的思维社会实现方案，主要依赖大型语言模型及其他神经网络专家通过自然语言接口进行交互。这种方式突破了单一大型语言模型的局限，提升了多模态零样本推理能力。在这些基于自然语言的思维社会中，所有智能体通过统一的符号语言进行通信，新成员能以模块化方式便捷加入。为展示此类系统的能力，我们构建并实验了多个系统（最多包含129个成员），利用其中的思维风暴解决实际人工智能任务：视觉问答、图像描述、文本到图像合成、3D生成、第一视角检索、具身人工智能及通用语言任务处理。我们视此为构建数十亿智能体（部分可能为人类）的超大规模思维社会的起点。随着这种异构思维巨社会的涌现，许多新研究课题对人工智能的未来发展至关重要：NLSOM应采用何种社会结构？君主制与民主制结构各有何优劣？如何运用神经网络经济学原理最大化强化学习NLSOM的总收益？本研究针对这些问题进行了识别、讨论与初步解答。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by Minsky's and Schmidhuber's theories of collective intelligence, this paper proposes Natural Language-Based Societies of Mind (NLSOMs), which are modular assemblies of diverse neural networks, including large language models, that communicate via natural language to overcome the limitations of single models. The method involves constructing societies with up to 129 member agents that engage in collaborative "mindstorm" dialogues to solve tasks. Experimental results demonstrate improved multimodal zero-shot reasoning across a range of practical AI tasks, including visual question answering, image captioning, text-to-image synthesis, 3D generation, egocentric retrieval, embodied AI, and general language-based problem solving. The work also explores critical research questions about optimal social structures and reward economies within such societies, viewing this as a foundational step toward future large-scale heterogeneous systems.
受明斯基和施密德胡贝尔的集体智能理论启发，本文提出了基于自然语言的心智社会（NLSOMs），即通过自然语言进行通信的、包含大型语言模型在内的多种神经网络的模块化组合，以克服单一模型的局限性。其方法在于构建最多包含129个成员代理的社会，这些代理通过协作性的“思维风暴”对话来解决问题。实验结果表明，该系统在多种实际AI任务中提升了多模态零样本推理能力，包括视觉问答、图像描述、文本到图像合成、3D生成、以自我为中心的检索、具身AI和基于语言的通用任务求解。该工作还探讨了关于此类社会最优组织结构与奖励机制的关键研究问题，将其视为迈向未来大规模异构系统的基础一步。
Learning Tree-Based Models with Gradient Descent
Authors: Sascha Marton
First: 2026-03-11T13:43:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T13:43:16+00:00
Comments: PhD thesis
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tree-based models are widely recognized for their interpretability and have proven effective in various application domains, particularly in high-stakes domains. However, learning decision trees (DTs) poses a significant challenge due to their combinatorial complexity and discrete, non-differentiable nature. As a result, traditional methods such as CART, which rely on greedy search procedures, remain the most widely used approaches. These methods make locally optimal decisions at each node, constraining the search space and often leading to suboptimal tree structures. Additionally, their demand for custom training methods precludes a seamless integration into modern machine learning (ML) approaches. In this thesis, we propose a novel method for learning hard, axis-aligned DTs through gradient descent. Our approach utilizes backpropagation with a straight-through operator on a dense DT representation, enabling the joint optimization of all tree parameters, thereby addressing the two primary limitations of traditional DT algorithms. First, gradient-based training is not constrained by the sequential selection of locally optimal splits but, instead, jointly optimizes all tree parameters. Second, by leveraging gradient descent for optimization, our approach seamlessly integrates into existing ML approaches e.g., for multimodal and reinforcement learning tasks, which inherently rely on gradient descent. These advancements allow us to achieve state-of-the-art results across multiple domains, including interpretable DTs rees for small tabular datasets, advanced models for complex tabular data, multimodal learning, and interpretable reinforcement learning without information loss. By bridging the gap between DTs and gradient-based optimization, our method significantly enhances the performance and applicability of tree-based models across various ML domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于梯度下降的树模型学习方法
树模型因其可解释性而广受认可，并在多个应用领域（尤其是高风险领域）展现出显著效果。然而，决策树（DTs）的组合复杂性与离散、不可微的特性使其学习过程面临重大挑战。因此，依赖贪婪搜索的传统方法（如CART）仍是当前主流方法。这些方法在节点层面进行局部最优决策，限制了搜索空间并常导致次优树结构。此外，其定制化训练需求阻碍了与现代机器学习（ML）方法的无缝集成。 本论文提出一种通过梯度下降学习硬性轴对齐决策树的新方法。该方法在密集DT表示上结合直通算子进行反向传播，实现所有树参数的联合优化，从而解决传统DT算法的两大局限：其一，基于梯度的训练不受局部最优分割顺序的约束，可同步优化所有参数；其二，通过梯度下降优化，本方法能无缝集成至依赖梯度下降的现有ML框架（如多模态与强化学习任务）。 这些突破使我们在多个领域取得先进成果，包括：针对小型表格数据的可解释DT、复杂表格数据的高级模型、多模态学习，以及无损可解释强化学习。通过弥合DT与梯度优化之间的鸿沟，本方法显著提升了树模型在各类ML领域的性能与适用性。

The proposed method learns hard, axis-aligned decision trees via gradient descent by using backpropagation with a straight-through operator on a dense representation, enabling joint optimization of all tree parameters and seamless integration into modern machine learning pipelines. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance across domains, including interpretable trees for tabular data, multimodal learning, and reinforcement learning, significantly enhancing the applicability of tree-based models.

To Mix or To Merge: Toward Multi-Domain Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models
Authors: Haoqing Wang, Xiang Long, Ziheng Li, Yilong Xu, Tingguang Li, Yehui Tang
First: 2026-02-13T03:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T12:27:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) plays a key role in stimulating the explicit reasoning capability of Large Language Models (LLMs). We can achieve expert-level performance in some specific domains via RLVR, such as coding or math. When a general multi-domain expert-level model is required, we need to carefully consider the collaboration of RLVR across different domains. The current state-of-the-art models mainly employ two different training paradigms for multi-domain RLVR: mixed multi-task RLVR and separate RLVR followed by model merging. However, most of the works did not provide a detailed comparison and analysis about these paradigms. To this end, we choose multiple commonly used high-level tasks (e.g., math, coding, science, instruction following, and agent) as our target domains and design extensive qualitative and quantitative experiments using open-source datasets. We find the RLVR across domains exhibits few mutual interferences, and reasoning-intensive domains demonstrate mutually synergistic effects. Furthermore, we analyze the internal mechanisms of mutual gains from the perspectives of weight space geometry, information constraints, model prediction behavior and self-verification. This project is named as M2RL that means Mixed multi-task training or separate training followed by model Merging for Reinforcement Learning, and the homepage is at https://github.com/Mosi-AI/M2RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合还是合并：迈向大语言模型的多领域强化学习
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在激发大语言模型（LLMs）的显式推理能力方面起着关键作用。通过RLVR，我们能在特定领域（如编程或数学）实现专家级性能。当需要通用的多领域专家级模型时，需审慎考虑RLVR在不同领域间的协同机制。当前最先进的模型主要采用两种多领域RLVR训练范式：混合多任务RLVR与独立RLVR后模型合并。然而，现有研究大多未对这两种范式进行系统比较分析。为此，我们选取数学、编程、科学、指令遵循及智能体等常见高阶任务作为目标领域，基于开源数据集设计了系统的定性与定量实验。研究发现：跨领域RLVR存在较少相互干扰，推理密集型领域间呈现协同增强效应。进一步从权重空间几何、信息约束、模型预测行为及自我验证等维度，深入解析了跨领域增益的内在机制。本项目命名为M2RL（意为“混合多任务训练或独立训练后模型合并的强化学习”），项目主页位于https://github.com/Mosi-AI/M2RL。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the optimal training paradigm for achieving multi-domain expert-level performance in large language models (LLMs) using Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). The motivation stems from the need to understand how to best combine RLVR training across diverse domains like math, coding, and science, comparing the prevalent paradigms of mixed multi-task training versus separate training followed by model merging. Through extensive experiments on open-source datasets, the method reveals that RLVR across domains exhibits minimal mutual interference and that reasoning-intensive domains can even demonstrate synergistic effects, enhancing each other's performance. The main experimental results are further analyzed by examining internal mechanisms such as weight space geometry and model prediction behavior, providing insights into the mutual gains observed.
本文研究了如何利用可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型（LLMs）中实现多领域专家级性能的最佳训练范式。其动机源于需要理解如何最好地结合数学、编程和科学等不同领域的RLVR训练，比较了混合多任务训练与分别训练后模型合并这两种主流范式。通过在开源数据集上进行大量实验，该方法发现跨领域的RLVR训练相互干扰很小，且推理密集型领域甚至表现出协同效应，能相互提升性能。主要实验结果通过分析权重空间几何、模型预测行为等内部机制得到进一步阐释，为观察到的相互增益提供了见解。
Position: Beyond Model-Centric Prediction -- Agentic Time Series Forecasting
Authors: Mingyue Cheng, Xiaoyu Tao, Qi Liu, Ze Guo, Enhong Chen
First: 2026-02-02T08:01:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T11:27:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Time series forecasting has traditionally been formulated as a model-centric, static, and single-pass prediction problem that maps historical observations to future values. While this paradigm has driven substantial progress, it proves insufficient in adaptive and multi-turn settings where forecasting requires informative feature extraction, reasoning-driven inference, iterative refinement, and continual adaptation over time. In this paper, we argue for agentic time series forecasting (ATSF), which reframes forecasting as an agentic process composed of perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory. Rather than focusing solely on predictive models, ATSF emphasizes organizing forecasting as an agentic workflow that can interact with tools, incorporate feedback from outcomes, and evolve through experience accumulation. We outline three representative implementation paradigms -- workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid agentic workflow paradigm -- and discuss the opportunities and challenges that arise when shifting from model-centric prediction to agentic forecasting. Together, this position aims to establish agentic forecasting as a foundation for future research at the intersection of time series forecasting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：观点：超越模型中心预测——智能体时间序列预测
时间序列预测传统上被构建为一个模型中心、静态、单次执行的预测问题，即将历史观测值映射为未来值。尽管这一范式推动了显著进展，但在需要信息特征提取、推理驱动推断、迭代优化以及持续时域适应的自适应多轮场景中，其局限性日益凸显。本文提出智能体时间序列预测（ATSF）框架，将预测重构为由感知、规划、行动、反思与记忆构成的智能体过程。ATSF不仅关注预测模型，更强调将预测组织为可与工具交互、整合结果反馈、通过经验积累进化的智能体工作流。我们概述了三种典型实现范式——基于工作流的设计、智能体强化学习及混合智能体工作流范式，并探讨了从模型中心预测转向智能体预测所面临的机遇与挑战。本观点旨在将智能体预测确立为时间序列预测交叉领域未来研究的基石。

The method emphasizes organizing forecasting as an interactive workflow that can utilize tools, incorporate feedback, and evolve through experience, outlining three implementation paradigms: workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid agentic workflow. The main experimental results are not detailed as this is a conceptual position paper, but it discusses the opportunities and challenges of shifting to agentic forecasting to establish a foundation for future research.
本文的动机在于传统以模型为中心、单次预测的方法在自适应和多轮预测场景中存在不足，因此主张将时间序列预测重构为一种智能体过程，即智能体时间序列预测（ATSF），该过程包含感知、规划、行动、反思和记忆。方法上强调将预测组织为可交互的工作流程，能够利用工具、整合反馈并通过经验积累不断演进，概述了三种实现范式：基于工作流的设计、智能体强化学习以及混合智能体工作流。由于这是一篇概念性立场论文，未详述具体实验结果，但讨论了从模型中心预测转向智能体预测所带来的机遇与挑战，旨在为未来研究奠定基础。
ResWM: Residual-Action World Model for Visual RL
Authors: Jseen Zhang, Gabriel Adineera, Jinzhou Tan, Jinoh Kim
First: 2026-03-11T11:27:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T11:27:08+00:00
Comments: Submit KDD2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning predictive world models from raw visual observations is a central challenge in reinforcement learning (RL), especially for robotics and continuous control. Conventional model-based RL frameworks directly condition future predictions on absolute actions, which makes optimization unstable: the optimal action distributions are task-dependent, unknown a priori, and often lead to oscillatory or inefficient control. To address this, we introduce the Residual-Action World Model (ResWM), a new framework that reformulates the control variable from absolute actions to residual actions -- incremental adjustments relative to the previous step. This design aligns with the inherent smoothness of real-world control, reduces the effective search space, and stabilizes long-horizon planning. To further strengthen the representation, we propose an Observation Difference Encoder that explicitly models the changes between adjacent frames, yielding compact latent dynamics that are naturally coupled with residual actions. ResWM is integrated into a Dreamer-style latent dynamics model with minimal modifications and no extra hyperparameters. Both imagination rollouts and policy optimization are conducted in the residual-action space, enabling smoother exploration, lower control variance, and more reliable planning. Empirical results on the DeepMind Control Suite demonstrate that ResWM achieves consistent improvements in sample efficiency, asymptotic returns, and control smoothness, significantly surpassing strong baselines such as Dreamer and TD-MPC. Beyond performance, ResWM produces more stable and energy-efficient action trajectories, a property critical for robotic systems deployed in real-world environments. These findings suggest that residual action modeling provides a simple yet powerful principle for bridging algorithmic advances in RL with the practical requirements of robotics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ResWM：面向视觉强化学习的残差动作世界模型
从原始视觉观测中学习预测性世界模型是强化学习（RL）的核心挑战，在机器人学和连续控制领域尤为突出。传统基于模型的RL框架直接将未来预测条件建立在绝对动作上，这导致优化不稳定：最优动作分布具有任务依赖性、先验未知性，且常引发振荡或低效控制。为此，我们提出残差动作世界模型（ResWM），该框架将控制变量从绝对动作重构为残差动作——即相对于上一步的增量调整。该设计契合现实世界控制固有的平滑性，缩减有效搜索空间，并稳定长时程规划。为增强表征能力，我们进一步提出观测差分编码器，显式建模相邻帧间的变化，生成与残差动作自然耦合的紧凑潜在动态。ResWM以最小修改且无需额外超参数的方式集成至Dreamer式潜在动态模型中。想象推演与策略优化均在残差动作空间进行，从而实现更平滑的探索、更低的控制方差及更可靠的规划。在DeepMind控制套件上的实验表明，ResWM在样本效率、渐进回报与控制平滑性上均取得稳定提升，显著超越Dreamer、TD-MPC等强基线。除性能优势外，ResWM生成的动作轨迹更稳定且能效更高，这对实际部署的机器人系统至关重要。这些发现表明，残差动作建模为连接RL算法进展与机器人实践需求提供了简洁而有效的原理。

It proposes ResWM, a residual-action world model that reformulates control as incremental adjustments relative to previous actions, aligning with real-world smoothness and reducing search space; this is enhanced by an Observation Difference Encoder to capture frame changes for compact latent dynamics.
