CARE: Towards Clinical Accountability in Multi-Modal Medical Reasoning with an Evidence-Grounded Agentic Framework
Authors: Yuexi Du, Jinglu Wang, Shujie Liu, Nicha C. Dvornek, Yan Lu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T08:38:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T10:41:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Large visual language models (VLMs) have shown strong multi-modal medical reasoning ability, but most operate as end-to-end black boxes, diverging from clinicians' evidence-based, staged workflows and hindering clinical accountability. Complementarily, expert visual grounding models can accurately localize regions of interest (ROIs), providing explicit, reliable evidence that improves both reasoning accuracy and trust. In this paper, we introduce CARE, advancing Clinical Accountability in multi-modal medical Reasoning with an Evidence-grounded agentic framework. Unlike existing approaches that couple grounding and reasoning within a single generalist model, CARE decomposes the task into coordinated sub-modules to reduce shortcut learning and hallucination: a compact VLM proposes relevant medical entities; an expert entity-referring segmentation model produces pixel-level ROI evidence; and a grounded VLM reasons over the full image augmented by ROI hints. The VLMs are optimized with reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards to align answers with supporting evidence. Furthermore, a VLM coordinator plans tool invocation and reviews evidence-answer consistency, providing agentic control and final verification. Evaluated on standard medical VQA benchmarks, our CARE-Flow (coordinator-free) improves average accuracy by 10.9% over the same size (10B) state-of-the-art (SOTA). With dynamic planning and answer review, our CARE-Coord yields a further gain, outperforming the heavily pre-trained SOTA by 5.2%. Our experiments demonstrate that an agentic framework that emulates clinical workflows, incorporating decoupled specialized models and explicit evidence, yields more accurate and accountable medical AI. Project page: https://xypb.github.io/CARE-Project-Page/
中文标题/摘要
标题：CARE：基于证据驱动的智能体框架实现多模态医学推理的临床可问责性
大型视觉语言模型（VLM）已展现出强大的多模态医学推理能力，但多数模型作为端到端黑箱运行，与临床医生基于证据的分阶段工作流程相悖，且阻碍了临床可问责性。互补性地，专家视觉定位模型能精准定位感兴趣区域（ROI），提供显式可靠的证据，既提升推理准确性也增强可信度。本文提出CARE框架，通过证据驱动的智能体架构推进多模态医学推理的临床可问责性。与现有将定位与推理耦合在单一通用模型中的方法不同，CARE将任务分解为协同子模块以减少捷径学习与幻觉：紧凑型VLM提出相关医学实体；专家实体指代分割模型生成像素级ROI证据；基于证据的VLM结合ROI提示对完整图像进行推理。通过可验证奖励的强化学习优化VLM，使答案与支撑证据对齐。此外，VLM协调器规划工具调用并核查证据-答案一致性，提供智能体控制与最终验证。在标准医学VQA基准测试中，CARE-Flow（无协调器版）较同规模（100亿参数）前沿模型平均准确率提升10.9%；具备动态规划与答案审查的CARE-Coord进一步获得增益，超越强预训练前沿模型5.2%。实验表明，模拟临床工作流程、融合解耦专用模型与显式证据的智能体框架能产生更精准、可问责的医学人工智能。项目页面：https://xypb.github.io/CARE-Project-Page/

Motivated by the need to align AI with clinicians' evidence-based workflows for better accountability, this paper introduces CARE, an agentic framework that decomposes multi-modal medical reasoning into specialized modules to reduce hallucinations. The method employs a compact VLM to propose medical entities, an expert segmentation model to localize pixel-level evidence, and a grounded VLM to reason over image regions, all optimized with reinforcement learning using verifiable rewards and coordinated by a planning module for consistency. 本研究旨在使AI与临床医生基于证据的工作流程对齐，以提升临床问责性，提出了CARE框架，该框架通过分解多模态医学推理任务为专门模块来减少幻觉。方法采用紧凑视觉语言模型提出医学实体，专家分割模型定位像素级证据，以及基于证据的视觉语言模型进行区域推理，并通过可验证奖励的强化学习进行优化，由协调模块规划工具调用并审查证据一致性。在医学视觉问答基准测试中，CARE-Flow相比同等规模的先进模型平均准确率提升10.9%，而具备动态规划的CARE-Coord进一步超越强预训练先进模型5.2%，证明了通过显式证据基础能提高准确性和问责性。
Reinforcement Learning with Conditional Expectation Reward
Authors: Changyi Xiao, Caijun Xu, Yixin Cao
First: 2026-03-11T10:36:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T10:36:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has proven effective in enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models, particularly in domains such as mathematics where reliable rule-based verifiers can be constructed. However, the reliance on handcrafted, domain-specific verification rules substantially limits the applicability of RLVR to general reasoning domains with free-form answers, where valid answers often exhibit significant variability, making it difficult to establish complete and accurate rules. To address this limitation, we propose Conditional Expectation Reward (CER), which leverages the large language model itself as an implicit verifier, and is therefore applicable to general domains and eliminates the need for external verifiers or auxiliary models. CER is defined as the expected likelihood of generating the reference answer conditioned on the generated answer. In contrast to rule-based verifiers that yield binary feedback, CER provides a soft, graded reward signal that reflects varying degrees of correctness, making it better suited to tasks where answers vary in correctness. Experimental results demonstrate that CER is effective across a wide range of reasoning tasks, spanning both mathematical and general domains, indicating that CER serves as a flexible and general verification mechanism. The code is available at https://github.com/changyi7231/CER.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件期望奖励的强化学习
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）已被证明能有效提升大语言模型的推理能力，尤其在数学等可构建可靠规则验证器的领域。然而，该方法依赖人工构建的领域特定验证规则，极大限制了其在自由形式答案的通用推理领域的适用性——这类场景中有效答案通常存在显著差异，难以建立完备准确的规则。为突破此局限，我们提出条件期望奖励（CER），其利用大语言模型自身作为隐式验证器，从而适用于通用领域，且无需外部验证器或辅助模型。CER定义为在生成答案条件下产生参考答案的期望似然。相较于产生二元反馈的规则验证器，CER提供反映不同程度正确性的软性分级奖励信号，更适用于答案正确性存在差异的任务。实验结果表明，CER在数学与通用领域的广泛推理任务中均表现有效，表明其可作为灵活通用的验证机制。代码发布于 https://github.com/changyi7231/CER。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitation of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which relies on handcrafted, domain-specific verification rules and is thus not applicable to general reasoning domains with free-form, variable answers. The proposed method, Conditional Expectation Reward (CER), uses the large language model itself as an implicit verifier by defining the reward as the expected likelihood of generating a reference answer conditioned on the model's generated answer, providing a soft, graded signal instead of binary feedback. Experimental results show that CER is effective across a wide range of reasoning tasks, including both mathematical and general domains, demonstrating its flexibility as a general verification mechanism.
本研究的动机是克服可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的局限性，该方法依赖手工制作的领域特定验证规则，因此不适用于答案自由多变的一般推理领域。所提出的方法，条件期望奖励（CER），利用大语言模型本身作为隐式验证器，将奖励定义为在模型生成答案的条件下生成参考答案的期望似然，从而提供软性的、分级的反馈信号，而非二元判断。实验结果表明，CER在包括数学和一般领域在内的广泛推理任务中均有效，证明了其作为一种通用验证机制的灵活性。
Does LLM Alignment Really Need Diversity? An Empirical Study of Adapting RLVR Methods for Moral Reasoning
Authors: Zhaowei Zhang, Xiaohan Liu, Xuekai Zhu, Junchao Huang, Ceyao Zhang, Zhiyuan Feng, Yaodong Yang, Xiaoyuan Yi, Xing Xie
First: 2026-03-11T09:45:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T09:45:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has achieved remarkable success in logical reasoning tasks, yet whether large language model (LLM) alignment requires fundamentally different approaches remains unclear. Given the apparent tolerance for multiple valid responses in moral reasoning, a natural hypothesis is that alignment tasks inherently require diversity-seeking distribution-matching algorithms rather than reward-maximizing policy-based methods. We conduct the first comprehensive empirical study comparing both paradigms on MoReBench. To enable stable RLVR training, we build a rubric-grounded reward pipeline by training a Qwen3-1.7B judge model. Contrary to our hypothesis, we find that distribution-matching approaches do not demonstrate significant advantages over reward-maximizing methods as expected on alignment tasks. Through semantic visualization mapping high-reward responses to semantic space, we demonstrate that moral reasoning exhibits more concentrated high-reward distributions than mathematical reasoning, where diverse solution strategies yield similarly high rewards. This counter-intuitive finding explains why mode-seeking optimization proves equally or more effective for alignment tasks. Our results suggest that alignment tasks do not inherently require diversity-preserving algorithms, and standard reward-maximizing RLVR methods can effectively transfer to moral reasoning without explicit diversity mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LLM对齐真的需要多样性吗？一项关于将RLVR方法应用于道德推理的实证研究
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在逻辑推理任务中取得了显著成功，但大型语言模型（LLM）对齐是否需要根本不同的方法仍不明确。鉴于道德推理对多种有效回答的明显包容性，一个自然假设是对齐任务本质上需要寻求多样性的分布匹配算法，而非基于奖励最大化的策略方法。我们在MoReBench上首次进行了全面实证研究，比较这两种范式。为实现稳定的RLVR训练，我们通过训练Qwen3-1.7B评判模型构建了基于量规的奖励管道。与假设相反，我们发现分布匹配方法在对齐任务中并未如预期般展现出显著优于奖励最大化方法的优势。通过将高奖励回答映射到语义空间的语义可视化，我们证明道德推理的高奖励分布比数学推理更为集中，而后者中多样化的解决策略能产生相似的高奖励。这一反直觉的发现解释了为何寻求模态的优化方法在对齐任务中同样或更为有效。我们的结果表明，对齐任务并不固有地需要保持多样性的算法，标准的奖励最大化RLVR方法无需显式多样性机制即可有效迁移至道德推理。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether aligning large language models (LLMs) for moral reasoning inherently requires diversity-seeking methods, motivated by the observation that moral reasoning often tolerates multiple valid responses, unlike typical logical reasoning tasks where reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) excels. The method involves a comprehensive empirical comparison on MoReBench, employing a rubric-grounded reward pipeline with a trained Qwen3-1.7B judge model to enable stable RLVR training. The main experimental results reveal that distribution-matching approaches do not outperform reward-maximizing methods as hypothesized; semantic visualization shows moral reasoning has a concentrated high-reward distribution, unlike mathematical reasoning where diverse strategies yield similar rewards, explaining why mode-seeking optimization is effective and suggesting standard RLVR methods can transfer to alignment tasks without explicit diversity mechanisms.

Adaptive RAN Slicing Control via Reward-Free Self-Finetuning Agents
Authors: Yuanhao Li, Haozhe Wang, Geyong Min, Nektarios Georgalas, Wang Miao
First: 2026-03-11T09:14:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T09:14:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of Generative AI models into AI-native network systems offers a transformative path toward achieving autonomous and adaptive control. However, the application of such models to continuous control tasks is impeded by intrinsic architectural limitations, including finite context windows, the lack of explicit reward signals, and the degradation of the long context. This paper posits that the key to unlocking robust continuous control is enabling agents to internalize experience by distilling it into their parameters, rather than relying on prompt-based memory. To this end, we propose a novel self-finetuning framework that enables agentic systems to learn continuously through direct interaction with the environment, bypassing the need for handcrafted rewards. Our framework implements a bi-perspective reflection mechanism that generates autonomous linguistic feedback to construct preference datasets from interaction history. A subsequent preference-based fine-tuning process distills long-horizon experiences into the model's parameters. We evaluate our approach on a dynamic Radio Access Network (RAN) slicing task, a challenging multi-objective control problem that requires the resolution of acute trade-offs between spectrum efficiency, service quality, and reconfiguration stability under volatile network conditions. Experimental results show that our framework outperforms standard Reinforcement Learning (RL) baselines and existing Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents in sample efficiency, stability, and multi-metric optimization. These findings demonstrate the potential of self-improving generative agents for continuous control tasks, paving the way for future AI-native network infrastructure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于无奖励自微调智能体的自适应无线接入网切片控制
生成式人工智能模型与AI原生网络系统的融合为实现自主自适应控制提供了变革性路径。然而，此类模型在连续控制任务中的应用受限于固有架构缺陷，包括有限上下文窗口、缺乏显式奖励信号以及长上下文退化问题。本文提出实现稳健连续控制的关键在于使智能体通过将经验蒸馏至参数内部来内化学习，而非依赖基于提示的记忆机制。为此，我们提出一种新型自微调框架，使智能系统能通过与环境直接交互实现持续学习，无需人工设计奖励函数。该框架采用双视角反思机制生成自主语言反馈，从交互历史构建偏好数据集，随后通过基于偏好的微调过程将长周期经验蒸馏至模型参数。我们在动态无线接入网切片任务上评估该方法——这是一个需要在频谱效率、服务质量与重配置稳定性之间进行动态权衡的多目标控制难题。实验结果表明，本框架在样本效率、稳定性及多指标优化方面均优于标准强化学习基线及现有基于大语言模型的智能体。这些发现证明了自进化生成式智能体在连续控制任务中的潜力，为未来AI原生网络基础设施的发展开辟了新路径。

In experiments on a dynamic Radio Access Network slicing task, the method outperforms standard Reinforcement Learning and existing LLM-based agents in sample efficiency, stability, and multi-metric optimization, demonstrating its potential for robust autonomous control in volatile network conditions.
本文针对生成式AI模型在AI原生网络连续控制任务中的应用挑战，如有限上下文窗口和缺乏显式奖励信号等问题，提出了一种自微调框架。该方法使智能体无需人工设计奖励即可通过环境交互直接学习，利用双视角反思机制生成语言反馈，并通过基于偏好的微调将长期经验提炼到模型参数中。在动态无线接入网络切片任务的实验中，该方法在样本效率、稳定性和多指标优化方面优于标准强化学习和现有基于大语言模型的智能体，展示了其在多变网络条件下实现鲁棒自主控制的潜力。
TikArt: Stabilizing Aperture-Guided Fine-Grained Visual Reasoning with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hao Ding, Zhichuan Yang, Weijie Ge, Ziqin Gao, Chaoyi Lu, Lei Zhao
First: 2026-02-16T05:46:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:57:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fine-grained visual reasoning in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) is bottlenecked by single-pass global image encoding: key evidence often lies in tiny objects, cluttered regions, subtle markings, or dense charts. We present \textbf{TikArt} (\textbf{T}h\textbf{i}n\textbf{k}ing \textbf{A}pe\textbf{rt}ure), an aperture-guided agent that formulates multimodal reasoning as sequential evidence acquisition over regions of interest. TikArt follows a Think--Aperture--Observe (TAO) loop that interleaves language reasoning with two aperture actions: Zoom, which extracts rectangular crops, and Segment, which invokes an off-the-shelf segmenter to produce object-centric mask-based views for irregular targets. A mandatory Observation step after every aperture action writes local evidence back into text, yielding interpretable aperture trajectories and persistent linguistic memory. Built on Qwen3-VL-8B, TikArt is trained with GRPO-style reinforcement learning under a two-stage curriculum. To stabilize long-horizon tool-integrated learning, we introduce Relative Uncertainty Reduction (RUR), a dense reward computed by a frozen evaluator that favors evidence-building trajectories and mitigates degenerate tool use. Experiments on high-resolution reasoning, general multimodal understanding, and both referring and reasoning-oriented segmentation show consistent gains over the backbone, demonstrating that aperture-guided observation improves fine-grained visual reasoning and transfers naturally to pixel-level grounding.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TikArt：基于强化学习的孔径引导细粒度视觉推理稳定化方法
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）中的细粒度视觉推理受限于单次全局图像编码：关键证据常存在于微小物体、杂乱区域、细微标记或密集图表中。本文提出\textbf{TikArt}（\textbf{T}h\textbf{i}n\textbf{k}ing \textbf{A}pe\textbf{rt}ure），一种孔径引导智能体，将多模态推理建模为对感兴趣区域的序列化证据采集过程。TikArt遵循“思考-孔径-观察”（TAO）循环，交替进行语言推理与两种孔径操作：提取矩形裁剪的“缩放”操作，以及调用现成分割器生成面向不规则目标的掩码中心视图的“分割”操作。每次孔径操作后强制执行的观察步骤会将局部证据写回文本，形成可解释的孔径轨迹与持久性语言记忆。 基于Qwen3-VL-8B构建的TikArt采用两阶段课程学习，通过GRPO风格强化学习进行训练。为稳定长时程工具集成学习，我们提出相对不确定性降低（RUR）奖励机制——由冻结评估器计算的稠密奖励，鼓励证据积累轨迹并抑制工具滥用。在高分辨率推理、通用多模态理解、指代与推理导向分割任务上的实验表明，该方法在基线上取得持续提升，证明孔径引导观察能改进细粒度视觉推理，并自然迁移至像素级定位任务。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for TikArt is to address the limitation of single-pass global image encoding in multimodal large language models (MLLMs), which often fails to capture fine-grained visual details crucial for reasoning. The method introduces an aperture-guided agent that performs sequential evidence acquisition through a Think-Aperture-Observe loop, utilizing Zoom and Segment actions to extract detailed regions and object-centric views, with each observation recorded as text for interpretable memory. Main experimental results on high-resolution reasoning, general multimodal understanding, and segmentation tasks show consistent improvements over the backbone model, demonstrating enhanced fine-grained reasoning and effective pixel-level grounding.
TikArt的动机是解决多模态大语言模型中单次全局图像编码的局限性，该限制常导致无法捕捉对推理至关重要的细粒度视觉细节。该方法引入了一种孔径引导的智能体，通过思考-孔径-观察循环进行序列化证据采集，利用缩放和分割动作提取详细区域和以对象为中心的视图，并将每次观察记录为文本以实现可解释的记忆。在高分辨率推理、通用多模态理解和分割任务上的主要实验结果表明，相较于基础模型取得了持续提升，证明了孔径引导观察能改进细粒度视觉推理并自然迁移到像素级定位。
Learning to Score: Tuning Cluster Schedulers through Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Martin Asenov, Qiwen Deng, Gingfung Yeung, Adam Barker
First: 2026-03-11T08:54:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:54:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Efficiently allocating incoming jobs to nodes in large-scale clusters can lead to substantial improvements in both cluster utilization and job performance. In order to allocate incoming jobs, cluster schedulers usually rely on a set of scoring functions to rank feasible nodes. Results from individual scoring functions are usually weighted equally, which could lead to sub-optimal deployments as the one-size-fits-all solution does not take into account the characteristics of each workload. Tuning the weights of scoring functions, however, requires expert knowledge and is computationally expensive. This paper proposes a reinforcement learning approach for learning the weights in scheduler scoring algorithms with the overall objective of improving the end-to-end performance of jobs for a given cluster. Our approach is based on percentage improvement reward, frame-stacking, and limiting domain information. We propose a percentage improvement reward to address the objective of multi-step parameter tuning. The inclusion of frame-stacking allows for carrying information across an optimization experiment. Limiting domain information prevents overfitting and improves performance in unseen clusters and workloads. The policy is trained on different combinations of workloads and cluster setups. We demonstrate the proposed approach improves performance on average by 33\% compared to fixed weights and 12\% compared to the best-performing baseline in a lab-based serverless scenario.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习评分：通过强化学习优化集群调度器
在大规模集群中高效分配任务至节点，可显著提升集群利用率和任务性能。集群调度器通常依赖一组评分函数对可行节点排序，但各评分函数结果常被等权重处理，这种通用方案未考虑各工作负载特性，可能导致次优部署。调整评分函数权重需专业知识且计算成本高昂。本文提出一种强化学习方法，以提升特定集群任务端到端性能为目标，学习调度器评分算法中的权重。该方法基于百分比改进奖励、帧堆叠和领域信息限制技术：百分比改进奖励用于实现多步参数调优目标；帧堆叠可在优化实验中传递信息；限制领域信息能防止过拟合并提升在未知集群与工作负载中的性能。策略通过不同工作负载与集群配置组合进行训练。实验表明，在实验室无服务器场景中，该方法相比固定权重平均提升33%性能，较最优基线提升12%。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to improve cluster utilization and job performance by moving beyond the sub-optimal, equal weighting of scoring functions in cluster schedulers, which fails to account for workload-specific characteristics and is difficult to tune manually. The method introduces a reinforcement learning framework that learns optimal weights for scheduler scoring algorithms, employing techniques like a percentage improvement reward for multi-step tuning, frame-stacking to retain information across experiments, and limiting domain information to enhance generalization. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach yields substantial performance gains, improving average job performance by 33% over fixed-weight schedulers and by 12% compared to the best-performing baseline in a lab-based serverless environment.
本文的动机在于，集群调度器中评分函数的权重通常被均等分配，这种一刀切的方法无法适应不同工作负载的特性，导致部署效果欠佳，且手动调整权重需要专业知识且计算成本高昂。为此，研究提出了一种强化学习方法，通过学习为调度器评分算法自动优化权重，其关键技术包括用于多步参数调整的百分比改进奖励、跨实验传递信息的帧堆叠，以及限制领域信息以防止过拟合并提升泛化能力。实验结果表明，该方法在实验室无服务器场景中，相比固定权重调度器平均性能提升了33%，相比性能最佳的基线方法也提升了12%。
DeepEyesV2: Toward Agentic Multimodal Model
Authors: Jack Hong, Chenxiao Zhao, ChengLin Zhu, Weiheng Lu, Guohai Xu, Xing Yu
First: 2025-11-07T14:31:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:46:41+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR2026. Homepage: https://visual-agent.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Agentic multimodal models should not only comprehend text and images, but also actively invoke external tools, such as code execution environments and web search, and integrate these operations into reasoning. In this work, we introduce DeepEyesV2 and explore how to build an agentic multimodal model from the perspectives of data construction, training methods, and model evaluation. We observe that direct reinforcement learning alone fails to induce robust tool-use behavior. This phenomenon motivates a two-stage training pipeline: a cold-start stage to establish tool-use patterns, and reinforcement learning stage to further refine tool invocation. We curate a diverse, moderately challenging training dataset, specifically including examples where tool use is beneficial. We further introduce RealX-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark designed to evaluate real-world multimodal reasoning, which inherently requires the integration of multiple capabilities, including perception, search, and reasoning. We evaluate DeepEyesV2 on RealX-Bench and other representative benchmarks, demonstrating its effectiveness across real-world understanding, mathematical reasoning, and search-intensive tasks. Moreover, DeepEyesV2 exhibits task-adaptive tool invocation, tending to use image operations for perception tasks and numerical computations for reasoning tasks. Reinforcement learning further enables complex tool combinations and allows model to selectively invoke tools based on context. We hope our study can provide guidance for community in developing agentic multimodal models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepEyesV2：迈向具身化多模态智能体模型
具身化多模态模型不仅需要理解文本与图像，还应能主动调用外部工具（如代码执行环境与网络搜索），并将这些操作整合进推理流程。本研究提出DeepEyesV2，从数据构建、训练方法与模型评估三个维度探索如何构建具身化多模态模型。我们发现仅依靠直接强化学习难以形成稳健的工具使用行为，因此设计了两阶段训练流程：冷启动阶段建立工具使用模式，强化学习阶段优化工具调用策略。我们构建了多样化、适度挑战性的训练数据集，特别纳入工具使用具有显著增益的示例。同时提出RealX-Bench综合评测基准，专门评估需要融合感知、搜索与推理能力的真实世界多模态推理任务。在RealX-Bench及其他代表性基准上的实验表明，DeepEyesV2在真实场景理解、数学推理与搜索密集型任务中均表现优异。该模型展现出任务自适应的工具调用特性：感知任务倾向调用图像操作，推理任务偏好数值计算。强化学习进一步支持复杂工具组合调用，并能依据上下文选择性启用工具。本研究旨在为具身化多模态模型的开发提供方法论参考。

The paper introduces DeepEyesV2, an agentic multimodal model designed to actively invoke and integrate external tools like code execution and web search into its reasoning process. The motivation stems from the need for models that go beyond passive comprehension to perform active, tool-augmented reasoning. The method employs a two-stage training pipeline: a cold-start stage to establish basic tool-use patterns, followed by a reinforcement learning stage to refine tool invocation, addressing the observed insufficiency of reinforcement learning alone. Main experimental results, evaluated on the introduced RealX-Bench and other benchmarks, show DeepEyesV2's effectiveness in real-world understanding, mathematical reasoning, and search tasks, with the model demonstrating task-adaptive tool use, such as employing image operations for perception and numerical computations for reasoning, and reinforcement learning enabling complex, context-sensitive tool combinations.
本文介绍了DeepEyesV2，一种代理式多模态模型，旨在主动调用并整合代码执行和网络搜索等外部工具到其推理过程中。其动机源于需要模型超越被动理解，实现主动的、工具增强的推理。方法采用两阶段训练流程：冷启动阶段建立基本的工具使用模式，随后强化学习阶段细化工具调用，以解决仅靠强化学习不足的问题。在引入的RealX-Bench及其他基准上的主要实验结果表明，DeepEyesV2在现实世界理解、数学推理和搜索任务中表现有效，模型展现出任务自适应的工具使用，例如在感知任务中使用图像操作、在推理任务中进行数值计算，且强化学习使其能够实现复杂、基于上下文的工具组合。
Tackling Length Inflation Without Trade-offs: Group Relative Reward Rescaling for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zichao Li, Jie Lou, Fangchen Dong, Zhiyuan Fan, Mengjie Ren, Hongyu Lin, Xianpei Han, Debing Zhang, Le Sun, Yaojie Lu, Xing Yu
First: 2026-03-11T08:41:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:41:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning significantly enhances LLM capabilities but suffers from a critical issue: length inflation, where models adopt verbosity or inefficient reasoning to maximize rewards. Prior approaches struggle to address this challenge in a general and lossless manner, primarily because additive penalties introduce a compensatory effect that creates optimization shortcuts, while heuristic gating strategies lack generality beyond binary feedback. To bridge this gap, we present Group Relative Reward Rescaling (GR$^3$), which reframes length control as a multiplicative rescaling paradigm, effectively establishing a generalized, continuous, and reward-dependent gating mechanism. To further ensure lossless optimization, we incorporate group-relative regularization and advantage-aware calibration, which dynamically adapt length budgets to instance difficulty and preserve the advantage signal of high-quality trajectories. Empirically, across both RLHF and RLVR settings, GR$^3$~maintains training dynamics and downstream performance comparable to standard GRPO while significantly mitigating length inflation, outperforming state-of-the-art length-regularized baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无权衡应对长度膨胀：强化学习中的组相对奖励重缩放
强化学习显著提升了大型语言模型的能力，但存在一个关键问题：长度膨胀，即模型为最大化奖励而采用冗长或低效的推理。先前方法难以以通用且无损的方式应对这一挑战，主要因为加法惩罚会引入补偿效应，形成优化捷径，而启发式门控策略在二元反馈之外缺乏普适性。为填补这一空白，我们提出了组相对奖励重缩放（GR$^3$），它将长度控制重构为乘法重缩放范式，有效建立了一种广义、连续且依赖奖励的门控机制。为确保无损优化，我们进一步引入组相对正则化和优势感知校准，动态调整长度预算以适应实例难度，并保留高质量轨迹的优势信号。实验表明，在RLHF和RLVR两种设置下，GR$^3$在保持训练动态和下游性能与标准GRPO相当的同时，显著缓解了长度膨胀，优于当前最先进的长度正则化基线。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the problem of length inflation in reinforcement learning for large language models, where models become verbose to maximize rewards, and prior methods either introduce optimization shortcuts with additive penalties or lack generality. The proposed solution, Group Relative Reward Rescaling (GR^3), reframes length control as a multiplicative rescaling paradigm with group-relative regularization and advantage-aware calibration to dynamically adapt length budgets based on instance difficulty while preserving high-quality trajectory signals. Experimental results show that GR^3 effectively mitigates length inflation across RLHF and RLVR settings, maintaining training dynamics and downstream performance comparable to standard methods and outperforming existing length-regularized baselines.
该论文针对强化学习在大语言模型中出现的长度膨胀问题，即模型为最大化奖励而变得冗长，先前方法要么因加法惩罚引入优化捷径，要么缺乏普适性。提出的解决方案是组相对奖励重缩放（GR^3），它将长度控制重构为乘法重缩放范式，结合组相对正则化和优势感知校准，根据实例难度动态调整长度预算并保留高质量轨迹信号。实验结果表明，在RLHF和RLVR设置中，GR^3有效缓解了长度膨胀，保持了与标准方法相当的训练动态和下游性能，并优于现有的长度正则化基线。
UAV-MARL: Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Time-Critical and Dynamic Medical Supply Delivery
Authors: Islam Guven, Mehmet Parlak
First: 2026-03-11T08:31:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:31:52+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 4 figures, 2 tables, conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) are increasingly used to support time-critical medical supply delivery, providing rapid and flexible logistics during emergencies and resource shortages. However, effective deployment of UAV fleets requires coordination mechanisms capable of prioritizing medical requests, allocating limited aerial resources, and adapting delivery schedules under uncertain operational conditions. This paper presents a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework for coordinating UAV fleets in stochastic medical delivery scenarios where requests vary in urgency, location, and delivery deadlines. The problem is formulated as a partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP) in which UAV agents maintain awareness of medical delivery demands while having limited visibility of other agents due to communication and localization constraints. The proposed framework employs Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) as the primary learning algorithm and evaluates several variants, including asynchronous extensions, classical actor--critic methods, and architectural modifications to analyze scalability and performance trade-offs. The model is evaluated using real-world geographic data from selected clinics and hospitals extracted from the OpenStreetMap dataset. The framework provides a decision-support layer that prioritizes medical tasks, reallocates UAV resources in real time, and assists healthcare personnel in managing urgent logistics. Experimental results show that classical PPO achieves superior coordination performance compared to asynchronous and sequential learning strategies, highlighting the potential of reinforcement learning for adaptive and scalable UAV-assisted healthcare logistics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UAV-MARL：面向时效性与动态医疗物资配送的多智能体强化学习
无人机正日益用于支持时效性医疗物资配送，在紧急情况和资源短缺时提供快速灵活的物流支持。然而，无人机编队的有效部署需要具备以下能力的协调机制：对医疗请求进行优先级排序、分配有限的空中资源，并在不确定的操作条件下调整配送计划。本文提出一种多智能体强化学习框架，用于在随机医疗配送场景中协调无人机编队，其中请求的紧急程度、位置和配送截止时间各不相同。该问题被建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，无人机智能体需保持对医疗配送需求的感知，同时因通信和定位限制对其他智能体的可见性有限。所提框架采用近端策略优化作为主要学习算法，并评估了多种变体，包括异步扩展、经典演员-评论家方法及架构修改，以分析可扩展性与性能权衡。模型使用从OpenStreetMap数据集提取的选定诊所和医院真实地理数据进行评估。该框架提供决策支持层，可对医疗任务进行优先级排序、实时重新分配无人机资源，并协助医护人员管理紧急物流。实验结果表明，与异步和顺序学习策略相比，经典PPO实现了更优的协调性能，凸显了强化学习在自适应、可扩展无人机辅助医疗物流中的潜力。

This paper addresses the challenge of coordinating unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) fleets for time-critical medical supply delivery, where dynamic requests and uncertain conditions demand adaptive resource allocation. The authors propose a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework, modeling the problem as a partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP) and employing Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) as the core algorithm, with evaluations of various algorithmic variants. Using real-world geographic data from OpenStreetMap, experiments demonstrate that classical PPO outperforms asynchronous and sequential learning strategies in coordination performance, offering a scalable decision-support system for prioritizing medical tasks and reallocating UAV resources in real time.
本文针对时间紧迫的医疗物资配送中无人机编队协调的挑战，旨在应对动态请求和不确定条件下自适应资源分配的需求。作者提出了一种多智能体强化学习框架，将问题建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，并以近端策略优化作为核心算法，评估了多种算法变体。基于OpenStreetMap的真实地理数据实验表明，经典近端策略优化在协调性能上优于异步和顺序学习策略，为实时优先处理医疗任务和重新分配无人机资源提供了一个可扩展的决策支持系统。
IH-Challenge: A Training Dataset to Improve Instruction Hierarchy on Frontier LLMs
Authors: Chuan Guo, Juan Felipe Ceron Uribe, Sicheng Zhu, Christopher A. Choquette-Choo, Steph Lin, Nikhil Kandpal, Milad Nasr, Rai, Sam Toyer, Miles Wang, Yaodong Yu, Alex Beutel, Kai Xiao
First: 2026-03-11T08:27:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:27:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Instruction hierarchy (IH) defines how LLMs prioritize system, developer, user, and tool instructions under conflict, providing a concrete, trust-ordered policy for resolving instruction conflicts. IH is key to defending against jailbreaks, system prompt extractions, and agentic prompt injections. However, robust IH behavior is difficult to train: IH failures can be confounded with instruction-following failures, conflicts can be nuanced, and models can learn shortcuts such as overrefusing. We introduce IH-Challenge, a reinforcement learning training dataset, to address these difficulties. Fine-tuning GPT-5-Mini on IH-Challenge with online adversarial example generation improves IH robustness by +10.0% on average across 16 in-distribution, out-of-distribution, and human red-teaming benchmarks (84.1% to 94.1%), reduces unsafe behavior from 6.6% to 0.7% while improving helpfulness on general safety evaluations, and saturates an internal static agentic prompt injection evaluation, with minimal capability regression. We release the IH-Challenge dataset (https://huggingface.co/datasets/openai/ih-challenge) to support future research on robust instruction hierarchy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IH-Challenge：提升前沿大语言模型指令层级能力的训练数据集
指令层级（IH）定义了大型语言模型在指令冲突时如何优先处理系统、开发者、用户和工具指令，为解决指令冲突提供了具体且基于信任排序的策略。IH是防御越狱攻击、系统提示提取和智能体提示注入的关键。然而，稳健的IH行为难以训练：IH失败可能与指令遵循失败相混淆，冲突可能微妙复杂，模型可能学习过度拒绝等捷径。为此，我们推出IH-Challenge强化学习训练数据集以应对这些挑战。通过在IH-Challenge上结合在线对抗样本生成对GPT-5-Mini进行微调，其在16个分布内、分布外及人工红队评估基准上的IH稳健性平均提升+10.0%（从84.1%升至94.1%），不安全行为从6.6%降至0.7%，同时提升通用安全评估中的帮助性，并在内部静态智能体提示注入评估中达到饱和，且能力衰退极小。我们公开IH-Challenge数据集（https://huggingface.co/datasets/openai/ih-challenge）以支持未来关于稳健指令层级的研究。

The method involves creating a specialized reinforcement learning training dataset called IH-Challenge, which is used to fine-tune models such as GPT-5-Mini with online adversarial example generation to address training difficulties like nuanced conflicts and model shortcuts. Exploratory Optimal Stopping: A Singular Control Formulation
Authors: Jodi Dianetti, Giorgio Ferrari, Renyuan Xu
First: 2024-08-18T02:31:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T07:17:41+00:00
Comments: 49 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper explores continuous-time and state-space optimal stopping problems from a reinforcement learning perspective. We begin by formulating the stopping problem using randomized stopping times, where the decision maker's control is represented by the probability of stopping within a given time-specifically, a bounded, non-decreasing, càdlàg control process. To encourage exploration and facilitate learning, we introduce a regularized version of the problem by penalizing the performance criterion with the cumulative residual entropy of the randomized stopping time. The regularized problem takes the form of an (n+1)-dimensional degenerate singular stochastic control with finite-fuel, where the regularized free boundary becomes the graph of a function mapping the state variable of the original stopping problem into the probability of stopping. We address this singular control problem through the dynamic programming principle, which enables us to identify the unique optimal exploratory strategy. Finally, we propose both model-based and model-free reinforcement learning algorithms tailored for exploratory optimal stopping problems. We establish policy improvement guarantees for the proposed algorithms. Moreover, the model-free method is of actor-critic type and it is scalable in high-dimensions under neural network parameterization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探索性最优停止：一种奇异控制表述
本文从强化学习的角度探讨连续时间和状态空间的最优停止问题。首先，我们使用随机化停止时间对停止问题进行建模，其中决策者的控制由给定时间内停止的概率表示——具体为一个有界、非递减、右连左极控制过程。为鼓励探索并促进学习，我们引入问题的正则化版本，通过随机化停止时间的累积残差熵对性能准则进行惩罚。正则化问题呈现为具有有限燃料的(n+1)维退化奇异随机控制形式，其中正则化自由边界成为将原始停止问题的状态变量映射至停止概率的函数图像。我们通过动态规划原理处理该奇异控制问题，从而识别出唯一的最优探索策略。最后，我们提出了分别针对模型驱动和无模型强化学习算法的探索性最优停止问题解决方案，并为所提算法建立了策略改进保证。此外，无模型方法属于行动者-评论家类型，在神经网络参数化下具备高维可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to incorporate exploration into continuous-time optimal stopping problems from a reinforcement learning perspective. The method formulates the problem using randomized stopping times, represented by a bounded, non-decreasing control process, and introduces a regularization term based on cumulative residual entropy to encourage exploration, transforming it into a finite-fuel singular stochastic control problem. The main experimental results include solving this via the dynamic programming principle to derive a unique optimal exploratory strategy, and proposing both model-based and model-free actor-critic algorithms with proven policy improvement guarantees and scalability in high dimensions under neural network parameterization.
本文的动机是从强化学习角度出发，在连续时间最优停止问题中引入探索机制。方法采用随机化停止时间，通过一个有界、非降的控制过程表示决策，并引入基于累积残差熵的正则化项以鼓励探索，从而将问题转化为有限燃料的奇异随机控制问题。主要实验结果包括通过动态规划原理求解得到唯一的最优探索策略，并提出了模型基础和模型无关的演员-评论家算法，这些算法具有策略改进的理论保证，且在神经网络参数化下能适应高维场景。
Revisiting Value Iteration: Unified Analysis of Discounted and Average-Reward Cases
Authors: Arsenii Mustafin, Xinyi Sheng, Dominik Baumann
First: 2025-10-27T22:42:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T07:14:56+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 2 figure
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Value Iteration (VI) is one of the most fundamental algorithms in Reinforcement Learning, its theoretical convergence guarantees still exhibit a persistent mismatch with empirical behavior. In the discounted-reward case, classical theory guarantees geometric convergence with rate $γ$, while in the average-reward case recent work suggests that only sublinear convergence can be expected. In practice, however, VI is often observed to converge significantly faster. In this work, we show through a unified geometry-based analysis that, under an assumption of a unique and unichain optimal policy, (i) convergence is geometric in both the discounted- and average-reward settings and (ii) the convergence rate is faster than previous analyses suggest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重访价值迭代：折扣与平均奖励情形的统一分析
价值迭代（VI）是强化学习中最基础的算法之一，但其理论收敛保证与实证表现之间仍存在持续的不匹配。在折扣奖励情形中，经典理论保证以速率$γ$几何收敛；而在平均奖励情形中，近期研究认为仅能实现次线性收敛。然而实践中，VI常被观察到收敛速度显著更快。本文通过基于几何的统一分析证明，在假设存在唯一且单链最优策略的前提下：（i）折扣奖励与平均奖励情形下均呈几何收敛；（ii）收敛速率比先前分析所提示的更快。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the persistent mismatch between theoretical convergence guarantees and empirical performance of Value Iteration (VI) in reinforcement learning, where classical theory predicts geometric convergence with rate γ for discounted rewards and only sublinear convergence for average rewards, yet VI is often observed to converge much faster in practice. Through a unified geometry-based analysis, the authors demonstrate that under the assumption of a unique and unichain optimal policy, convergence is geometric in both discounted- and average-reward settings, and the convergence rate is faster than previously suggested by earlier analyses.
本文针对强化学习中值迭代算法的理论收敛保证与实证性能之间的持续不匹配问题展开研究，经典理论预测折扣奖励情况下的几何收敛速率为γ，而平均奖励情况下仅能预期次线性收敛，但在实践中值迭代常被观察到收敛得更快。通过基于几何的统一分析，作者证明在假设存在唯一且单链最优策略的条件下，值迭代在折扣奖励和平均奖励设置下均呈现几何收敛，且收敛速度比先前分析所建议的更快。
Muscle Synergy Priors Enhance Biomechanical Fidelity in Predictive Musculoskeletal Locomotion Simulation
Authors: Ilseung Park, Eunsik Choi, Jangwhan Ahn, Jooeun Ahn
First: 2026-03-11T06:48:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T06:48:15+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human locomotion emerges from high-dimensional neuromuscular control, making predictive musculoskeletal simulation challenging. We present a physiology-informed reinforcement-learning framework that constrains control using muscle synergies. We extracted a low-dimensional synergy basis from inverse musculoskeletal analyses of a small set of overground walking trials and used it as the action space for a muscle-driven three-dimensional model trained across variable speeds, slopes and uneven terrain. The resulting controller generated stable gait from 0.7-1.8 m/s and on $\pm$ 6$^{\circ}$ grades and reproduced condition-dependent modulation of joint angles, joint moments and ground reaction forces. Compared with an unconstrained controller, synergy-constrained control reduced non-physiological knee kinematics and kept knee moment profiles within the experimental envelope. Across conditions, simulated vertical ground reaction forces correlated strongly with human measurements, and muscle-activation timing largely fell within inter-subject variability. These results show that embedding neurophysiological structure into reinforcement learning can improve biomechanical fidelity and generalization in predictive human locomotion simulation with limited experimental data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：肌肉协同先验增强预测性肌肉骨骼运动模拟的生物力学保真度
人类运动源于高维神经肌肉控制，使得预测性肌肉骨骼模拟具有挑战性。我们提出一种生理学启发的强化学习框架，利用肌肉协同约束控制。我们从少量地面行走试验的逆向肌肉骨骼分析中提取低维协同基，并将其用作在可变速度、坡度和不平坦地形上训练的肌肉驱动三维模型的动作空间。所得控制器在0.7-1.8 m/s速度范围和±6°坡度上生成稳定步态，并复现了关节角度、关节力矩和地面反作用力的条件依赖性调节。与无约束控制器相比，协同约束控制减少了非生理性膝关节运动学，并将膝关节力矩曲线保持在实验包络内。在所有条件下，模拟的垂直地面反作用力与人体测量值高度相关，肌肉激活时序基本落在受试者间变异范围内。这些结果表明，将神经生理结构嵌入强化学习，可在有限实验数据下提升预测性人类运动模拟的生物力学保真度与泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The study was motivated by the challenge of simulating human locomotion due to its complex neuromuscular control, aiming to improve biomechanical realism in predictive simulations. The method involved a reinforcement learning framework that incorporated muscle synergy priors, where synergies extracted from inverse analyses of walking trials were used to constrain the action space of a 3D muscle-driven model trained across varied speeds, slopes, and terrain. Key experimental results showed that the synergy-constrained controller generated stable gait across a range of conditions, reduced non-physiological knee kinematics, kept knee moments within experimental bounds, and produced ground reaction forces and muscle activations that closely matched human data, enhancing fidelity and generalization with limited experimental input.
该研究旨在解决人类运动模拟中因复杂神经肌肉控制带来的挑战，以提高预测仿真的生物力学真实性。方法上，采用强化学习框架并融入肌肉协同先验，通过从步行试验的逆向分析中提取协同作用来约束三维肌肉驱动模型的动作空间，并在不同速度、坡度和地形上进行训练。主要实验结果表明，协同约束控制器在多种条件下生成稳定步态，减少了非生理性膝关节运动学，将膝关节力矩保持在实验范围内，且模拟的垂直地面反作用力和肌肉激活时序与人类数据高度吻合，从而在有限实验数据下提升了仿真的保真度和泛化能力。
MemOCR: Layout-Aware Visual Memory for Efficient Long-Horizon Reasoning
Authors: Yaorui Shi, Shugui Liu, Yu Yang, Wenyu Mao, Yuxin Chen, Qi GU, Hui Su, Xunliang Cai, Xiang Wang, An Zhang
First: 2026-01-29T09:47:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T06:10:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-horizon agentic reasoning necessitates effectively compressing growing interaction histories into a limited context window. Most existing memory systems serialize history as text, where token-level cost is uniform and scales linearly with length, often spending scarce budget on low-value details. To this end, we introduce MemOCR, a multimodal memory agent that improves long-horizon reasoning under tight context budgets by allocating memory space with adaptive information density through visual layout. Concretely, MemOCR maintains a structured rich-text memory (e.g., headings, highlights) and renders it into an image that the agent consults for memory access, visually prioritizing crucial evidence while aggressively compressing auxiliary details. To ensure robustness across varying memory budgets, we train MemOCR with reinforcement learning under budget-aware objectives that expose the agent to diverse compression levels. Across long-context multi-hop and single-hop question-answering benchmarks, MemOCR outperforms strong text-based baselines and achieves more effective context utilization under extreme budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemOCR：面向高效长程推理的布局感知视觉记忆系统
长程智能体推理需将不断增长的交互历史有效压缩至有限上下文窗口。现有记忆系统多将历史序列化为文本，其词元级成本固定且随长度线性增长，常将稀缺资源消耗于低价值细节。为此，我们提出MemOCR——一种多模态记忆智能体，通过视觉布局实现自适应信息密度的记忆空间分配，从而提升严格上下文预算下的长程推理能力。具体而言，MemOCR维护结构化富文本记忆（如标题、高亮内容），并将其渲染为可供智能体查询记忆的图像，在视觉层面突出关键证据的同时对辅助细节进行激进压缩。为确保不同记忆预算下的鲁棒性，我们采用预算感知的强化学习目标训练MemOCR，使智能体适应多样化压缩层级。在长上下文多跳与单跳问答基准测试中，MemOCR优于强文本基线，并在极端预算下实现更高效的上下文利用。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency of text-based memory systems in long-horizon reasoning, where uniform token-level costs waste context budgets on low-value details. To improve memory efficiency, the authors propose MemOCR, a multimodal memory agent that structures rich-text memory with visual layouts, rendering it into an image to prioritize crucial information and compress auxiliary details adaptively. Using reinforcement learning with budget-aware objectives, MemOCR is trained for robustness across varying compression levels, and experimental results on long-context multi-hop and single-hop QA benchmarks show it outperforms text-based baselines and achieves more effective context utilization under extreme budgets.
本文针对长时程推理中基于文本的记忆系统效率低下问题，其中统一的令牌级成本将有限的上下文预算浪费在低价值细节上。为提高记忆效率，作者提出了MemOCR，一种多模态记忆代理，它通过视觉布局结构化富文本记忆，将其渲染为图像以优先处理关键信息并自适应压缩辅助细节。通过使用具有预算感知目标的强化学习进行训练，MemOCR在不同压缩级别下保持鲁棒性，实验结果表明，在长上下文多跳和单跳问答基准测试中，MemOCR优于基于文本的基线方法，并在极端预算下实现了更有效的上下文利用。
GTR-Turbo: Merged Checkpoint is Secretly a Free Teacher for Agentic VLM Training
Authors: Tong Wei, Yijun Yang, Changhao Zhang, Junliang Xing, Yuanchun Shi, Zongqing Lu, Deheng Ye
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-12-15T07:11:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:58:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn reinforcement learning (RL) for multi-modal agents built upon vision-language models (VLMs) is hampered by sparse rewards and long-horizon credit assignment. Recent methods densify the reward by querying a teacher that provides step-level feedback, e.g., Guided Thought Reinforcement (GTR) and On-Policy Distillation, but rely on costly, often privileged models as the teacher, limiting practicality and reproducibility. We introduce GTR-Turbo, a highly efficient upgrade to GTR that matches its performance without training on or querying an expensive teacher model. Specifically, GTR-Turbo merges the weights of checkpoints produced during ongoing RL training and then uses the resulting merged model as a "free" teacher to guide subsequent RL via supervised fine-tuning or soft logit distillation. This design removes dependence on privileged VLMs (e.g., GPT or Gemini), mitigates the "entropy collapse" observed in prior work, and maintains stable training. Across diverse visual agentic tasks, GTR-Turbo improves the accuracy of the baseline model by 10-30% while reducing wall-clock training time by 50% and compute cost by 60% relative to GTR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GTR-Turbo：合并检查点在智能体化视觉语言模型训练中悄然成为免费教师
基于视觉语言模型的多模态智能体多轮强化学习常受稀疏奖励与长程信用分配问题制约。现有方法通过查询提供步骤级反馈的教师模型来稠密化奖励，如引导思维强化与策略蒸馏，但依赖昂贵且常具特权访问的教师模型，限制了实用性与可复现性。本文提出GTR-Turbo——一种对GTR的高效升级方案，无需训练或查询昂贵教师模型即可达到同等性能。具体而言，GTR-Turbo合并持续强化学习训练中产生的检查点权重，将所得合并模型作为“免费”教师，通过监督微调或软对数蒸馏指导后续强化学习。该设计消除了对特权视觉语言模型的依赖，缓解了先前工作中观察到的“熵崩溃”现象，并保持训练稳定性。在多样化视觉智能体任务中，GTR-Turbo将基线模型准确率提升10-30%，同时相比GTR减少50%训练时间与60%计算成本。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the inefficiency and high cost of using privileged teacher models for step-level feedback in multi-turn reinforcement learning for vision-language agents, which suffer from sparse rewards. The method introduces GTR-Turbo, which merges the weights of checkpoints generated during ongoing RL training and uses this merged model as a free teacher to guide subsequent training via supervised fine-tuning or soft logit distillation. The main experimental results show that GTR-Turbo improves baseline model accuracy by 10-30% across diverse visual agentic tasks while reducing wall-clock training time by 50% and compute cost by 60% compared to the prior GTR method.

ToolRLA: Multiplicative Reward Decomposition for Tool-Integrated Agents
Authors: Pengbo Liu
First: 2026-03-02T08:52:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:50:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-integrated agents that interleave reasoning with API calls are promising for complex tasks, yet aligning them for high-stakes, domain-specific deployment remains challenging: existing reinforcement learning approaches rely on coarse binary rewards that cannot distinguish tool selection errors from malformed parameters. We present ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline (SFT -> GRPO -> DPO) for domain-specific tool agents. The core contribution is a fine-grained reward function with multiplicative correctness decomposition spanning four dimensions -- format validity, tool selection, parameter accuracy, and regulatory compliance -- that encodes domain priority orderings as inductive biases in the reward landscape. Deployed on a financial advisory copilot (80+ advisors, 1,200+ daily queries), ToolRLA achieves over three months: a 47% improvement in task completion rate (62%->91%), a 63% reduction in tool invocation errors (38%->14%), and a 93% reduction in regulatory violations (12%->0.8%), within sub-2-second latency. Ablation studies show the multiplicative reward design accounts for 7 percentage points of improvement over additive alternatives. Generalization is further validated on ToolBench and API-Bank.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ToolRLA：面向工具集成智能体的乘性奖励分解框架
融合推理与API调用的工具集成智能体在处理复杂任务方面前景广阔，但其在高风险领域特定场景下的对齐部署仍面临挑战：现有强化学习方法依赖粗粒度的二元奖励机制，无法区分工具选择错误与参数格式错误。本文提出ToolRLA——一个面向领域特定工具智能体的三阶段后训练流程（监督微调→分组相对策略优化→直接偏好优化）。核心贡献在于构建了细粒度乘性奖励函数，通过格式有效性、工具选择、参数准确性、合规性四个维度的乘性正确率分解，将领域优先级次序编码为奖励空间的归纳偏置。在金融顾问智能副驾系统（覆盖80+顾问，日均1200+查询）的部署中，ToolRLA在三个月内实现：任务完成率提升47%（62%→91%），工具调用错误减少63%（38%→14%），违规操作降低93%（12%→0.8%），且延迟低于2秒。消融实验表明乘性奖励设计较加性方案额外贡献7个百分点的性能提升。该框架在ToolBench和API-Bank基准测试中进一步验证了泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning tool-integrated agents for high-stakes, domain-specific tasks, where existing reinforcement learning methods suffer from coarse binary rewards that fail to differentiate between types of errors like tool selection and parameter malformation. It introduces ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline (SFT, GRPO, DPO) featuring a fine-grained multiplicative reward function that decomposes correctness into four dimensions—format validity, tool selection, parameter accuracy, and regulatory compliance—to encode domain priorities as inductive biases. In a deployment on a financial advisory copilot handling over 1,200 daily queries, the method achieved significant improvements over three months: a 47% increase in task completion rate (from 62% to 91%), a 63% reduction in tool invocation errors (from 38% to 14%), and a 93% drop in regulatory violations (from 12% to 0.8%), while maintaining sub-2-second latency, with ablation studies confirming the multiplicative reward design contributed 7 percentage points of improvement over additive alternatives and generalization validated on benchmarks like ToolBench and API-Bank.
本文针对高风险领域特定任务中工具集成智能体的对齐挑战，指出现有强化学习方法依赖粗糙的二元奖励，无法区分工具选择错误与参数格式错误等问题。提出了ToolRLA，一个包含三阶段后训练流程（监督微调、分组策略优化、直接偏好优化）的方法，其核心是细粒度的乘法奖励函数，将正确性分解为四个维度——格式有效性、工具选择、参数准确性和法规遵从性，以此将领域优先级作为归纳偏置编码到奖励景观中。在一个拥有80多名顾问、每日处理1200多次查询的财务咨询助手部署中，该方法在三个月内实现了显著提升：任务完成率提高47%（从62%升至91%），工具调用错误减少63%（从38%降至14%），违规行为下降93%（从12%降至0.8%），同时保持亚2秒延迟；消融实验表明乘法奖励设计比加法替代方案多贡献7个百分点的改进，并在ToolBench和API-Bank等基准上验证了泛化能力。
SPAARS: Safer RL Policy Alignment through Abstract Exploration and Refined Exploitation of Action Space
Authors: Swaminathan S K, Aritra Hazra
First: 2026-03-10T08:52:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:45:21+00:00
Comments: 9 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) offers a promising paradigm for robotics by pre-training policies on safe, offline demonstrations and fine-tuning them via online interaction. However, a fundamental challenge remains: how to safely explore online without deviating from the behavioral support of the offline data? While recent methods leverage conditional variational autoencoders (CVAEs) to bound exploration within a latent space, they inherently suffer from an exploitation gap -- a performance ceiling imposed by the decoder's reconstruction loss. We introduce SPAARS, a curriculum learning framework that initially constrains exploration to the low-dimensional latent manifold for sample-efficient, safe behavioral improvement, then seamlessly transfers control to the raw action space, bypassing the decoder bottleneck. SPAARS has two instantiations: the CVAE-based variant requires only unordered (s,a) pairs and no trajectory segmentation; SPAARS-SUPE pairs SPAARS with OPAL temporal skill pretraining for stronger exploration structure at the cost of requiring trajectory chunks. We prove an upper bound on the exploitation gap using the Performance Difference Lemma, establish that latent-space policy gradients achieve provable variance reduction over raw-space exploration, and show that concurrent behavioral cloning during the latent phase directly controls curriculum transition stability. Empirically, SPAARS-SUPE achieves 0.825 normalized return on kitchen-mixed-v0 versus 0.75 for SUPE, with 5x better sample efficiency; standalone SPAARS achieves 92.7 and 102.9 normalized return on hopper-medium-v2 and walker2d-medium-v2 respectively, surpassing IQL baselines of 66.3 and 78.3 respectively, confirming the utility of the unordered-pair CVAE instantiation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPAARS：通过抽象探索与精细化动作空间利用实现更安全的强化学习策略对齐
离线到在线强化学习（RL）通过离线安全演示预训练策略并在线交互微调，为机器人学提供了前景广阔的研究范式。然而，核心挑战依然存在：如何在不偏离离线数据行为支持的前提下安全进行在线探索？现有方法虽利用条件变分自编码器（CVAE）将探索限制在潜在空间内，却因解码器重构损失导致固有的利用缺口——即性能上限问题。本文提出SPAARS课程学习框架：初期将探索约束在低维潜在流形以实现样本高效的安全行为改进，随后无缝切换至原始动作空间以规避解码器瓶颈。SPAARS具有两种实现形式：基于CVAE的变体仅需无序状态-动作对且无需轨迹分割；SPAARS-SUPE将SPAARS与OPAL时序技能预训练结合，以轨迹片段为代价获得更强的探索结构。我们通过性能差异引理证明了利用缺口的上界，论证了潜在空间策略梯度相比原始空间探索可实现可证明的方差缩减，并表明潜在阶段并行的行为克隆能直接控制课程转换稳定性。实验表明：在kitchen-mixed-v0环境中，SPAARS-SUPE获得0.825归一化回报（SUPE为0.75）且样本效率提升5倍；独立SPAARS在hopper-medium-v2和walker2d-medium-v2环境中分别获得92.7和102.9归一化回报，显著超越IQL基线的66.3和78.3，验证了无序对CVAE实现的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge of safely exploring during the online fine-tuning phase in offline-to-online reinforcement learning for robotics, where methods constrained to a latent action space often hit a performance ceiling due to decoder reconstruction loss. The proposed method, SPAARS, is a curriculum learning framework that first explores safely within a low-dimensional latent manifold and then transfers control to the raw action space to bypass the decoder bottleneck, with two variants: a CVAE-based one using unordered state-action pairs and SPAARS-SUPE which incorporates temporal skill pretraining. Experimental results show that SPAARS-SUPE achieves a 0.825 normalized return on the kitchen-mixed-v0 task, outperforming the SUPE baseline of 0.75 with 5x better sample efficiency, while the standalone SPAARS variant significantly surpasses IQL baselines on hopper and walker2d benchmarks.
本文的动机是解决机器人离线到在线强化学习中在线微调阶段的安全探索难题，现有方法受限于潜在动作空间常因解码器重建损失导致性能上限。所提出的方法SPAARS是一个课程学习框架，它首先在低维潜在流形内进行安全探索，随后将控制转移到原始动作空间以绕过解码器瓶颈，其包含两个变体：基于CVAE的版本使用无序状态-动作对，而SPAARS-SUPE则结合了时序技能预训练以增强探索结构。实验结果表明，SPAARS-SUPE在kitchen-mixed-v0任务上取得了0.825的标准化回报，优于SUPE基线的0.75，且样本效率提升5倍；独立的SPAARS变体在hopper和walker2d基准测试中也显著超越了IQL基线。
Adaptive Active Learning for Regression via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Simon D. Nguyen, Troy Russo, Kentaro Hoffman, Tyler H. McCormick
First: 2026-03-11T05:33:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:33:07+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 103 figures. Main paper (8 pages, 4 figures) plus appendix with proofs and supplemental experimental results. Submitted to UAI2026. Codebase available at https://github.com/thatswhatsimonsaid/WeightedGreedySampling
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Active learning for regression reduces labeling costs by selecting the most informative samples. Improved Greedy Sampling is a prominent method that balances feature-space diversity and output-space uncertainty using a static, multiplicative rule. We propose Weighted improved Greedy Sampling (WiGS), which replaces this framework with a dynamic, additive criterion. We formulate weight selection as a reinforcement learning problem, enabling an agent to adapt the exploration-investigation balance throughout learning. Experiments on 18 benchmark datasets and a synthetic environment show WiGS outperforms iGS and other baseline methods in both accuracy and labeling efficiency, particularly in domains with irregular data density where the baseline's multiplicative rule ignores high-error samples in dense regions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的回归任务自适应主动学习
回归任务的主动学习通过选择信息量最大的样本来降低标注成本。改进型贪婪采样是一种主流方法，它采用静态乘法规则平衡特征空间多样性与输出空间不确定性。本文提出加权改进型贪婪采样，以动态加法准则替代原有框架。我们将权重选择构建为强化学习问题，使智能体能在学习过程中自适应调整探索与利用的平衡。在18个基准数据集和合成环境上的实验表明，WiGS在准确率和标注效率上均优于iGS及其他基线方法，尤其在数据密度分布不均的场景中，基线方法的乘法规则会忽略密集区域的高误差样本。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the need for more efficient active learning in regression tasks by proposing a dynamic alternative to the static sampling rule of the Improved Greedy Sampling (iGS) method. The authors introduce Weighted improved Greedy Sampling (WiGS), which formulates the selection of a balancing weight between feature-space diversity and output-space uncertainty as a reinforcement learning problem, allowing the sampling strategy to adapt over time. Experimental results on 18 benchmark datasets and a synthetic environment demonstrate that WiGS achieves higher accuracy and labeling efficiency than iGS and other baselines, showing particular strength in handling datasets with irregular data density where traditional methods may overlook informative samples.
本文针对回归任务中主动学习效率提升的需求，提出了对改进贪婪采样（iGS）静态规则的一种动态替代方法。作者引入了加权改进贪婪采样（WiGS），通过强化学习框架将特征空间多样性与输出空间不确定性之间的平衡权重选择问题公式化，从而使采样策略能够自适应调整。在18个基准数据集和合成环境上的实验结果表明，WiGS在准确性和标注效率上均优于iGS及其他基线方法，尤其在处理数据密度不规则的领域时表现突出，能够有效避免传统方法忽略密集区域高误差样本的问题。
Scalable Multi-Task Learning through Spiking Neural Networks with Adaptive Task-Switching Policy for Intelligent Autonomous Agents
Authors: Rachmad Vidya Wicaksana Putra, Avaneesh Devkota, Muhammad Shafique
First: 2025-04-18T08:12:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T04:56:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 63rd ACM/IEEE Design Automation Conference (DAC), July 26-29, 2026 in Long Beach, CA, USA Codes: https://github.com/rachmadvwp/SwitchMT
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Training resource-constrained autonomous agents on multiple tasks simultaneously is crucial for adapting to diverse real-world environments. Recent works employ reinforcement learning (RL) approach, but they still suffer from sub-optimal multi-task performance due to task interference. State-of-the-art works employ Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) to improve RL-based multi-task learning and enable low-power/energy operations through network enhancements and spike-driven data stream processing. However, they rely on fixed task-switching intervals during its training, thus limiting its performance and scalability. To address this, we propose SwitchMT, a novel methodology that employs adaptive task-switching for effective, scalable, and simultaneous multi-task learning. SwitchMT employs the following key ideas: (1) leveraging a Deep Spiking Q-Network with active dendrites and dueling structure, that utilizes task-specific context signals to create specialized sub-networks; and (2) devising an adaptive task-switching policy that leverages both rewards and internal dynamics of the network parameters. Experimental results demonstrate that SwitchMT achieves competitive scores in multiple Atari games (i.e., Pong: -8.8, Breakout: 5.6, and Enduro: 355.2) and longer game episodes as compared to the state-of-the-art. These results also highlight the effectiveness of SwitchMT methodology in addressing task interference without increasing the network complexity, enabling intelligent autonomous agents with scalable multi-task learning capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向智能自主代理的可扩展多任务学习：基于脉冲神经网络与自适应任务切换策略
在资源受限条件下对自主代理进行多任务同步训练，是适应多样化现实环境的关键。现有研究多采用强化学习方法，但仍受任务干扰影响导致性能欠佳。前沿工作通过脉冲神经网络改进基于强化学习的多任务学习，借助网络增强与脉冲驱动数据流处理实现低功耗运行。然而，这些方法依赖固定任务切换间隔，限制了性能与可扩展性。为此，我们提出SwitchMT——一种采用自适应任务切换的新方法，实现高效、可扩展的同步多任务学习。其核心创新包括：（1）构建具有主动树突与对决结构的深度脉冲Q网络，利用任务特定上下文信号创建专用子网络；（2）设计融合奖励信号与网络参数内部动态的自适应任务切换策略。实验表明，SwitchMT在多项Atari游戏（Pong: -8.8, Breakout: 5.6, Enduro: 355.2）中取得优于现有方法的得分与更长游戏回合。这些结果证实该方法能在不增加网络复杂度的前提下有效缓解任务干扰，为智能自主代理提供可扩展的多任务学习能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of task interference in multi-task reinforcement learning for resource-constrained autonomous agents, which limits performance and scalability. It proposes SwitchMT, a method that combines a Deep Spiking Q-Network with task-specific context signals and an adaptive task-switching policy based on rewards and network dynamics to reduce interference. Experimental results on Atari games show competitive scores, such as -8.8 in Pong and 355.2 in Enduro, and longer episode durations, demonstrating effective scalable learning without added network complexity.
本文针对资源受限的自主智能体在多任务强化学习中因任务干扰导致的性能与可扩展性限制问题，提出了一种名为SwitchMT的新方法。该方法采用具有任务特定上下文信号的深度脉冲Q网络，并结合基于奖励和网络内部动态的自适应任务切换策略，以减少干扰。在Atari游戏上的实验结果表明，该方法取得了有竞争力的分数，如在Pong中为-8.8，在Enduro中为355.2，并实现了更长的游戏回合，证明了其在未增加网络复杂性的情况下实现了有效的可扩展多任务学习。
Graph-GRPO: Training Graph Flow Models with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Baoheng Zhu, Deyu Bo, Delvin Ce Zhang, Xiao Wang
First: 2026-03-11T04:20:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T04:20:45+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph generation is a fundamental task with broad applications, such as drug discovery. Recently, discrete flow matching-based graph generation, \aka, graph flow model (GFM), has emerged due to its superior performance and flexible sampling. However, effectively aligning GFMs with complex human preferences or task-specific objectives remains a significant challenge. In this paper, we propose Graph-GRPO, an online reinforcement learning (RL) framework for training GFMs under verifiable rewards. Our method makes two key contributions: (1) We derive an analytical expression for the transition probability of GFMs, replacing the Monte Carlo sampling and enabling fully differentiable rollouts for RL training; (2) We propose a refinement strategy that randomly perturbs specific nodes and edges in a graph, and regenerates them, allowing for localized exploration and self-improvement of generation quality. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of Graph-GRPO. With only 50 denoising steps, our method achieves 95.0\% and 97.5\% Valid-Unique-Novelty scores on the planar and tree datasets, respectively. Moreover, Graph-GRPO achieves state-of-the-art performance on the molecular optimization tasks, outperforming graph-based and fragment-based RL methods as well as classic genetic algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Graph-GRPO：基于强化学习的图流模型训练方法
图生成是药物发现等领域的基础任务。近期，基于离散流匹配的图流模型因其优越性能和灵活采样特性而兴起，但如何使其有效契合复杂的人类偏好或任务目标仍是重大挑战。本文提出Graph-GRPO——一种在可验证奖励下训练图流模型的在线强化学习框架，其核心贡献包括：（1）推导出图流模型转移概率的解析表达式，替代蒙特卡洛采样，实现完全可微分的强化学习训练流程；（2）提出通过随机扰动图中特定节点与边并重新生成的优化策略，实现局部探索与生成质量的自我提升。在合成与真实数据集上的实验表明，仅需50步去噪过程，本方法在平面图和树图数据集上分别达到95.0%和97.5%的有效-唯一-新颖性评分，并在分子优化任务中超越基于图/片段的强化学习方法及经典遗传算法，取得最先进性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning graph flow models (GFMs) with complex human preferences or task-specific objectives in graph generation, which is crucial for applications like drug discovery. The proposed method, Graph-GRPO, introduces an online reinforcement learning framework with two key innovations: an analytical expression for GFM transition probabilities to enable fully differentiable rollouts, and a refinement strategy that perturbs and regenerates specific nodes and edges for localized exploration. Experimental results show that with only 50 denoising steps, the method achieves 95.0% and 97.5% Valid-Unique-Novelty scores on planar and tree datasets, respectively, and outperforms existing methods in molecular optimization tasks.

Latent Poincaré Shaping for Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hanchen Xia, Baoyou Chen, Zelin Zang, Yutang Ge, Guojiang Zhao, Siyu Zhu
First: 2026-02-10T03:35:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T03:30:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose LaPha, a method for training AlphaZero-like LLM agents in a Poincaré latent space. Under LaPha, the search process can be visualized as a tree rooted at the prompt and growing outward from the origin toward the boundary of the Poincaré ball, where negative curvature provides exponentially increasing capacity with radius. Using hyperbolic geodesic distance to rule-verified correctness, we define a node potential and assign dense process rewards by potential differences. We further attach a lightweight value head on the same shared latent space, enabling self-guided test-time scaling with almost no additional overhead. On MATH-500, LaPha improves Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B from 66.0% to 88.2%. With value-head-guided search, LaPha-1.5B reaches 56.7% accuracy on AIME'24, and LaPha-7B further achieves 60.0% on AIME'24 and 53.3% on AIME'25.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向智能体强化学习的潜在庞加莱塑形
我们提出LaPha方法，用于在庞加莱潜在空间中训练类AlphaZero的大语言模型智能体。该方法将搜索过程可视化为以提示为根、从原点向庞加莱球边界生长的树结构，其负曲率特性使模型容量随半径呈指数增长。通过双曲测地线距离与规则验证正确性的结合，我们定义了节点势能函数，并依据势能差分配密集过程奖励。我们在共享潜在空间上附加轻量级价值头，实现几乎零额外开销的自引导测试时扩展。在MATH-500基准测试中，LaPha将Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B的准确率从66.0%提升至88.2%。通过价值头引导搜索，LaPha-1.5B在AIME'24上达到56.7%准确率，LaPha-7B更在AIME'24和AIME'25上分别取得60.0%和53.3%的准确率。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LaPha, a method motivated by the need to enhance the reasoning capabilities of AlphaZero-like LLM agents by training them within a Poincaré latent space, which leverages hyperbolic geometry to provide exponentially increasing representational capacity. The method visualizes the search process as a tree growing from the origin toward the boundary of a Poincaré ball, using hyperbolic geodesic distance to measure correctness and define node potentials, thereby assigning dense process rewards based on potential differences; it also incorporates a lightweight value head on the shared latent space for efficient self-guided scaling during testing. Experimental results show significant improvements: on MATH-500, LaPha boosts Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B from 66.0% to 88.2% accuracy, and with value-head-guided search, LaPha-1.5B achieves 56.7% on AIME'24, while LaPha-7B reaches 60.0% on AIME'24 and 53.3% on AIME'25.

Utility Function is All You Need: LLM-based Congestion Control
Authors: Neta Rozen-Schiff, Liron Schiff, Stefan Schmid
First: 2026-03-11T03:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T03:11:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Congestion is a critical and challenging problem in communication networks. Congestion control protocols allow network applications to tune their sending rate in a way that optimizes their performance and the network utilization. In the common distributed setting, the applications cannot collaborate with each other directly but instead obtain similar estimations about the state of the network using latency and loss measurements. These measurements can be fed into analytical functions, referred to by utility functions, whose gradients help each and all distributed senders to converge to a desired state. The above process becomes extremely complicated when each application has different optimization goals and requirements. Crafting these utilization functions has been a research subject for over a decade, with small incremental changes requiring rigorous mathematical analysis as well as real-world experiments. In this work, we present GenCC, a framework leveraging the code generation capabilities of large language models (LLMs) coupled with realistic network testbed, to design congestion control utility functions. Using GenCC, we analyze the impact of different guidance strategies on the performance of the generated protocols, considering application-specific requirements and network capacity. Our results show that LLMs, guided by either a generative code evolution strategy or mathematical chain-of-thought (CoT), can obtain close to optimal results, improving state-of-the-art congestion control protocols by 37%-142%, depending on the scenario.
中文标题/摘要
标题：效用函数即一切：基于大语言模型的拥塞控制
拥塞是通信网络中一个关键且具有挑战性的问题。拥塞控制协议使网络应用能够调整其发送速率，以优化其性能和网络利用率。在常见的分布式环境中，应用之间无法直接协作，而是通过延迟和丢包测量获得对网络状态的相似估计。这些测量值可输入到被称为效用函数的解析函数中，其梯度帮助每个分布式发送方共同收敛到期望状态。当每个应用具有不同的优化目标和需求时，上述过程变得极为复杂。设计这些效用函数已成为十多年的研究课题，微小的增量改进都需要严格的数学分析和实际实验。本研究提出GenCC框架，该框架利用大语言模型的代码生成能力结合真实网络测试平台，设计拥塞控制效用函数。通过GenCC，我们分析了不同引导策略对生成协议性能的影响，并考虑了应用特定需求和网络容量。结果表明，在生成式代码进化策略或数学思维链引导下，大语言模型可获得接近最优的结果，将最先进的拥塞控制协议性能提升37%-142%，具体取决于场景。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the complexity of designing congestion control utility functions for diverse application requirements, this paper introduces GenCC, a framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to generate these functions through code generation, guided by strategies like generative code evolution or mathematical chain-of-thought. The method integrates LLMs with a realistic network testbed to tailor protocols to specific needs and network capacities. Experimental results demonstrate that LLM-generated protocols achieve near-optimal performance, improving state-of-the-art congestion control by 37% to 142% across various scenarios.
针对不同应用需求下拥塞控制效用函数设计复杂的问题，本文提出了GenCC框架，利用大型语言模型（LLMs）的代码生成能力，通过生成式代码进化或数学思维链等策略指导，生成这些函数。该方法将LLMs与真实网络测试平台结合，以根据特定需求和网络容量定制协议。实验结果表明，LLM生成的协议实现了接近最优的性能，在不同场景下将最先进的拥塞控制协议提升了37%至142%。
PlayWorld: Learning Robot World Models from Autonomous Play
Authors: Tenny Yin, Zhiting Mei, Zhonghe Zheng, Miyu Yamane, David Wang, Jade Sceats, Samuel M. Bateman, Lihan Zha, Apurva Badithela, Ola Shorinwa, Anirudha Majumdar
First: 2026-03-09T23:58:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T01:39:15+00:00
Comments: https://robot-playworld.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Action-conditioned video models offer a promising path to building general-purpose robot simulators that can improve directly from data. Yet, despite training on large-scale robot datasets, current state-of-the-art video models still struggle to predict physically consistent robot-object interactions that are crucial in robotic manipulation. To close this gap, we present PlayWorld, a simple, scalable, and fully autonomous pipeline for training high-fidelity video world simulators from interaction experience. In contrast to prior approaches that rely on success-biased human demonstrations, PlayWorld is the first system capable of learning entirely from unsupervised robot self-play, enabling naturally scalable data collection while capturing complex, long-tailed physical interactions essential for modeling realistic object dynamics. Experiments across diverse manipulation tasks show that PlayWorld generates high-quality, physically consistent predictions for contact-rich interactions that are not captured by world models trained on human-collected data. We further demonstrate the versatility of PlayWorld in enabling fine-grained failure prediction and policy evaluation, with up to 40% improvements over human-collected data. Finally, we demonstrate how PlayWorld enables reinforcement learning in the world model, improving policy performance by 65% in success rates when deployed in the real world.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PlayWorld：通过自主游戏学习机器人世界模型
动作条件视频模型为构建能直接从数据中改进的通用机器人模拟器提供了可行路径。然而，尽管基于大规模机器人数据集进行训练，当前最先进的视频模型仍难以预测对机器人操作至关重要的物理一致性机器人-物体交互。为弥补这一差距，我们提出PlayWorld——一个简单、可扩展且完全自主的流程，用于从交互经验中训练高保真视频世界模拟器。与以往依赖成功偏向性人类演示的方法不同，PlayWorld是首个能够完全从无监督机器人自主游戏中学习的系统，在捕捉复杂长尾物理交互（对建模真实物体动力学至关重要）的同时，实现了自然可扩展的数据收集。在多样化操作任务上的实验表明，PlayWorld能对密集接触交互生成高质量、物理一致的预测，这是基于人类收集数据训练的世界模型所无法捕捉的。我们进一步展示了PlayWorld在实现细粒度故障预测与策略评估方面的通用性，相比人类收集数据最高可提升40%的性能。最后，我们演示了PlayWorld如何支持在世界模型中进行强化学习，在真实世界部署时将策略成功率提升了65%。
