The motivation for PlayWorld is to address the limitations of current action-conditioned video models in predicting physically consistent robot-object interactions, which are crucial for robotic manipulation, despite training on large-scale datasets. The method introduces a simple, scalable, and fully autonomous pipeline that learns world models from unsupervised robot self-play, enabling data collection without reliance on success-biased human demonstrations and capturing complex, long-tailed physical interactions. Experimental results show that PlayWorld generates high-quality, physically consistent predictions for contact-rich interactions, outperforms models trained on human-collected data by up to 40% in failure prediction and policy evaluation, and improves real-world policy performance by 65% in success rates through reinforcement learning in the world model.
PlayWorld的动机是解决当前基于动作的视频模型在预测物理一致的机器人-物体交互方面的局限性，尽管这些模型在大规模数据集上训练，但对机器人操作至关重要。该方法引入了一个简单、可扩展且完全自主的流程，通过无监督的机器人自我游戏学习世界模型，避免了依赖偏向成功的人类演示，并能捕捉复杂的长尾物理交互。实验结果表明，PlayWorld能生成高质量的、物理一致的接触丰富交互预测，在失败预测和策略评估上比基于人类收集数据的模型提升高达40%，并通过在世界模型中进行强化学习，将真实世界中的策略成功率提高了65%。
PvP: Data-Efficient Humanoid Robot Learning with Proprioceptive-Privileged Contrastive Representations
Authors: Mingqi Yuan, Tao Yu, Haolin Song, Bo Li, Xin Jin, Hua Chen, Wenjun Zeng
Venue: CVPR
First: 2025-12-15T08:50:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T01:31:17+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Achieving efficient and robust whole-body control (WBC) is essential for enabling humanoid robots to perform complex tasks in dynamic environments. Despite the success of reinforcement learning (RL) in this domain, its sample inefficiency remains a significant challenge due to the intricate dynamics and partial observability of humanoid robots. To address this limitation, we propose PvP, a Proprioceptive-Privileged contrastive learning framework that leverages the intrinsic complementarity between proprioceptive and privileged states. PvP learns compact and task-relevant latent representations without requiring hand-crafted data augmentations, enabling faster and more stable policy learning. To support systematic evaluation, we develop SRL4Humanoid, the first unified and modular framework that provides high-quality implementations of representative state representation learning (SRL) methods for humanoid robot learning. Extensive experiments on the LimX Oli robot across velocity tracking and motion imitation tasks demonstrate that PvP significantly improves sample efficiency and final performance compared to baseline SRL methods. Our study further provides practical insights into integrating SRL with RL for humanoid WBC, offering valuable guidance for data-efficient humanoid robot learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PvP：基于本体感知-特权对比表征的数据高效人形机器人学习
实现高效稳健的全身控制对于人形机器人在动态环境中执行复杂任务至关重要。尽管强化学习在该领域已取得成果，但由于人形机器人复杂的动力学特性和部分可观测性，其样本效率低仍是重大挑战。为应对此局限，本文提出PvP——一种利用本体感知状态与特权状态内在互补性的对比学习框架。PvP无需人工设计数据增强即可学习紧凑且任务相关的潜在表征，从而实现更快速稳定的策略学习。为支持系统化评估，我们开发了首个面向人形机器人学习的统一模块化框架SRL4Humanoid，其高质量实现了代表性状态表征学习方法。在LimX Oli机器人上进行的速度跟踪与运动模仿实验表明，相较于基线SRL方法，PvP显著提升了样本效率与最终性能。本研究进一步为SRL与RL在人形机器人全身控制中的融合提供了实践洞见，为数据高效的人形机器人学习提供了重要指导。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the sample inefficiency of reinforcement learning for humanoid whole-body control by proposing PvP, a framework that learns compact latent representations through contrastive learning between proprioceptive and privileged states, eliminating the need for manual data augmentation. The method is evaluated using a newly developed modular framework called SRL4Humanoid, and experiments on the LimX Oli robot show that PvP achieves superior sample efficiency and final performance in velocity tracking and motion imitation tasks compared to baseline state representation learning methods.
本文针对人形机器人全身控制中强化学习样本效率低的问题，提出了PvP框架，该框架通过本体感知与特权状态间的对比学习来获取紧凑的潜在表征，无需人工数据增强。该方法通过新开发的模块化框架SRL4Humanoid进行评估，在LimX Oli机器人上的实验表明，在速度跟踪和运动模仿任务中，PvP相比基线状态表征学习方法显著提高了样本效率和最终性能。
Quantum entanglement provides a competitive advantage in adversarial games
Authors: Peiyong Wang, Kieran Hymas, James Quach
First: 2026-03-11T00:15:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T00:15:56+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Whether uniquely quantum resources confer advantages in fully classical, competitive environments remains an open question. Competitive zero-sum reinforcement learning is particularly challenging, as success requires modelling dynamic interactions between opposing agents rather than static state-action mappings. Here, we conduct a controlled study isolating the role of quantum entanglement in a quantum-classical hybrid agent trained on Pong, a competitive Markov game. An 8-qubit parameterised quantum circuit serves as a feature extractor within a proximal policy optimisation framework, allowing direct comparison between separable circuits and architectures incorporating fixed (CZ) or trainable (IsingZZ) entangling gates. Entangled circuits consistently outperform separable counterparts with comparable parameter counts and, in low-capacity regimes, match or exceed classical multilayer perceptron baselines. Representation similarity analysis further shows that entangled circuits learn structurally distinct features, consistent with improved modelling of interacting state variables. These findings establish entanglement as a function resource for representation learning in competitive reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量子纠缠在对抗性游戏中提供竞争优势
量子资源能否在完全经典的竞争环境中提供优势仍是一个开放性问题。竞争性零和强化学习尤其具有挑战性，因为成功需要建模对抗智能体之间的动态交互，而非静态的状态-动作映射。本研究通过控制实验，在训练于对抗性马尔可夫游戏《乒乓》的量子-经典混合智能体中，分离出量子纠缠的作用。一个8量子比特参数化量子电路作为近端策略优化框架中的特征提取器，使可分离电路与采用固定纠缠门（CZ）或可训练纠缠门（IsingZZ）的架构能够直接比较。纠缠电路在参数量相近时持续优于可分离电路，并在低容量场景中达到或超越经典多层感知机基线。表征相似性分析进一步表明，纠缠电路学习到结构独特的特征，这与交互状态变量建模能力的提升相一致。这些发现确立了纠缠作为竞争性强化学习中表征学习的功能性资源。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether quantum entanglement offers a competitive edge in classical adversarial environments, specifically in zero-sum reinforcement learning games like Pong. The method employs a hybrid quantum-classical agent where an 8-qubit parameterized quantum circuit acts as a feature extractor within a proximal policy optimization framework, comparing separable circuits against those with fixed or trainable entangling gates. Experimental results show that entangled circuits consistently outperform separable ones with similar parameter counts and, in low-capacity settings, match or surpass classical multilayer perceptron baselines, with representation analysis indicating they learn structurally distinct features for better modeling of agent interactions.
本文研究了量子纠缠是否能在经典对抗性环境（特别是如Pong这样的零和强化学习游戏）中提供竞争优势。方法采用一种混合量子-经典智能体，其中8量子比特参数化量子电路在近端策略优化框架中充当特征提取器，并比较了可分离电路与具有固定或可训练纠缠门的电路架构。实验结果表明，具有可比参数量的纠缠电路持续优于可分离电路，且在低容量状态下达到或超越了经典多层感知机基线，表征相似性分析进一步表明纠缠电路学习了结构独特的特征，从而能更好地建模智能体间的交互作用。
From Prior to Pro: Efficient Skill Mastery via Distribution Contractive RL Finetuning
Authors: Zhanyi Sun, Shuran Song
First: 2026-03-10T22:49:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T22:49:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We introduce Distribution Contractive Reinforcement Learning (DICE-RL), a framework that uses reinforcement learning (RL) as a "distribution contraction" operator to refine pretrained generative robot policies. DICE-RL turns a pretrained behavior prior into a high-performing "pro" policy by amplifying high-success behaviors from online feedback. We pretrain a diffusion- or flow-based policy for broad behavioral coverage, then finetune it with a stable, sample-efficient residual off-policy RL framework that combines selective behavior regularization with value-guided action selection. Extensive experiments and analyses show that DICE-RL reliably improves performance with strong stability and sample efficiency. It enables mastery of complex long-horizon manipulation skills directly from high-dimensional pixel inputs, both in simulation and on a real robot. Project website: https://zhanyisun.github.io/dice.rl.2026/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从先验到专业：基于分布收缩强化学习微调的高效技能掌握方法
我们提出了分布收缩强化学习（DICE-RL）框架，该框架将强化学习作为“分布收缩”算子，用于优化预训练的生成式机器人策略。DICE-RL通过在线反馈放大高成功率行为，将预训练的行为先验转化为高性能的“专业”策略。我们首先预训练具有广泛行为覆盖的扩散或流模型策略，随后采用结合选择性行为正则化与价值引导动作选择的稳定、样本高效的残差离策略强化学习框架进行微调。大量实验与分析表明，DICE-RL能以强大的稳定性和样本效率持续提升性能，支持在仿真和真实机器人上直接从高维像素输入掌握复杂长时程操作技能。项目网站：https://zhanyisun.github.io/dice.rl.2026/。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Distribution Contractive Reinforcement Learning (DICE-RL), motivated by the need to efficiently refine pretrained generative robot policies into high-performance skills. The method uses RL as a distribution contraction operator, starting with a diffusion- or flow-based policy for broad coverage and finetuning it via a stable, sample-efficient residual off-policy framework that combines selective behavior regularization with value-guided action selection. Experimental results demonstrate that DICE-RL reliably improves performance with strong stability and sample efficiency, enabling mastery of complex long-horizon manipulation tasks directly from high-dimensional pixel inputs in both simulation and real-robot settings.
本文提出了分布收缩强化学习（DICE-RL），其动机在于需要将预训练的生成式机器人策略高效精炼为高性能技能。该方法将强化学习作为分布收缩算子，首先使用扩散或流模型策略实现广泛行为覆盖，然后通过一个稳定、样本高效的残差离策略框架进行微调，该框架结合了选择性行为正则化和价值引导的动作选择。实验结果表明，DICE-RL以强大的稳定性和样本效率可靠地提升了性能，能够在仿真和真实机器人中直接从高维像素输入掌握复杂的长时程操作技能。
Synthesizing Interpretable Control Policies through Large Language Model Guided Search
Authors: Carlo Bosio, Mark W. Mueller
Venue: Published at ACC 2025
First: 2024-10-07T18:12:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T22:31:58+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 7 figures, conference paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The combination of Large Language Models (LLMs), systematic evaluation, and evolutionary algorithms has enabled breakthroughs in combinatorial optimization and scientific discovery. We propose to extend this powerful combination to the control of dynamical systems, generating interpretable control policies capable of complex behaviors. With our novel method, we represent control policies as programs in standard languages like Python. We evaluate candidate controllers in simulation and evolve them using a pre-trained LLM. Unlike conventional learning-based control techniques, which rely on black-box neural networks to encode control policies, our approach enhances transparency and interpretability. We still take advantage of the power of large AI models, but only at the policy design phase, ensuring that all system components remain interpretable and easily verifiable at runtime. Additionally, the use of standard programming languages makes it straightforward for humans to finetune or adapt the controllers based on their expertise and intuition. We illustrate our method through its application to the synthesis of an interpretable control policy for the \textit{pendulum swing-up} and the \textit{ball in cup} tasks. We make the code available at https://github.com/muellerlab/synthesizing_interpretable_control_policies.git.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过大语言模型引导搜索合成可解释控制策略
大语言模型（LLMs）、系统化评估与进化算法的结合，已在组合优化和科学发现领域实现突破。本研究将这一强大组合拓展至动态系统控制领域，生成具备复杂行为能力的可解释控制策略。我们提出一种新方法，将控制策略表示为Python等标准语言的程序代码。通过在仿真环境中评估候选控制器，并利用预训练大语言模型进行演化，与传统依赖黑盒神经网络编码控制策略的学习型控制技术不同，本方法显著提升了策略的透明度和可解释性。我们仍借助大型AI模型的能力，但仅将其用于策略设计阶段，确保所有系统组件在运行时保持可解释且易于验证。此外，采用标准编程语言使人类能基于专业知识和直觉直接微调或适配控制器。我们通过合成“钟摆起摆”和“球入杯”任务的可解释控制策略，展示了该方法的应用效果。代码已开源：https://github.com/muellerlab/synthesizing_interpretable_control_policies.git。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for transparent and interpretable control policies in dynamical systems, this paper introduces a method that synthesizes controllers as programs in standard languages like Python, using a pre-trained Large Language Model (LLM) to guide an evolutionary search process. The approach leverages LLMs during policy design to generate and refine candidate controllers evaluated in simulation, contrasting with black-box neural network methods to enhance verifiability and human understanding. Experimental results on benchmark tasks, including pendulum swing-up and ball in cup, demonstrate that the method produces effective interpretable policies, with the use of standard languages facilitating human finetuning and adaptation based on expertise.
本文旨在为动态系统设计透明且可解释的控制策略，提出了一种将控制器合成为Python等标准语言程序的方法，利用预训练大语言模型引导进化搜索过程。该方法在大语言模型指导下，通过仿真评估生成和优化候选控制器，避免了传统黑盒神经网络方法的不可解释性，增强了运行时组件的可验证性和可理解性。在摆锤起摆和球入杯等基准任务上的实验结果表明，该方法能生成有效的可解释策略，且标准语言的使用便于人类基于专业知识和直觉进行微调与适配。
SiMPO: Measure Matching for Online Diffusion Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Haitong Ma, Chenxiao Gao, Tianyi Chen, Na Li, Bo Dai
First: 2026-03-10T22:01:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T22:01:13+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A commonly used family of RL algorithms for diffusion policies conducts softmax reweighting over the behavior policy, which usually induces an over-greedy policy and fails to leverage feedback from negative samples. In this work, we introduce Signed Measure Policy Optimization (SiMPO), a simple and unified framework that generalizes reweighting scheme in diffusion RL with general monotonic functions. SiMPO revisits diffusion RL via a two-stage measure matching lens. First, we construct a virtual target policy by $f$-divergence regularized policy optimization, where we can relax the non-negativity constraint to allow for a signed target measure. Second, we use this signed measure to guide diffusion or flow models through reweighted matching. This formulation offers two key advantages: a) it generalizes to arbitrary monotonically increasing weighting functions; and b) it provides a principled justification and practical guidance for negative reweighting. Furthermore, we provide geometric interpretations to illustrate how negative reweighting actively repels the policy from suboptimal actions. Extensive empirical evaluations demonstrate that SiMPO achieves superior performance by leveraging these flexible weighting schemes, and we provide practical guidelines for selecting reweighting methods tailored to the reward landscape.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SiMPO：在线扩散强化学习的测度匹配方法
扩散策略中常用的强化学习算法族通过对行为策略进行softmax重加权，这通常会导致策略过度贪婪且无法利用负样本反馈。本文提出符号测度策略优化（SiMPO），这是一个通过单调函数推广扩散强化学习中重加权方案的统一框架。SiMPO通过两阶段测度匹配视角重新审视扩散强化学习：首先，通过$f$-散度正则化策略优化构建虚拟目标策略，其中放宽非负约束以允许符号测度；其次，利用该符号测度通过重加权匹配指导扩散或流模型。该框架具有两大优势：a)可推广至任意单调递增加权函数；b)为负向重加权提供理论依据与实践指导。此外，本文通过几何解释阐明负向重加权如何主动使策略远离次优动作。大量实验表明，SiMPO通过灵活加权方案实现卓越性能，并为针对奖励场景选择重加权方法提供实用指南。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Signed Measure Policy Optimization (SiMPO), motivated by limitations in existing diffusion reinforcement learning methods that use softmax reweighting, which often leads to over-greedy policies and fails to utilize negative feedback. The method generalizes reweighting through a two-stage measure matching framework: first constructing a virtual target policy via f-divergence regularized optimization that allows a signed measure, then guiding diffusion or flow models with reweighted matching. Experimental results across evaluations show SiMPO achieves superior performance by enabling flexible weighting schemes, including negative reweighting to repel suboptimal actions, with practical guidelines for adapting to reward landscapes.

Long Chain-of-Thought Compression via Fine-Grained Group Policy Optimization
Authors: Xinchen Han, Hossam Afifi, Michel Marot, Xilu Wang, Lu Yin
Venue: ICASSP
First: 2026-02-10T18:15:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T20:59:28+00:00
Comments: IEEE International Conference on Acoustics, Speech, and Signal Processing (ICASSP), 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) often generate unnecessarily verbose Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning that increases computational costs and latency without proportional performance gains. In this paper, we propose Fine-grained Group policy Optimization (FGO), a Reinforcement Learning (RL) algorithm that refines group responses by subdividing them and assigning appropriate weights based on length and entropy, thereby enabling effective CoT compression. Meanwhile, as an enhanced variant of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), FGO successfully addresses two major limitations of the GRPO: inefficient data utilization and entropy collapse. We evaluate FGO on multiple reasoning LLMs and benchmarks, including MATH500, AIME24, AMC23, and Minerva. Experimental results show that FGO achieves efficient CoT compression without degrading performance, and simultaneously resolves the key limitations of GRPO. Code: https://github.com/Mr-XcHan/FGO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于细粒度分组策略优化的长链思维压缩方法
大语言模型（LLMs）生成的链式思维（CoT）推理常存在冗余冗长问题，导致计算成本与延迟增加却未带来相应性能提升。本文提出细粒度分组策略优化（FGO）算法，该强化学习方法通过细分组响应并依据长度与熵值分配权重，实现高效CoT压缩。作为分组相对策略优化（GRPO）的增强变体，FGO成功解决了GRPO的两大局限：数据利用效率低下与熵崩溃问题。我们在MATH500、AIME24、AMC23及Minerva等多个推理基准测试中验证FGO，实验表明该方法在保持性能的同时实现高效CoT压缩，并同步解决了GRPO的关键缺陷。代码：https://github.com/Mr-XcHan/FGO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of Large Language Models (LLMs) generating excessively verbose Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning, which increases computational costs without proportional performance benefits. To tackle this, the authors propose Fine-grained Group policy Optimization (FGO), a Reinforcement Learning algorithm that compresses CoT by subdividing group responses and weighting them based on length and entropy, while also overcoming inefficiencies and entropy collapse in prior methods like Group Relative Policy Optimization. Experiments on reasoning benchmarks such as MATH500, AIME24, AMC23, and Minerva demonstrate that FGO achieves effective CoT compression without performance degradation and successfully resolves key limitations of GRPO.
本文针对大语言模型生成冗长思维链推理导致计算成本增加而性能提升有限的问题，提出了一种细粒度组策略优化方法。该方法通过强化学习算法，将组响应细分为更小单元并根据长度和熵分配权重，从而实现有效的思维链压缩，同时解决了组相对策略优化中数据利用效率低和熵崩溃两大局限。在MATH500、AIME24、AMC23和Minerva等多个推理基准上的实验结果表明，该方法能在不降低性能的前提下高效压缩思维链，并成功克服了先前方法的不足。
An Updated Assessment of Reinforcement Learning for Macro Placement
Authors: Chung-Kuan Cheng, Andrew B. Kahng, Sayak Kundu, Yucheng Wang, Zhiang Wang
First: 2023-02-21T21:26:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T20:18:33+00:00
Comments: There are total sixteen pages and two pages for the appendix. It includes six figures and eleven tables. This paper has been accepted and published in IEEE Transactions on CAD
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We provide an improved assessment of Google Brain's deep reinforcement learning approach to macro placement and its updated Circuit Training (CT) implementation in GitHub. A stronger simulated annealing (SA) baseline leverages the "go-with-the-winners" metaheuristic and a multi-threading implementation. We develop and release new public benchmarks in sub-10nm technology: LEF/DEF for Google's 7nm TSMC Ariane protobuf and scaled variants, as well as testcases implemented in the open-source ASAP7 7nm research enablement. We evaluate from-scratch training and fine-tuning results for the latest "AlphaChip" release of Circuit Training, alongside multiple alternative macro placers. We also study the recently-published pre-training guidance in. A commercial place-and-route tool is used to provide "true reward" post-route power, performance and area metrics. All data, evaluation flows and related scripts are publicly available in the MacroPlacement GitHub repository. Our study affords insights into reproducibility and reporting in the research literature, and points out still-missing confirmations (e.g., of CT's scalability and pre-training methodology) that remain open questions for the research community.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习在宏单元布局中的更新评估
本文对Google Brain采用深度强化学习进行宏单元布局的方法及其在GitHub上更新的Circuit Training（CT）实现进行了改进评估。我们构建了更强大的模拟退火基准线，采用“胜者导向”元启发式算法和多线程实现。针对10纳米以下工艺，我们开发并发布了新的公开基准测试集：包括Google 7纳米TSMC Ariane protobuf的LEF/DEF文件及其缩放变体，以及基于开源ASAP7 7纳米研究平台实现的测试用例。我们评估了Circuit Training最新“AlphaChip”版本的从头训练与微调结果，并与多种替代宏单元布局工具进行对比。同时研究了近期发布的预训练指导方法。采用商用布局布线工具获取布线后“真实奖励”的功耗、性能与面积指标。所有数据、评估流程及相关脚本已在MacroPlacement GitHub仓库公开。本研究为学术文献的可复现性与报告规范提供了见解，并指出仍需研究界验证的开放问题（如CT的可扩展性及预训练方法论）。

This paper provides an updated evaluation of Google Brain's deep reinforcement learning (RL) approach for macro placement, specifically its Circuit Training (CT) implementation, motivated by the need for a stronger, reproducible assessment in advanced technology nodes. The method involves establishing a robust simulated annealing baseline using a "go-with-the-winners" metaheuristic, creating new public benchmarks in sub-10nm technologies (including TSMC 7nm and ASAP7), and evaluating CT's from-scratch training and fine-tuning against alternative placers, with a commercial tool used for post-route validation. Key experimental results show that the study offers insights into reproducibility and reporting, while highlighting open questions regarding CT's scalability and pre-training methodology, with all data and evaluation flows made publicly available.

Actor-Accelerated Policy Dual Averaging for Reinforcement Learning in Continuous Action Spaces
Authors: Ji Gao, Caleb Ju, Guanghui Lan, Zhaohui Tong
First: 2026-03-10T20:05:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T20:05:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy Dual Averaging (PDA) offers a principled Policy Mirror Descent (PMD) framework that more naturally admits value function approximation than standard PMD, enabling the use of approximate advantage (or Q-) functions while retaining strong convergence guarantees. However, applying PDA in continuous state and action spaces remains computationally challenging, since action selection involves solving an optimization sub-problem at each decision step. In this paper, we propose \textit{actor-accelerated PDA}, which uses a learned policy network to approximate the solution of the optimization sub-problems, yielding faster runtimes while maintaining convergence guarantees. We provide a theoretical analysis that quantifies how actor approximation error impacts the convergence of PDA under suitable assumptions. We then evaluate its performance on several benchmarks in robotics, control, and operations research problems. Actor-accelerated PDA achieves superior performance compared to popular on-policy baselines such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). Overall, our results bridge the gap between the theoretical advantages of PDA and its practical deployment in continuous-action problems with function approximation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续动作空间中强化学习的行动者加速策略对偶平均法
策略对偶平均（PDA）提供了一个原则性的策略镜像下降（PMD）框架，相比标准PMD能更自然地引入价值函数近似，允许使用近似优势（或Q）函数，同时保持强收敛保证。然而，在连续状态和动作空间中应用PDA仍存在计算挑战，因为动作选择需要在每个决策步骤求解优化子问题。本文提出\textit{行动者加速PDA}，通过学习的策略网络来近似优化子问题的解，在保持收敛保证的同时显著提升运行效率。我们提供了理论分析，量化了在适当假设下行动者近似误差对PDA收敛性的影响，并在机器人、控制与运筹学领域的多个基准问题上评估其性能。与近端策略优化（PPO）等主流同策略基线方法相比，行动者加速PDA展现出更优性能。总体而言，本研究弥合了PDA的理论优势与其在函数近似的连续动作问题中实际应用之间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the computational challenge of applying Policy Dual Averaging (PDA) in continuous action spaces, where solving an optimization sub-problem at each step is costly. The method introduces actor-accelerated PDA, which uses a learned policy network to approximate the solutions to these sub-problems, thereby accelerating runtime while preserving theoretical convergence guarantees, with analysis quantifying the impact of approximation error. Experimental results on robotics, control, and operations research benchmarks show that this approach outperforms on-policy baselines like Proximal Policy Optimization, bridging the gap between PDA's theoretical benefits and practical deployment.
本研究的动机是解决在连续动作空间中应用策略对偶平均（PDA）的计算挑战，因为每一步都需要求解优化子问题成本高昂。方法提出了演员加速的PDA，使用学习到的策略网络来近似这些子问题的解，从而在保持理论收敛保证的同时加速运行，并通过分析量化了近似误差的影响。在机器人学、控制和运筹学基准测试中的实验结果表明，该方法优于近端策略优化等主流同策略基线，弥合了PDA理论优势与实际在连续动作问题中部署的差距。
